// v25 counsel/pdf/student-info menu verified build
const CONFIG = {
  masterSheetName: '내신석차연명부',
  abbrSheetName: '축약어',
  upperSheetName: '학생별 누적표',
  tableHeaders: ['월', '학번', '이름', '내신', '국선택', '국점수', '국등급', '수선택', '수점수', '수등급', '영점수', '영등급', '탐1선택', '탐1점수', '탐1등급', '탐2선택', '탐2점수', '탐2등급', '3개합', '2개합'],
  visibleYellow: '#fff2cc',
  latestTextColors: ['#0000ff', '#7030a0', '#00b050', '#000000']
};

const USED_MOCK_MONTHS = [3, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10, 11];

function onOpen() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  ui.createMenu('데이터 설정')
    .addItem('모의고사 붙여넣기 확인', 'showUploadDialog')
    .addItem('내신석차연명부 업로드', 'showMasterUploadDialog')
    .addSubMenu(
      ui.createMenu('학생 정보 업로드')
        .addItem('설문조사 결과 붙여넣기 확인', 'showInfoUploadDialog')
        .addItem('학생 사진 업로드', 'showPhotoUploadDialog')
    )
    .addItem('대학 정보 업로드', 'showCollegePdfUploadDialog')
    .addItem('조회 캐시 초기화', 'clearRuntimeCache')
    .addItem('월별 데이터 삭제', 'showDeleteMonthDialog')
    .addToUi();

  // 신규 기능은 실패하더라도 기존 메뉴와 기능에 영향을 주지 않도록 안전하게 실행함.
  safeEnsureSubjectAnalysisSheetOnOpen_();
}

function clearRuntimeCache() {
  bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().alert('조회 캐시를 초기화했습니다.');
}



function showStudentInfoUploadDialog() {
  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('StudentInfoUploadDialog')
    .setWidth(420)
    .setHeight(260);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, '학생 정보 업로드');
}

function showUploadDialog() {
  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('UploadDialog')
    .setWidth(420)
    .setHeight(360);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, '모의고사 붙여넣기 확인');
}

function showDeleteMonthDialog() {
  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('DeleteMonthDialog')
    .setWidth(360)
    .setHeight(220);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, '월별 데이터 삭제');
}

function checkMonthExists(month) {
  month = normalizeUsedMockMonth_(month);
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  return !!ss.getSheetByName(getTableSheetName_(month));
}

function isUsedMockMonth_(month) {
  return USED_MOCK_MONTHS.indexOf(Number(month)) !== -1;
}

function normalizeUsedMockMonth_(month) {
  const value = normalizeMonth_(month);
  if (!isUsedMockMonth_(value)) {
    throw new Error('모의고사는 3월, 5월, 6월, 7월, 9월, 10월, 11월만 처리할 수 있습니다.');
  }
  return value;
}

function monthArtifactsExist_(ss, month) {
  if (ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month))) return true;
  if (ss.getSheetByName(getTableSheetName_(month))) return true;
  for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
    if (ss.getSheetByName(getClassSheetName_(month, classNum))) return true;
  }

  const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  if (upper && upper.getLastRow() >= 2) {
    const values = upper.getRange(2, 1, upper.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getValues();
    if (values.some(row => Number(row[0]) === month)) return true;
  }

  return false;
}

function validatePastedMockDataSheet_(rawValues, month) {
  if (!rawValues || rawValues.length < 3) {
    throw new Error(getDataSheetName_(month) + ' 탭에서 데이터 행을 찾지 못했습니다. 엑셀 원본의 1~2행 헤더를 포함하여 A1부터 붙여넣어야 합니다.');
  }

  const width = rawValues.reduce((max, row) => Math.max(max, row.length), 0);
  if (width < 38) {
    throw new Error(getDataSheetName_(month) + ' 탭의 열 수가 부족합니다. A열부터 AL열까지 원본 전체를 그대로 붙여넣어야 합니다.');
  }

  let validCount = 0;
  for (let i = 2; i < rawValues.length; i++) {
    const row = rawValues[i];
    if (isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;

    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[4]);

    if (year && classNum && number && name) validCount++;
  }

  if (validCount === 0) {
    throw new Error(getDataSheetName_(month) + ' 탭에서 학생 데이터를 찾지 못했습니다. B열 학년, C열 반, D열 번호, E열 이름 구조인지 확인해 주세요.');
  }
}

function processPastedMockData(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const month = normalizeUsedMockMonth_(payload && payload.month);
    ensureBaseSheets_(ss);

    if (checkMonthExists(month) && !(payload && payload.overwrite)) {
      return { status: 'MONTH_EXISTS' };
    }

    const rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
    if (!rawSheet) {
      throw new Error(getDataSheetName_(month) + ' 탭이 없습니다. 해당 이름의 탭을 만든 뒤 엑셀 원본을 A1부터 붙여넣어 주세요.');
    }

    const rawValues = rectangularize_(rawSheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues());
    validatePastedMockDataSheet_(rawValues, month);

    const duplicateInfo = findDuplicateStudents_(rawValues, ss);
    if (duplicateInfo.length > 0) {
      return { status: 'DUPLICATES', duplicates: duplicateInfo };
    }

    const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
    const abbrMap = buildAbbrMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName));
    const tableRows = buildMonthlyTableRows_(rawValues, month, studentMap, abbrMap);

    deleteDerivedMonthArtifacts_(ss, month);

    const tableSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getTableSheetName_(month));
    writeTableSheet_(tableSheet, tableRows);
    sortMonthlyTable_(tableSheet);
    formatScoreLikeSheet_(tableSheet);

    for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
      const classSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getClassSheetName_(month, classNum));
      writeClassSheet_(classSheet, month, classNum);
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      formatScoreLikeSheet_(classSheet);
    }

    updateUpperSheet_(ss, month, tableRows);
    ss.setActiveSheet(tableSheet);

    updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, month);
    finalizeBaseSheets_(ss);
    ss.setActiveSheet(tableSheet);

    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();

    return {
      status: 'SUCCESS',
      month: month,
      count: tableRows.length
    };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function processUpload(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const month = normalizeMonth_(payload.month);
    ensureBaseSheets_(ss);

    if (checkMonthExists(month) && !payload.overwrite) {
      return { status: 'MONTH_EXISTS' };
    }

    const rawValues = readUploadFile_(payload);
    const normalizedRaw = rectangularize_(rawValues);
    if (normalizedRaw.length < 3) {
      throw new Error('업로드 파일에서 데이터 행을 찾지 못했습니다. 1~2행은 헤더, 3행부터 데이터여야 합니다.');
    }

    const duplicateInfo = findDuplicateStudents_(normalizedRaw, ss);
    if (duplicateInfo.length > 0) {
      return { status: 'DUPLICATES', duplicates: duplicateInfo };
    }

    if (checkMonthExists(month)) {
      deleteMonthArtifacts_(ss, month);
    }

    const rawSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getDataSheetName_(month));
writeMatrixToSheet_(rawSheet, normalizedRaw);
rawSheet.hideSheet();

    const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
    const abbrMap = buildAbbrMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName));
    const tableRows = buildMonthlyTableRows_(normalizedRaw, month, studentMap, abbrMap);

    const tableSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getTableSheetName_(month));
    writeTableSheet_(tableSheet, tableRows);
    sortMonthlyTable_(tableSheet);
    formatScoreLikeSheet_(tableSheet);

    for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
      const classSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getClassSheetName_(month, classNum));
      writeClassSheet_(classSheet, month, classNum);
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      formatScoreLikeSheet_(classSheet);
    }

    updateUpperSheet_(ss, month, tableRows);

updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, month);
finalizeBaseSheets_(ss);
ss.setActiveSheet(tableSheet);

    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();

    return {
      status: 'SUCCESS',
      month: month,
      count: tableRows.length
    };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function deleteMonthData(month) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    month = normalizeUsedMockMonth_(month);
    ensureBaseSheets_(ss);
    if (!monthArtifactsExist_(ss, month)) {
      return { status: 'NOT_FOUND', month: month };
    }
    deleteMonthArtifacts_(ss, month);
    updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, getLatestExistingMonth_(ss));
finalizeBaseSheets_(ss);
    ss.setActiveSheet(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName));
    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
    return { status: 'DELETED', month: month };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function ensureBaseSheets_(ss) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const legacyUpperName = '상위권 누적표';
  const upperName = CONFIG.upperSheetName;

  // 예전 이름 탭이 있고 현재 이름 탭이 없으면 이름 변경
  const legacyUpper = ss.getSheetByName(legacyUpperName);
  let currentUpper = ss.getSheetByName(upperName);

  if (legacyUpper && !currentUpper) {
    legacyUpper.setName(upperName);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  }

  const master = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  const abbr = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName);

  if (!master) throw new Error('내신석차연명부 탭이 없습니다.');
  if (!abbr) throw new Error('축약어 탭이 없습니다.');

  // 이름 변경 이후 반드시 다시 가져옴
  let upper = ss.getSheetByName(upperName);

  if (!upper) {
    upper = ss.insertSheet(upperName);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    upper = ss.getSheetByName(upperName);
  }

  if (!upper) {
    throw new Error('학생별 누적표 탭을 만들지 못했습니다.');
  }

  ensureHeaderRow_(upper, CONFIG.tableHeaders);
}

function finalizeBaseSheets_(ss) {
  const master = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  const abbr = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName);
  const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);

  applyCommonSheetStyle_(master);
  applyCommonSheetStyle_(abbr);
  applyCommonSheetStyle_(upper, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);

  applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(master);
  applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(abbr);
  applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(upper, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);

  hideStaticSheets_(ss);

  // 모의고사 또는 내신 자료가 갱신될 때 전용 분석 탭도 함께 갱신함.
  // 오류가 발생해도 기존 자료 처리 흐름은 중단하지 않음.
  safeRefreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss);
}

function getStaticHiddenSheetNames_() {
  return [
    CONFIG.masterSheetName,
    CONFIG.abbrSheetName,
    '대학지원',
    '상담',
    '대학정보',
    '정보',
    '학생사진'
  ];
}

function safeHideSheet_(ss, sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  try {
    if (sheet.isSheetHidden()) return;
    const visibleCount = ss.getSheets().filter(s => !s.isSheetHidden()).length;
    if (visibleCount <= 1) return;
    sheet.hideSheet();
  } catch (e) {}
}

function hideStaticSheets_(ss) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  getStaticHiddenSheetNames_().forEach(name => {
    safeHideSheet_(ss, ss.getSheetByName(name));
  });

  const dataRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사 데이터$/;
  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    if (dataRegex.test(sheet.getName())) {
      safeHideSheet_(ss, sheet);
    }
  });
}

function updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, currentMonth) {
  const dataRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사 데이터$/;
  const classRegex = /^([1-8])반\((\d+)월\)$/;

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();
    const dataMatch = name.match(dataRegex);
    const classMatch = name.match(classRegex);

    if (dataMatch) {
      sheet.hideSheet();
      return;
    }

    if (classMatch) {
      if (currentMonth && Number(classMatch[2]) === Number(currentMonth)) {
        sheet.showSheet();
      } else {
        sheet.hideSheet();
      }
    }
  });

  hideStaticSheets_(ss);
}

function getLatestExistingMonth_(ss) {
  const tableRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const months = ss.getSheets()
    .map(sheet => {
      const match = sheet.getName().match(tableRegex);
      return match ? Number(match[1]) : null;
    })
    .filter(v => v !== null && isUsedMockMonth_(v));

  return months.length ? Math.max(...months) : null;
}

function applyCommonSheetStyle_(sheet, minCols) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), minCols || 1);

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.setColumnWidths(1, lastCol, 60);
  sheet.setRowHeights(1, lastRow, 30);

  const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol);
  range
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setWrapStrategy(SpreadsheetApp.WrapStrategy.CLIP)
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);

  const filter = sheet.getFilter();
  if (filter) filter.remove();
  range.createFilter();
}

function applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(sheet, minCols) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), minCols || 1);
  const range = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol);
  const displayValues = range.getDisplayValues();

  const fontSizes = displayValues.map(row =>
    row.map(value => getFittedFontSize_(value))
  );

  range.setFontSizes(fontSizes);
}

function getFittedFontSize_(value) {
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text) return 10;

  let units = 0;
  for (const ch of text) {
    if (ch === ' ') {
      units += 0.6;
    } else if (/[\u0000-\u007F]/.test(ch)) {
      units += 1;
    } else {
      units += 1.9;
    }
  }

  return Math.max(1, Math.min(10, Math.floor(76 / units)));
}

function deleteMonthArtifacts_(ss, month) {
  const names = [getDataSheetName_(month), getTableSheetName_(month)];
  for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
    names.push(getClassSheetName_(month, classNum));
  }

  names.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  });

  removeMonthFromUpperSheet_(ss, month);
}

function removeMonthFromUpperSheet_(ss, month) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders);
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) {
    formatScoreLikeSheet_(sheet);
    return;
  }
  const data = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).getValues();
  const kept = data.filter(row => Number(row[0]) !== month);
  rewriteUpperData_(sheet, kept);
}

function updateUpperSheet_(ss, month, monthlyRows) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders);

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  let existing = [];

  if (lastRow >= 2) {
    existing = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).getValues();
  }

  existing = existing.filter(row => Number(row[0]) !== month);

  const merged = existing.concat(monthlyRows);
  merged.sort(compareUpperRows_);
  rewriteUpperData_(sheet, merged);
}

function rewriteUpperData_(sheet, rows) {
  ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders);
  const maxRows = Math.max(sheet.getMaxRows() - 1, 1);
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, maxRows, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).clearContent().clearFormat();
  if (rows.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).setValues(rows);
  }
  formatScoreLikeSheet_(sheet, true);
  sortUpperSheet_(sheet);
}

function writeTableSheet_(sheet, rows) {
  ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders);
  if (rows.length > 0) {
    sheet.getRange(2, 1, rows.length, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).setValues(rows);
  }
}

function writeClassSheet_(sheet, month, classNum) {
  ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders);
  const sourceTable = getTableSheetName_(month);
  const formula = `=IFERROR(SORT(FILTER('${sourceTable}'!A2:T,'${sourceTable}'!B2:B<>"",VALUE(MID('${sourceTable}'!B2:B,2,1))=${classNum}),2,TRUE),"")`;
  sheet.getRange('A2').setFormula(formula);
}

function ensureHeaderRow_(sheet, headers) {
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setValues([headers]);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, headers.length).setFontWeight('bold').setHorizontalAlignment('center').setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
}

function writeMatrixToSheet_(sheet, matrix) {
  if (matrix.length === 0) return;
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, matrix.length, matrix[0].length).setValues(matrix);
  applyCommonSheetStyle_(sheet);
  applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(sheet);
}

function freezeHeader_(sheet) {
  if (sheet) sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
}

function applyFilterToUsedRange_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < 1) return;
  const filter = sheet.getFilter();
  if (filter) filter.remove();
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).createFilter();
}

function applyBordersToUsedRange_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 1 || lastCol < 1) return;
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true);
}

function formatScoreLikeSheet_(sheet, isUpperSheet) {
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);
  if (lastCol < CONFIG.tableHeaders.length) return;

  applyCommonSheetStyle_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);

  if (lastRow >= 2) {
    const bodyRange = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);
    bodyRange.setBackground(null).setFontColor('#000000');

    const values = bodyRange.getValues();
    const backgrounds = [];
    const fontColors = [];
    const monthColorMap = isUpperSheet ? buildMonthColorMap_(values) : {};

    for (let r = 0; r < values.length; r++) {
      const row = values[r];
      const naesin = toNumber_(row[3]);
      const month = Number(row[0]);
      const bgColor = naesin !== null && naesin >= 1 && naesin <= 2 ? CONFIG.visibleYellow : '#ffffff';
      const textColor = isUpperSheet ? (monthColorMap[month] || '#000000') : '#000000';
      backgrounds.push(new Array(CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).fill(bgColor));
      fontColors.push(new Array(CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).fill(textColor));
    }

    bodyRange.setBackgrounds(backgrounds);
    bodyRange.setFontColors(fontColors);
  }

  applyAutoFontFitToSheet_(sheet, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);
  applyGradeColorStyle_(sheet);
}

function buildMonthColorMap_(rows) {
  const months = [...new Set(rows.map(row => Number(row[0])).filter(v => !isNaN(v)))].sort((a, b) => b - a);
  const map = {};
  months.forEach((month, index) => {
    map[month] = CONFIG.latestTextColors[Math.min(index, CONFIG.latestTextColors.length - 1)];
  });
  return map;
}

function sortMonthlyTable_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 3) return;
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).sort([
    { column: 4, ascending: true },
    { column: 2, ascending: true }
  ]);
}

function sortUpperSheet_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 3) return;
  sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).sort([
    { column: 4, ascending: true },
    { column: 2, ascending: true },
    { column: 1, ascending: false }
  ]);
}

function compareUpperRows_(a, b) {
  const naesinA = toNumber_(a[3]);
  const naesinB = toNumber_(b[3]);
  if (naesinA !== naesinB) return naesinA - naesinB;
  const studentA = String(a[1]);
  const studentB = String(b[1]);
  if (studentA !== studentB) return studentA.localeCompare(studentB, 'ko');
  return Number(b[0]) - Number(a[0]);
}

function buildMonthlyTableRows_(rawValues, month, studentMap, abbrMap) {
  const rawMap = {};

  for (let i = 2; i < rawValues.length; i++) {
    const row = rawValues[i];
    if (isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;

    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number) continue;

    const key = makeStudentKey_(year, classNum, number);
    rawMap[key] = row;
  }

  const rows = [];
  Object.keys(studentMap)
    .sort((a, b) => String(studentMap[a].studentNo).localeCompare(String(studentMap[b].studentNo), 'ko'))
    .forEach(key => {
      const studentInfo = studentMap[key];
      const row = rawMap[key];

      if (!row) {
  rows.push([
    month,
    studentInfo.studentNo,
    studentInfo.name,
    normalizeNumericCell_(studentInfo.naesin),

    // 국어: 선택, 점수, 등급
    '미응시', 0, 99,

    // 수학: 선택, 점수, 등급
    '미응시', 0, 99,

    // 영어: 점수, 등급
    0, 99,

    // 탐구1: 선택, 점수, 등급
    '미응시', 0, 99,

    // 탐구2: 선택, 점수, 등급
    '미응시', 0, 99,

    // 3개합, 2개합
    99,
    99
  ]);
  return;
}

      const koreanChoice = abbreviateSubject_(row[5], abbrMap) || '미응시';
      const mathChoice = abbreviateSubject_(row[12], abbrMap) || '미응시';
      const inquiry1Choice = abbreviateSubject_(row[24], abbrMap) || '미응시';
      const inquiry2Choice = abbreviateSubject_(row[29], abbrMap) || '미응시';

      const grades = [row[11], row[18], row[22], row[28], row[33]];
      const grade3 = calcBestGradeSum_(grades, 3);
      const grade2 = calcBestGradeSum_(grades, 2);

      rows.push([
        month,
        studentInfo.studentNo,
        studentInfo.name,
        normalizeNumericCell_(studentInfo.naesin),
        koreanChoice,
        formatScoreValue_(row[8]),
        formatGradeValue_(row[11]),
        mathChoice,
        formatScoreValue_(row[15]),
        formatGradeValue_(row[18]),
        formatScoreValue_(row[19]),
        formatGradeValue_(row[22]),
        inquiry1Choice,
        formatScoreValue_(row[25]),
        formatGradeValue_(row[28]),
        inquiry2Choice,
        formatScoreValue_(row[30]),
        formatGradeValue_(row[33]),
        grade3,
        grade2
      ]);
    });

  return rows;
}

function formatMockValue_(value) {
  const normalized = normalizeNumericCell_(value);
  return normalized === '' ? '-' : normalized;
}

function formatScoreValue_(value) {
  const normalized = normalizeNumericCell_(value);
  return normalized === '' ? 0 : normalized;
}

function formatGradeValue_(value) {
  const normalized = normalizeNumericCell_(value);
  return normalized === '' ? 99 : normalized;
}

function calcBestGradeSum_(gradeCandidates, countNeeded) {
  const valid = gradeCandidates
    .map(v => toNumber_(v))
    .filter(v => v !== null)
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);
  if (valid.length < countNeeded) return 99;
  return valid.slice(0, countNeeded).reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0);
}

function buildStudentMap_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow) return {};

  const numRows = lastRow - MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow + 1;
  const values = sheet
    .getRange(MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceStartCol, numRows, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceNumCols)
    .getDisplayValues();

  const map = {};
  values.forEach(row => {
    const year = extractNumberText_(row[0]);       // B열 학년
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(row[1]);   // C열 반
    const number = extractNumberText_(row[2]);     // D열 번호
    const name = trimCell_(row[3]);                // E열 이름
    const naesin = row[MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.naesinRelativeIndex]; // R열 전학년 내신

    if (!year || !classNum || !number || !name) return;

    const key = makeStudentKey_(year, classNum, number);
    map[key] = {
      year: year,
      classNum: classNum,
      number: String(Number(number)).padStart(2, '0'),
      studentNo: makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number),
      name: name,
      naesin: naesin
    };
  });
  return map;
}

function buildAbbrMap_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return {};
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 2).getValues();
  const map = {};
  values.forEach(row => {
    const from = trimCell_(row[0]);
    const to = trimCell_(row[1]);
    if (from) map[from] = to || from;
  });
  return map;
}

function abbreviateSubject_(value, abbrMap) {
  const text = trimCell_(value);
  if (!text) return '';
  return abbrMap[text] || text;
}

function findDuplicateStudents_(rawValues, ss) {
  const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
  const seen = {};
  const duplicates = [];

  for (let i = 2; i < rawValues.length; i++) {
    const row = rawValues[i];
    if (isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;
    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number) continue;

    const studentNo = makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);
    if (seen[studentNo]) {
      const key = makeStudentKey_(year, classNum, number);
      const name = studentMap[key] ? studentMap[key].name : '';
      duplicates.push({ studentNo: studentNo, name: name || '(이름 확인 필요)' });
    }
    seen[studentNo] = true;
  }

  const uniqueMap = {};
  duplicates.forEach(item => {
    uniqueMap[item.studentNo] = item;
  });

  return Object.keys(uniqueMap).sort().map(key => uniqueMap[key]);
}

function readUploadFile_(payload) {
  if (!payload || !payload.base64 || !payload.fileName) {
    throw new Error('업로드 파일 정보가 올바르지 않습니다.');
  }

  const bytes = Utilities.base64Decode(payload.base64);
  const blob = Utilities.newBlob(bytes, payload.mimeType || MimeType.PLAIN_TEXT, payload.fileName);
  const lower = String(payload.fileName).toLowerCase();

  if (lower.endsWith('.csv')) {
    return parseCsvBlob_(blob);
  }
  if (lower.endsWith('.xlsx') || lower.endsWith('.xls')) {
    return parseExcelBlob_(blob);
  }
  throw new Error('지원하지 않는 파일 형식입니다. xlsx, xls, csv만 업로드할 수 있습니다.');
}

function parseCsvBlob_(blob) {
  const charsets = ['UTF-8', 'MS949', 'EUC-KR'];
  for (let i = 0; i < charsets.length; i++) {
    try {
      const text = blob.getDataAsString(charsets[i]);
      const rows = Utilities.parseCsv(text);
      if (rows && rows.length > 0) return rows;
    } catch (e) {}
  }
  throw new Error('CSV 파일을 읽지 못했습니다. 인코딩을 확인해 주세요.');
}

function parseExcelBlob_(blob) {
  let tempId = '';
  try {
    const created = Drive.Files.create(
      {
        name: 'temp_upload_' + new Date().getTime(),
        mimeType: 'application/vnd.google-apps.spreadsheet'
      },
      blob
    );

    tempId = created.id;

    const tempSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(tempId);
    const tempSheet = tempSs.getSheets()[0];
    return tempSheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues();
  } catch (e) {
    throw new Error('엑셀 파일 변환 상세 오류: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : e));
  } finally {
    if (tempId) {
      try {
        DriveApp.getFileById(tempId).setTrashed(true);
      } catch (e) {}
    }
  }
}

function createFreshSheet_(ss, sheetName) {
  const old = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
  if (old) ss.deleteSheet(old);
  return ss.insertSheet(sheetName);
}

function getDataSheetName_(month) {
  return `(${month}월)모의고사 데이터`;
}

function getTableSheetName_(month) {
  return `(${month}월)모의고사표`;
}

function getClassSheetName_(month, classNum) {
  return `${classNum}반(${month}월)`;
}

function normalizeMonth_(month) {
  const value = Number(month);
  if (!value || value < 3 || value > 12) {
    throw new Error('월은 3~12 사이여야 합니다.');
  }
  return value;
}

function makeStudentKey_(year, classNum, number) {
  return [Number(year), Number(classNum), Number(number)].join('|');
}

function makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number) {
  return `${Number(year)}${Number(classNum)}${String(Number(number)).padStart(2, '0')}`;
}

function normalizeNumericCell_(value) {
  const num = toNumber_(value);
  return num === null ? '' : num;
}

function toNumber_(value) {
  if (value === '' || value === null || value === undefined) return null;
  if (typeof value === 'number') return value;
  const cleaned = String(value).replace(/,/g, '').trim();
  if (cleaned === '') return null;
  const num = Number(cleaned);
  return isNaN(num) ? null : num;
}

function trimCell_(value) {
  return value === null || value === undefined ? '' : String(value).trim();
}

function isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row) {
  return row.every(cell => trimCell_(cell) === '');
}

function rectangularize_(rows) {
  const width = rows.reduce((max, row) => Math.max(max, row.length), 0);
  return rows.map(row => {
    const copy = row.slice();
    while (copy.length < width) copy.push('');
    return copy;
  });
}

const APP_ICON_URL = 'https://luxury-rolypoly-a65ba5.netlify.app/icon-512.png';

    .addMetaTag('viewport', 'width=device-width, initial-scale=1, maximum-scale=1, user-scalable=no, viewport-fit=cover')
    .setXFrameOptionsMode(HtmlService.XFrameOptionsMode.ALLOWALL);
}

function mobileCheckPassword(password) {
  const pw = String(password || '').trim();
  return pw === '17752' || pw === '9810138';
}

function mobileGetLoginAccess(password) {
  const pw = String(password || '').trim();
  return {
    ok: pw === '17752' || pw === '9810138',
    canEditCollegeApply: pw === '9810138'
  };
}

function mobileGetInitData() {
  const cached = getCachedJson_('initData');
  if (cached) return cached;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const months = getAvailableMonths_(ss);

  const result = {
    currentYear: String(new Date().getFullYear()),
    months: months,
    subjectMonths: getAvailableSubjectMonths_(ss),
    middleSchools: getMiddleSchoolOptions_(ss)
  };

  putCachedJson_('initData', result, 300);
  return result;
}

function mobileGetNameSuggestions(keyword) {
  const query = String(keyword || '').trim();
  if (!query) return [];

  const cacheKey = 'nameSuggestions_' + query;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  if (!sheet) return [];

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getDisplayValues();
  const byStudent = {};

  values.forEach(row => {
    const studentNo = String(row[1] || '').trim();
    const name = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    if (!studentNo || !name) return;
    if (!name.includes(query)) return;

    if (!byStudent[studentNo]) {
      const classNum = extractClassNumFromStudentNo_(studentNo);
      byStudent[studentNo] = {
        studentNo: studentNo,
        name: name,
        classNum: classNum,
        label: `${name}(${classNum}반)`
      };
    }
  });

  const result = Object.values(byStudent)
    .sort((a, b) => {
      const nameCompare = a.name.localeCompare(b.name, 'ko');
      if (nameCompare !== 0) return nameCompare;
      return Number(a.classNum) - Number(b.classNum);
    })
    .slice(0, 10);

  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, result, 120);
  return result;
}

function mobileSearch(payload) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const selectedStudentNo = String(payload.studentNo || '').trim();
  const nameKeyword = String(payload.nameKeyword || '').trim();
  const classValue = String(payload.classValue || '').trim();
  const middleSchool = String(payload.middleSchool || '').trim();
  const month = payload.month ? normalizeMonth_(payload.month) : null;

  // 학생 상세는 사진·개별 정보가 포함되므로 캐시하지 않음
  if (selectedStudentNo) {
    return buildMobileStudentResult_(ss, selectedStudentNo);
  }

  // 이름 검색이 있으면 학생 개인 상세를 우선한다. 출신중 필터는 반/ALL 목록 조회에만 적용한다.
  if (nameKeyword) {
    const targetStudentNo = resolveStudentNoByExactName_(ss, nameKeyword);
    return buildMobileStudentResult_(ss, targetStudentNo);
  }

  if (!month) throw new Error('월을 선택해 주세요.');
  if (!classValue) throw new Error('반을 선택해 주세요.');

  const cacheKey = 'classResult_' + month + '_' + classValue + '_' + (middleSchool || 'ALL');
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const result = buildMobileClassResult_(ss, month, classValue, middleSchool);
  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, result, 180);
  return result;
}

function getAvailableMonths_(ss) {
  const cached = getCachedJson_('availableMonths');
  if (cached) return cached;

  const regex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const months = ss.getSheets()
    .map(sheet => {
      const match = sheet.getName().match(regex);
      return match ? Number(match[1]) : null;
    })
    .filter(v => v !== null && isUsedMockMonth_(v))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);

  const result = months.map(month => ({
    value: month,
    label: `${month}월`
  }));

  putCachedJson_('availableMonths', result, 300);
  return result;
}

function resolveStudentNoByExactName_(ss, nameKeyword) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) throw new Error('학생별 누적표에 데이터가 없습니다.');

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 3).getDisplayValues();
  const exact = {};

  values.forEach(row => {
    const studentNo = String(row[1] || '').trim();
    const name = String(row[2] || '').trim();
    if (!studentNo || !name) return;
    if (name !== nameKeyword) return;

    if (!exact[studentNo]) {
      exact[studentNo] = studentNo;
    }
  });

  const matches = Object.keys(exact);

  if (matches.length === 0) {
    throw new Error('해당 이름의 학생을 찾지 못했습니다.');
  }

  if (matches.length > 1) {
    throw new Error('동명이인이 있습니다. 자동완성 목록에서 반을 선택해 주세요.');
  }

  return matches[0];
}

function buildMobileClassResult_(ss, month, classValue, middleSchool) {
  let sheet;

  if (classValue === 'ALL') {
    sheet = ss.getSheetByName(getTableSheetName_(month));
  } else {
    sheet = ss.getSheetByName(getClassSheetName_(month, Number(classValue)));
  }

  if (!sheet) {
    throw new Error('선택한 월/반의 데이터가 없습니다.');
  }

  const titleBase = classValue === 'ALL' ? `${month}월 전체` : `${month}월 ${classValue}반`;
  const filterText = middleSchool && middleSchool !== 'ALL' ? ` / ${middleSchool}` : '';

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) {
    return {
      mode: 'class',
      title: titleBase + filterText,
      headers: ['학번', '이름', '내신', '국등급', '수등급', '영등급', '탐1등급', '탐2등급'],
      rows: []
    };
  }

  // A:R까지만 읽으면 충분
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 18).getDisplayValues();
  const schoolMap = buildStudentMiddleSchoolMap_(ss);
  const selectedSchool = String(middleSchool || '').trim();

  let rows = values
    .filter(row => String(row[1] || '').trim() !== '')
    .filter(row => {
      if (!selectedSchool || selectedSchool === 'ALL') return true;
      const studentNo = String(row[1] || '').trim();
      return String(schoolMap[studentNo] || '').trim() === selectedSchool;
    })
    .map(row => ([
      row[1],  // B 학번
      row[2],  // C 이름
      row[3],  // D 내신
      row[6],  // G 국등급
      row[9],  // J 수등급
      row[11], // L 영등급
      row[14], // O 탐1등급
      row[17]  // R 탐2등급
    ]));

  rows.sort((a, b) => {
    const naesinA = toSortNumber_(a[2]);
    const naesinB = toSortNumber_(b[2]);
    if (naesinA !== naesinB) return naesinA - naesinB;
    return String(a[0]).localeCompare(String(b[0]), 'ko');
  });

  return {
    mode: 'class',
    title: titleBase + filterText,
    headers: ['학번', '이름', '내신', '국등급', '수등급', '영등급', '탐1등급', '탐2등급'],
    rows: rows
  };
}

function buildMobileStudentResult_(ss, studentNo) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) throw new Error('학생별 누적표에 데이터가 없습니다.');

  // A:T까지 읽어 3개합, 2개합도 상세 정보에 활용
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 20).getDisplayValues();

  const matched = values
    .filter(row => String(row[1] || '').trim() === String(studentNo))
    .sort((a, b) => Number(b[0]) - Number(a[0]));

  if (matched.length === 0) {
    throw new Error('해당 학생의 누적 데이터를 찾지 못했습니다.');
  }

  const tableRows = matched.map(row => ([
    row[0],  // A 월
    row[1],  // B 학번
    row[2],  // C 이름
    row[3],  // D 내신
    row[4],  // E 국선택
    row[6],  // G 국등급
    row[7],  // H 수선택
    row[9],  // J 수등급
    row[11], // L 영등급
    row[12], // M 탐1선택
    row[14], // O 탐1등급
    row[15], // P 탐2선택
    row[17]  // R 탐2등급
  ]));

  const studentInfo = buildStudentInfoForMobile_(ss, matched, studentNo);

  return {
    mode: 'student',
    title: studentInfo.title,
    studentInfo: studentInfo,
    headers: ['월', '학번', '이름', '내신', '국선택', '국등급', '수선택', '수등급', '영등급', '탐1선택', '탐1등급', '탐2선택', '탐2등급'],
    rows: tableRows,
    charts: buildStudentCharts_(matched)
  };
}

function buildStudentCharts_(rows) {
  return [
    buildSingleChart_(rows, '국어', 4, 6),
    buildSingleChart_(rows, '수학', 7, 9),
    buildSingleChart_(rows, '영어', null, 11),
    buildSingleChart_(rows, '탐1', 12, 14),
    buildSingleChart_(rows, '탐2', 15, 17)
  ];
}

function buildSingleChart_(rows, label, choiceIdx, gradeIdx) {
  const points = rows
    .map(row => ({
      month: Number(row[0]),
      grade: toSortNumber_(row[gradeIdx])
    }))
    .filter(item => isFinite(item.month) && isFinite(item.grade));

  let title = `${label} 등급변화`;
  if (choiceIdx !== null) {
    const choiceInfo = buildChoiceInfoText_(rows, choiceIdx);
    title += `(${choiceInfo})`;
  }

  return {
    title: title,
    points: points
  };
}

function buildChoiceInfoText_(rows, choiceIdx) {
  const items = rows
    .map(row => ({
      month: Number(row[0]),
      choice: String(row[choiceIdx] || '').trim()
    }))
    .filter(item => isFinite(item.month) && item.choice !== '')
    .sort((a, b) => a.month - b.month);

  if (items.length === 0) return '-';

  const uniqueChoices = [...new Set(items.map(item => item.choice))];

  // 변화 없으면 과목명만
  if (uniqueChoices.length === 1) {
    return uniqueChoices[0];
  }

  const groups = [];
  items.forEach(item => {
    const last = groups[groups.length - 1];
    if (!last || last.choice !== item.choice) {
      groups.push({ choice: item.choice, months: [item.month] });
    } else {
      last.months.push(item.month);
    }
  });

  return groups
    .map(group => `${group.months.map(monthToCircleText_).join('')}${group.choice}`)
    .join('→');
}

function monthToCircleText_(month) {
  const map = {
    1: '①', 2: '②', 3: '③', 4: '④', 5: '⑤', 6: '⑥',
    7: '⑦', 8: '⑧', 9: '⑨', 10: '⑩', 11: '⑪', 12: '⑫'
  };
  return map[Number(month)] || String(month);
}

function extractClassNumFromStudentNo_(studentNo) {
  const text = String(studentNo || '').trim();
  if (text.length < 2) return '';
  return String(Number(text.substring(1, 2)));
}

function toSortNumber_(value) {
  if (value === '' || value === null || value === undefined) return 999;
  const num = Number(String(value).replace(/,/g, '').trim());
  return isNaN(num) ? 999 : num;
  }

}

/*******************************
 * 내신석차연명부 업로드 기능
 * - 메뉴: 데이터 설정 > 내신석차연명부 업로드
 * - 업로드 파일의 첫 번째 시트를 내신석차연명부 탭으로 통째로 교체
 * - B열 학년, C열 반, D열 번호, E열 이름, R열 내신 / 7행부터 데이터
 * - 업로드 후 기존 월별 모의고사표, 반별표, 학생별 누적표 재계산
 *******************************/

const MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG = {
  dataStartRow: 7,
  sourceStartCol: 2,      // B열
  sourceNumCols: 17,      // B:R
  naesinRelativeIndex: 16 // B:R 범위에서 R열 인덱스
};
