  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('MasterUploadDialog')
    .setWidth(520)
    .setHeight(360);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, '내신석차연명부 업로드');
}

function processMasterUpload(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);

  let tempId = '';

  try {
    if (!payload || !payload.base64 || !payload.fileName) {
      throw new Error('업로드 파일 정보가 올바르지 않습니다.');
    }

    const fileName = String(payload.fileName || '');
    const lower = fileName.toLowerCase();
    if (!lower.endsWith('.xlsx') && !lower.endsWith('.xls')) {
      throw new Error('내신석차연명부는 xlsx 또는 xls 파일만 업로드할 수 있습니다.');
    }

    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const bytes = Utilities.base64Decode(payload.base64);
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(bytes, payload.mimeType || 'application/vnd.openxmlformats-officedocument.spreadsheetml.sheet', fileName);

    const created = Drive.Files.create(
      {
        name: 'temp_master_upload_' + new Date().getTime(),
        mimeType: 'application/vnd.google-apps.spreadsheet'
      },
      blob
    );

    tempId = created.id;

    const tempSs = SpreadsheetApp.openById(tempId);
    const tempSheet = tempSs.getSheets()[0];
    validateMasterSheet_(tempSheet);

    replaceMasterSheet_(ss, tempSheet);
    applyMasterSheetFontSize10_(ss);
    rebuildAllMonthlySheetsAfterMasterUpdate_(ss);

    const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
    if (upper) ss.setActiveSheet(upper);
    hideStaticSheets_(ss);

    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
    return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
  } finally {
    if (tempId) {
      try {
        DriveApp.getFileById(tempId).setTrashed(true);
      } catch (e) {}
    }
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function validateMasterSheet_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow) {
    throw new Error('내신석차연명부 데이터가 없습니다. 7행부터 학생 데이터가 있어야 합니다.');
  }

  const numRows = lastRow - MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow + 1;
  const values = sheet
    .getRange(MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceStartCol, numRows, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceNumCols)
    .getDisplayValues();

  const validCount = values.filter(row => {
    const year = extractNumberText_(row[0]);
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(row[1]);
    const number = extractNumberText_(row[2]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[3]);
    return year && classNum && number && name;
  }).length;

  if (validCount === 0) {
    throw new Error('학생 데이터를 찾지 못했습니다. B열 학년, C열 반, D열 번호, E열 이름, R열 내신 구조인지 확인해 주세요.');
  }
}

function replaceMasterSheet_(ss, sourceSheet) {
  const oldSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  const tempSheetName = '__새_내신석차연명부__' + new Date().getTime();
  const oldSheetName = '__기존_내신석차연명부__' + new Date().getTime();

  const copied = sourceSheet.copyTo(ss);
  copied.setName(tempSheetName);

  if (oldSheet) {
    oldSheet.setName(oldSheetName);
  }

  copied.setName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  ss.setActiveSheet(copied);
  ss.moveActiveSheet(1);

  if (oldSheet) {
    ss.deleteSheet(oldSheet);
  }
}

function rebuildAllMonthlySheetsAfterMasterUpdate_(ss) {
  ensureBaseSheets_(ss);

  const masterSheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(masterSheet);
  const abbrMap = buildAbbrMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName));
  const months = getAllMockMonthsForNaesinRefresh_(ss);

  months.forEach(month => {
    let tableSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getTableSheetName_(month));

    // 월별 모의고사표가 없으면 숨겨진 원자료 탭에서만 복구합니다.
    // 원자료 탭 자체는 절대 삭제하지 않습니다.
    if (!tableSheet) {
      const rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
      if (!rawSheet) return;

      const rawValues = rectangularize_(rawSheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues());
      const tableRows = buildMonthlyTableRows_(rawValues, month, studentMap, abbrMap);

      tableSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getTableSheetName_(month));
      writeTableSheet_(tableSheet, tableRows);
      sortMonthlyTable_(tableSheet);
      formatScoreLikeSheet_(tableSheet);
      ensureClassSheetsForMonth_(ss, month);
      return;
    }

    // 정상 상황: 기존 월별 모의고사표의 D열 내신만 갱신합니다.
    refreshNaesinColumnInSheet_(tableSheet, studentMap);
    sortMonthlyTable_(tableSheet);
    formatScoreLikeSheet_(tableSheet);
    ensureClassSheetsForMonth_(ss, month);
  });

  rebuildUpperSheetFromMonthlyTablesOnly_(ss);
  updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, months.length ? Math.max.apply(null, months) : null);
  finalizeBaseSheets_(ss);
}

function getAllMockMonthsForNaesinRefresh_(ss) {
  const monthMap = {};
  const rawRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사 데이터$/;
  const tableRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const classRegex = /^[1-8]반\((\d+)월\)$/;

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();

    let match = name.match(rawRegex);
    if (match) monthMap[Number(match[1])] = true;

    match = name.match(tableRegex);
    if (match) monthMap[Number(match[1])] = true;

    match = name.match(classRegex);
    if (match) monthMap[Number(match[1])] = true;
  });

  const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  if (upper && upper.getLastRow() >= 2) {
    const values = upper.getRange(2, 1, upper.getLastRow() - 1, 1).getDisplayValues();
    values.forEach(row => {
      const month = Number(row[0]);
      if (!isNaN(month) && month >= 3 && month <= 12) {
        monthMap[month] = true;
      }
    });
  }

  return Object.keys(monthMap)
    .map(Number)
    .filter(month => isUsedMockMonth_(month))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);
}

function refreshNaesinColumnInSheet_(sheet, studentMap) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  const numRows = lastRow - 1;
  const studentNos = sheet.getRange(2, 2, numRows, 1).getDisplayValues();

  const naesinValues = studentNos.map(row => {
    const studentNo = String(row[0] || '').trim();
    const key = makeStudentKeyFromStudentNo_(studentNo);
    const info = key ? studentMap[key] : null;
    return [info ? normalizeNumericCell_(info.naesin) : ''];
  });

  sheet.getRange(2, 4, numRows, 1).setValues(naesinValues); // D열 내신
}

function makeStudentKeyFromStudentNo_(studentNo) {
  const text = String(studentNo || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
  if (text.length < 4) return '';

  const year = text.substring(0, 1);
  const classNum = text.substring(1, 2);
  const number = text.substring(2);

  if (!year || !classNum || !number) return '';
  return makeStudentKey_(year, classNum, number);
}

function ensureClassSheetsForMonth_(ss, month) {
  const tableSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getTableSheetName_(month));
  if (!tableSheet) return;

  for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
    const sheetName = getClassSheetName_(month, classNum);
    let classSheet = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);

    if (!classSheet) {
      classSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, sheetName);
      writeClassSheet_(classSheet, month, classNum);
      formatScoreLikeSheet_(classSheet);
    }
  }
}

function rebuildUpperSheetFromMonthlyTablesOnly_(ss) {
  const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  ensureHeaderRow_(upper, CONFIG.tableHeaders);

  const tableRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const tableSheets = ss.getSheets()
    .map(sheet => {
      const match = sheet.getName().match(tableRegex);
      return match ? { month: Number(match[1]), sheet: sheet } : null;
    })
    .filter(item => item !== null)
    .sort((a, b) => a.month - b.month);

  const rows = [];

  tableSheets.forEach(item => {
    const sheet = item.sheet;
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow < 2) return;

    const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CONFIG.tableHeaders.length).getValues();
    values.forEach(row => {
      if (String(row[1] || '').trim() !== '') rows.push(row);
    });
  });

  rewriteUpperData_(upper, rows);
}

function applyMasterSheetFontSize10_(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  if (!sheet) return;

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  const lastRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1);
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 1);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, lastCol).setFontSize(10);
}

function getRawDataMonths_(ss) {
  const regex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사 데이터$/;
  return ss.getSheets()
    .map(sheet => {
      const match = sheet.getName().match(regex);
      return match ? Number(match[1]) : null;
    })
    .filter(month => month !== null && isUsedMockMonth_(month))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);
}

function deleteDerivedMonthArtifacts_(ss, month) {
  const names = [getTableSheetName_(month)];
  for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
    names.push(getClassSheetName_(month, classNum));
  }

  names.forEach(name => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(name);
    if (sheet) ss.deleteSheet(sheet);
  });
}

function extractNumberText_(value) {
  const text = trimCell_(value);
  if (!text) return '';
  const match = text.match(/\d+/);
  return match ? String(Number(match[0])) : '';
}


/*******************************
 * 정보 업로드 및 학생 상세 정보 조회
 * - 메뉴: 데이터 설정 > 학생 정보 업로드 > 설문조사 결과 붙여넣기 확인
 * - 사용자가 엑셀 설문조사 결과를 정보 탭 A1부터 직접 붙여넣음
 * - A열 학년, B열 반, C열 번호, D열 이름 / 1행 헤드, 2행부터 데이터
 *******************************/

const INFO_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '정보',
  dataStartRow: 2,
  sourceStartCol: 1,
  sourceNumCols: 18
};

function showInfoUploadDialog() {
  const ui = SpreadsheetApp.getUi();
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(INFO_CONFIG.sheetName);

  if (!sheet) {
    ui.alert(
      '설문조사 결과 붙여넣기 안내',
      '구글시트에 \'정보\' 탭을 만든 뒤, 설문조사 결과 엑셀 내용을 A1부터 직접 붙여넣으세요.\n\n필수 1행 헤더: 학년, 반, 번호, 이름, 출신중, 내신, 농어촌, 특별전형, 생일, 연락처, 계열, 희망학과1, 희망학과2, 주소, 父성명, 父연락처, 母성명, 母연락처',
      ui.ButtonSet.OK
    );
    return;
  }

  try {
    validateInfoSheet_(sheet);
    hideStaticSheets_(ss);
    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
    ui.alert(
      '정보 탭 확인 완료',
      '\'정보\' 탭의 1행 헤더와 학생 데이터 구조가 정상입니다.\n웹앱의 담임용, 간단 통합 조회, 학생 상세 정보에서 이 탭을 그대로 사용합니다.',
      ui.ButtonSet.OK
    );
  } catch (e) {
    ui.alert(
      '정보 탭 확인 필요',
      String(e && e.message ? e.message : e) + '\n\n엑셀의 설문조사 결과 내용을 \'정보\' 탭 A1부터 다시 붙여넣으세요.',
      ui.ButtonSet.OK
    );
  }
}

function processInfoUpload(payload) {
  throw new Error('설문조사 결과는 업로드 방식이 아니라 구글시트 \'정보\' 탭에 직접 붙여넣는 방식으로 변경되었습니다.');
}

function validateInfoSheet_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < INFO_CONFIG.dataStartRow) {
    throw new Error('정보 파일에 학생 데이터가 없습니다. 2행부터 학생 데이터가 있어야 합니다.');
  }

  const headers = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, Math.min(sheet.getLastColumn(), 18)).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const required = ['학년', '반', '번호', '이름'];
  for (let i = 0; i < required.length; i++) {
    if (String(headers[i] || '').trim() !== required[i]) {
      throw new Error('정보 파일의 A~D열 헤드는 학년, 반, 번호, 이름 순서여야 합니다.');
    }
  }
}

function replaceInfoSheet_(ss, sourceSheet) {
  const oldSheet = ss.getSheetByName(INFO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  const tempSheetName = '__새_정보__' + new Date().getTime();
  const oldSheetName = '__기존_정보__' + new Date().getTime();

  const copied = sourceSheet.copyTo(ss);
  copied.setName(tempSheetName);

  if (oldSheet) oldSheet.setName(oldSheetName);

  copied.setName(INFO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  ss.setActiveSheet(copied);
  ss.moveActiveSheet(2);

  if (oldSheet) ss.deleteSheet(oldSheet);
}

function buildInfoMap_(ss) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(INFO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) return {};

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = sheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < INFO_CONFIG.dataStartRow) return {};

  const cacheKey = 'infoMap_' + lastRow + '_' + lastCol;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const values = sheet
    .getRange(INFO_CONFIG.dataStartRow, INFO_CONFIG.sourceStartCol, lastRow - INFO_CONFIG.dataStartRow + 1, INFO_CONFIG.sourceNumCols)
    .getDisplayValues();

  const map = {};
  values.forEach(row => {
    const year = extractNumberText_(row[0]);
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(row[1]);
    const number = extractNumberText_(row[2]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[3]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number || !name) return;

    const studentNo = makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);
    map[studentNo] = {
      studentNo: studentNo,
      name: name,
      school: trimCell_(row[4]),
      infoNaesin: trimCell_(row[5]),
      rural: trimCell_(row[6]),
      special: trimCell_(row[7]),
      birth: trimCell_(row[8]),
      studentPhone: trimCell_(row[9]),
      track: trimCell_(row[10]),
      major1: trimCell_(row[11]),
      major2: trimCell_(row[12]),
      address: trimCell_(row[13]),
      fatherName: trimCell_(row[14]),
      fatherPhone: trimCell_(row[15]),
      motherName: trimCell_(row[16]),
      motherPhone: trimCell_(row[17])
    };
  });

  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, map, 600);
  return map;
}

function getMiddleSchoolOptions_(ss) {
  const map = buildInfoMap_(ss);
  const schools = Object.values(map)
    .map(info => trimCell_(info.school))
    .filter(v => v !== '')
    .filter((v, idx, arr) => arr.indexOf(v) === idx)
    .sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko'));

  return [{ value: 'ALL', label: 'ALL(전체)' }].concat(schools.map(school => ({
    value: school,
    label: school
  })));
}

function buildStudentMiddleSchoolMap_(ss) {
  const infoMap = buildInfoMap_(ss);
  const result = {};
  Object.keys(infoMap).forEach(studentNo => {
    result[studentNo] = trimCell_(infoMap[studentNo].school);
  });
  return result;
}

function getInfoByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo) {
  const map = buildInfoMap_(ss);
  return map[String(studentNo || '').trim()] || null;
}

function getMasterGradeInfoByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo) {
  const blank = {
    overall: '',
    g1s1: '', g1s2: '', g1all: '',
    g2s1: '', g2s2: '', g2all: '',
    g3s1: '', g3s2: '', g3all: ''
  };

  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  if (!sheet) return blank;

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow) return blank;

  // B:R 범위. I~R열은 상대 인덱스 7~16입니다.
  const values = sheet
    .getRange(MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceStartCol, lastRow - MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow + 1, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceNumCols)
    .getDisplayValues();

  const target = String(studentNo || '').trim();
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const row = values[i];
    const year = extractNumberText_(row[0]);
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(row[1]);
    const number = extractNumberText_(row[2]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number) continue;

    const currentNo = makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);
    if (currentNo !== target) continue;

    return {
      overall: trimCell_(row[16]), // R열
      g1s1: trimCell_(row[7]),     // I열
      g1s2: trimCell_(row[8]),     // J열
      g1all: trimCell_(row[9]),    // K열
      g2s1: trimCell_(row[10]),    // L열
      g2s2: trimCell_(row[11]),    // M열
      g2all: trimCell_(row[12]),   // N열
      g3s1: trimCell_(row[13]),    // O열
      g3s2: trimCell_(row[14]),    // P열
      g3all: trimCell_(row[15])    // Q열
    };
  }

  return blank;
}

/*******************************
 * 학생 사진 업로드 기능
 * - 메뉴: 데이터 설정 > 사진 업로드
 * - 파일명: 이름(번호).jpg 또는 이름(학번).jpg
 * - 같은 학생 기존 사진은 새 사진으로 교체
 *******************************/

const PHOTO_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '학생사진',
  folderName: '학생사진_모의고사',
  folderIdPropertyKey: 'STUDENT_PHOTO_FOLDER_ID',
  headers: ['업로드일시', '학번', '학년', '반', '번호', '이름', '원본파일명', '저장파일명', '파일ID', 'MIME']
};

function processPhotoUpload(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);

  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    ensureBaseSheets_(ss);

    const photoSheet = ensurePhotoSheet_(ss);
    const files = payload && Array.isArray(payload.files) ? payload.files : [];

    if (files.length === 0) {
      throw new Error('업로드할 사진 파일이 없습니다.');
    }

    const folder = getOrCreatePhotoFolder_(ss);

    const students = buildStudentDirectory_(ss);
    const photoRowMap = buildPhotoRowMap_(photoSheet);

    const results = [];
    const errors = [];
    const trashFileIds = [];
    const recordByStudentNo = {};
    const recordOrder = [];

    files.forEach(file => {
      try {
        validatePhotoFile_(file);

        const parsed = parsePhotoFileName_(file.fileName);
        const student = resolveStudentForPhotoFromDirectory_(students, parsed);
        const studentNo = String(student.studentNo);
        const saveName = buildPhotoSaveName_(student, file.fileName);

        const bytes = Utilities.base64Decode(file.base64);
        const blob = Utilities.newBlob(
          bytes,
          file.mimeType || 'application/octet-stream',
          saveName
        );

        const created = folder.createFile(blob).setName(saveName);

        const oldRecord = photoRowMap[studentNo];
        if (oldRecord && oldRecord.fileId && oldRecord.fileId !== created.getId()) {
          trashFileIds.push(oldRecord.fileId);
        }

        if (recordByStudentNo[studentNo] && recordByStudentNo[studentNo].fileId) {
          trashFileIds.push(recordByStudentNo[studentNo].fileId);
        }

        if (!recordByStudentNo[studentNo]) {
          recordOrder.push(studentNo);
        }

        recordByStudentNo[studentNo] = {
          fileId: created.getId(),
          row: [
            new Date(),
            studentNo,
            student.year,
            student.classNum,
            student.number,
            student.name,
            file.fileName,
            saveName,
            created.getId(),
            file.mimeType || blob.getContentType() || ''
          ]
        };

        results.push({
          originalFileName: file.fileName,
          savedFileName: saveName,
          studentNo: studentNo,
          name: student.name,
          classNum: student.classNum,
          number: student.number
        });
      } catch (e) {
        errors.push({
          fileName: file && file.fileName ? file.fileName : '(파일명 없음)',
          message: e && e.message ? e.message : String(e)
        });
      }
    });

    const appendRows = [];

    recordOrder.forEach(studentNo => {
      const record = recordByStudentNo[studentNo];
      const oldRecord = photoRowMap[studentNo];

      if (oldRecord && oldRecord.rowNumber) {
        photoSheet
          .getRange(oldRecord.rowNumber, 1, 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length)
          .setValues([record.row]);
      } else {
        appendRows.push(record.row);
      }
    });

    if (appendRows.length > 0) {
      photoSheet
        .getRange(photoSheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, appendRows.length, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length)
        .setValues(appendRows);
    }

    photoSheet.hideSheet();

    [...new Set(trashFileIds)].forEach(fileId => {
      try {
        DriveApp.getFileById(fileId).setTrashed(true);
      } catch (e) {}
    });

    return {
      status: errors.length === 0 ? 'SUCCESS' : (results.length > 0 ? 'PARTIAL' : 'FAILED'),
      count: results.length,
      results: results,
      errors: errors
    };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function validatePhotoFile_(file) {
  if (!file || !file.fileName || !file.base64) {
    throw new Error('파일 정보가 올바르지 않습니다.');
  }

  const lower = String(file.fileName).toLowerCase();
  const allowed = ['.jpg', '.jpeg', '.png', '.webp', '.gif'];
  const ok = allowed.some(ext => lower.endsWith(ext));

  if (!ok) {
    throw new Error('사진 파일만 업로드할 수 있습니다. jpg, jpeg, png, webp, gif 형식만 허용됩니다.');
  }

  if (file.size && Number(file.size) > 5 * 1024 * 1024) {
    throw new Error('사진 1장 용량은 5MB 이하로 줄여 주세요.');
  }
}

function parsePhotoFileName_(fileName) {
  const title = stripFileExtension_(fileName).trim();
  const match = title.match(/^(.+?)\s*\(([^()]+)\)\s*$/);

  if (!match) {
    throw new Error('파일명 형식이 올바르지 않습니다. 예: 홍길동(1).jpg, 홍길동(33).jpg, 홍길동(3601).jpg');
  }

  const name = String(match[1] || '').trim();
  const identifier = String(match[2] || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();

  if (!name) {
    throw new Error('파일명에서 학생 이름을 찾지 못했습니다.');
  }

  if (!identifier) {
    throw new Error('파일명 괄호 안에서 번호를 찾지 못했습니다.');
  }

  return {
    name: name,
    identifier: identifier,
    originalFileName: fileName
  };
}

function buildStudentDirectory_(ss) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  if (!sheet) throw new Error('내신석차연명부 탭이 없습니다.');

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow) return [];

  const numRows = lastRow - MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow + 1;
  const values = sheet
    .getRange(MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.dataStartRow, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceStartCol, numRows, MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.sourceNumCols)
    .getDisplayValues();
  const students = [];

  values.forEach(row => {
    const year = extractNumberText_(row[0]);
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(row[1]);
    const number = extractNumberText_(row[2]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[3]);
    const naesin = row[MASTER_UPLOAD_CONFIG.naesinRelativeIndex];

    if (!year || !classNum || !number || !name) return;

    students.push({
      year: String(Number(year)),
      classNum: String(Number(classNum)),
      number: String(Number(number)).padStart(2, '0'),
      name: name,
      naesin: naesin,
      studentNo: makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number)
    });
  });

  return students;
}

function resolveStudentForPhotoFromDirectory_(students, parsed) {
  const name = parsed.name;
  const identifier = parsed.identifier;

  let matches = [];

  if (identifier.length >= 4) {
    matches = students.filter(student =>
      student.name === name && String(student.studentNo) === String(identifier)
    );
  } else {
    const targetNumber = String(Number(identifier)).padStart(2, '0');

    matches = students.filter(student =>
      student.name === name &&
      String(student.number).padStart(2, '0') === targetNumber
    );
  }

  if (matches.length === 0) {
    throw new Error(`${name}(${identifier})에 해당하는 학생을 내신석차연명부에서 찾지 못했습니다.`);
  }

  if (matches.length > 1) {
    throw new Error(`${name}(${identifier})와 일치하는 학생이 여러 명입니다. 파일명을 ${name}(학번) 형식으로 바꿔 업로드해 주세요.`);
  }

  return matches[0];
}

function buildPhotoSaveName_(student, originalFileName) {
  const ext = getFileExtension_(originalFileName) || '.jpg';
  return `${student.name}(${student.studentNo})${ext}`;
}

function stripFileExtension_(fileName) {
  return String(fileName || '').replace(/\.[^.]+$/, '');
}

function getFileExtension_(fileName) {
  const match = String(fileName || '').match(/\.[^.]+$/);
  return match ? match[0].toLowerCase() : '';
}

function getOrCreatePhotoFolder_(ss) {
  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const savedId = props.getProperty(PHOTO_CONFIG.folderIdPropertyKey);

  if (savedId) {
    try {
      return DriveApp.getFolderById(savedId);
    } catch (e) {
      props.deleteProperty(PHOTO_CONFIG.folderIdPropertyKey);
    }
  }

  const spreadsheetFile = DriveApp.getFileById(ss.getId());
  const parents = spreadsheetFile.getParents();
  const parent = parents.hasNext() ? parents.next() : DriveApp.getRootFolder();

  const folders = parent.getFoldersByName(PHOTO_CONFIG.folderName);
  const folder = folders.hasNext() ? folders.next() : parent.createFolder(PHOTO_CONFIG.folderName);

  props.setProperty(PHOTO_CONFIG.folderIdPropertyKey, folder.getId());
  return folder;
}

function ensurePhotoSheet_(ss) {
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(PHOTO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(PHOTO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  }

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([PHOTO_CONFIG.headers]);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');

  sheet.hideSheet();
  return sheet;
}

function buildPhotoRowMap_(sheet) {
  const map = {};
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();

  if (lastRow < 2) return map;

  const values = sheet
    .getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length)
    .getDisplayValues();

  values.forEach((row, index) => {
    const studentNo = String(row[1] || '').trim();
    const fileId = String(row[8] || '').trim();

    if (!studentNo) return;

    map[studentNo] = {
      rowNumber: index + 2,
      fileId: fileId
    };
  });

  return map;
}

function getPhotoRecordByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(PHOTO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) return null;

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return null;

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();

  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    if (String(values[i][1] || '').trim() === String(studentNo)) {
      return {
        uploadedAt: values[i][0],
        studentNo: values[i][1],
        year: values[i][2],
        classNum: values[i][3],
        number: values[i][4],
        name: values[i][5],
        originalFileName: values[i][6],
        savedFileName: values[i][7],
        fileId: values[i][8],
        mimeType: values[i][9]
      };
    }
  }

  return null;
}

function getPhotoDataUrlForStudent_(ss, studentNo) {
  const record = getPhotoRecordByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo);
  if (!record || !record.fileId) return '';

  try {
    const file = DriveApp.getFileById(record.fileId);
    const blob = file.getBlob();
    const contentType = blob.getContentType() || record.mimeType || 'image/jpeg';
    const base64 = Utilities.base64Encode(blob.getBytes());
    return `data:${contentType};base64,${base64}`;
  } catch (e) {
    return '';
  }
}

function buildStudentInfoForMobile_(ss, matched, studentNo) {
  const latest = matched[matched.length - 1];
  const masterGrade = getMasterGradeInfoByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo);
  const extraInfo = getInfoByStudentNo_(ss, studentNo);
  const studentName = latest[2] || (extraInfo ? extraInfo.name : '');
  const studentPhone = extraInfo ? extraInfo.studentPhone : '';

  return {
    studentNo: studentNo,
    name: studentName,
    title: `${studentNo} ${studentName}${studentPhone ? ' / ' + studentPhone : ''}`,
    naesin: masterGrade.overall || latest[3] || '',
    latestMonth: latest[0] || '',
    latestThreeSum: latest[18] || '',
    latestTwoSum: latest[19] || '',
    photoDataUrl: getPhotoDataUrlForStudent_(ss, studentNo),
    gradeMatrix: masterGrade,
    info: extraInfo || {}
  };
}

function authorizePhotoUpload_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  ensureBaseSheets_(ss);
  ensurePhotoSheet_(ss);

  const folder = getOrCreatePhotoFolder_(ss);
  const file = folder.createFile(
    Utilities.newBlob('photo upload auth test', 'text/plain', 'photo_upload_auth_test.txt')
  );

  file.setTrashed(true);

  return 'OK';
}


/***********************
 * 교과용 과목별 조회
 ***********************/
const SUBJECT_MONTHS = [3, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10, 11];

function getAvailableSubjectMonths_(ss) {
  const cached = getCachedJson_('availableSubjectMonths');
  if (cached) return cached;

  const months = SUBJECT_MONTHS.filter(month => !!ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month)));
  const result = months.map(month => ({
    value: month,
    label: month + '월'
  }));

  putCachedJson_('availableSubjectMonths', result, 300);
  return result;
}


function buildNaesinByStudentNo_(ss) {
  const map = {};
  try {
    const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
    Object.keys(studentMap).forEach(key => {
      const item = studentMap[key];
      if (!item || !item.studentNo) return;
      const naesin = normalizeNumericCell_(item.naesin);
      if (naesin !== '') map[String(item.studentNo)] = String(naesin);
    });
  } catch (e) {}
  return map;
}

function buildSubjectDisplayName_(item, naesinMap, isMultiSubject) {
  const name = String(item && item.name != null ? item.name : '').trim();
  if (isMultiSubject) return name;

  const studentNo = String(item && item.studentNo != null ? item.studentNo : '').trim();
  const naesin = naesinMap && studentNo ? String(naesinMap[studentNo] || '').trim() : '';

  return naesin ? name + '(' + naesin + ')' : name;
}


function normalizeSimpleSearchText_(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value)
    .toLowerCase()
    .replace(/\s+/g, '')
    .trim();
}

function normalizeSimpleSearchDigits_(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value).replace(/\D/g, '');
}

function parseSimpleNaesinQuery_(query) {
  const text = String(query || '').trim();

  const rangeMatch = text.match(/^(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)\s*[~\-]\s*(\d+(?:\.\d+)?)$/);
  if (rangeMatch) {
    const a = Number(rangeMatch[1]);
    const b = Number(rangeMatch[2]);
    if (!isNaN(a) && !isNaN(b)) {
      return {
        type: 'range',
        min: Math.min(a, b),
        max: Math.max(a, b),
        center: (a + b) / 2
      };
    }
  }

  const singleMatch = text.match(/^(\d+(?:\.\d+))$/);
  if (singleMatch) {
    const center = Number(singleMatch[1]);
    if (!isNaN(center)) {
      return {
        type: 'single',
        min: Math.max(0, center - 0.1),
        max: center + 0.1,
        center: center
      };
    }
  }

  return null;
}


function parseSimpleBirthMonthQuery_(query) {
  const text = String(query || '').trim();
  const match = text.match(/^0?([1-9]|1[0-2])\s*월$/);
  if (!match) return null;
  return Number(match[1]);
}

function getBirthMonthFromValue_(value) {
  const raw = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!raw) return null;

  // 숫자만 추출해서 처리합니다.
  // 생년월일이 030315처럼 0으로 시작해도 시트에서는 30315로 들어갈 수 있으므로
  // 6자리보다 짧으면 왼쪽에 0을 채워 YYMMDD로 맞춥니다.
  const digits = normalizeSimpleSearchDigits_(raw);

  if (digits.length > 0 && digits.length <= 6) {
    const birth6 = digits.padStart(6, '0');
    const month = Number(birth6.substring(2, 4));
    return month >= 1 && month <= 12 ? month : null;
  }

  // 8자리(YYYYMMDD)인 경우
  if (digits.length === 8) {
    const month = Number(digits.substring(4, 6));
    return month >= 1 && month <= 12 ? month : null;
  }

  // 13.08.03, 2013-08-03처럼 구분자가 있는 경우
  const ymd = raw.match(/(\d{2,4})\D+(\d{1,2})\D+(\d{1,2})/);
  if (ymd) {
    const month = Number(ymd[2]);
    return month >= 1 && month <= 12 ? month : null;
  }

  return null;
}

function collectSimpleSearchStudents_(ss) {
  const masterMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
  const infoMap = buildInfoMap_(ss);
  const students = {};

  Object.keys(masterMap || {}).forEach(key => {
    const item = masterMap[key];
    if (!item || !item.studentNo) return;
    const studentNo = String(item.studentNo);
    students[studentNo] = {
      studentNo: studentNo,
      name: trimCell_(item.name),
      naesin: trimCell_(item.naesin),
      school: '',
      rural: '',
      special: '',
      birth: '',
      studentPhone: '',
      track: '',
      major1: '',
      major2: '',
      address: '',
      fatherName: '',
      fatherPhone: '',
      motherName: '',
      motherPhone: ''
    };
  });

  Object.keys(infoMap || {}).forEach(studentNo => {
    const info = infoMap[studentNo] || {};
    if (!students[studentNo]) {
      students[studentNo] = {
        studentNo: studentNo,
        name: trimCell_(info.name),
        naesin: trimCell_(info.infoNaesin)
      };
    }

    students[studentNo].name = students[studentNo].name || trimCell_(info.name);
    students[studentNo].naesin = students[studentNo].naesin || trimCell_(info.infoNaesin);
    students[studentNo].school = trimCell_(info.school);
    students[studentNo].rural = trimCell_(info.rural);
    students[studentNo].special = trimCell_(info.special);
    students[studentNo].birth = trimCell_(info.birth);
    students[studentNo].studentPhone = trimCell_(info.studentPhone);
    students[studentNo].track = trimCell_(info.track);
    students[studentNo].major1 = trimCell_(info.major1);
    students[studentNo].major2 = trimCell_(info.major2);
    students[studentNo].address = trimCell_(info.address);
    students[studentNo].fatherName = trimCell_(info.fatherName);
    students[studentNo].fatherPhone = trimCell_(info.fatherPhone);
    students[studentNo].motherName = trimCell_(info.motherName);
    students[studentNo].motherPhone = trimCell_(info.motherPhone);
  });

  return Object.values(students)
    .filter(item => item.studentNo && item.name)
    .sort((a, b) => String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko', { numeric: true }));
}

function scoreSimpleTextMatch_(queryNorm, value) {
  const valueText = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!valueText) return 0;

  const valueNorm = normalizeSimpleSearchText_(valueText);
  if (!valueNorm || !queryNorm) return 0;

  if (valueNorm === queryNorm) return 120;
  if (valueNorm.indexOf(queryNorm) === 0) return 95;
  if (valueNorm.indexOf(queryNorm) >= 0) return 75;
  return 0;
}

function buildSimpleMatchInfo_(label, value) {
  const text = trimCell_(value);
  return text ? label + ': ' + text : '';
}

function mobileSimpleSearch(payload) {
  const query = String(payload && payload.query || '').trim();
  if (!query) throw new Error('검색어를 입력해 주세요.');

  const cacheKey = 'simpleSearch_naesin_decimal_v4_' + query;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const students = collectSimpleSearchStudents_(ss);
  const queryNorm = normalizeSimpleSearchText_(query);
  const queryDigits = normalizeSimpleSearchDigits_(query);
  const naesinQuery = parseSimpleNaesinQuery_(query);
  const birthMonthQuery = parseSimpleBirthMonthQuery_(query);

  const results = [];

  students.forEach(student => {
    let score = 0;
    const matches = [];

    const naesinText = trimCell_(student.naesin);
    const naesinNum = toNumber_(naesinText);

    if (naesinQuery && naesinNum !== null) {
      if (naesinNum >= naesinQuery.min && naesinNum <= naesinQuery.max) {
        const diff = Math.abs(naesinNum - naesinQuery.center);
        score += 160 - Math.min(80, diff * 100);
        matches.push(buildSimpleMatchInfo_('내신', naesinText));
      }
    }

    // 내신 검색어(예: 1.5, 1.0~3.0)는 내신 칸만 검색합니다.
    // 소수점이 포함된 검색어의 숫자만 뽑아 전화번호·생년월일과 매칭되는 문제를 막기 위한 분기입니다.
    if (!naesinQuery) {
      if (birthMonthQuery !== null) {
        const birthMonth = getBirthMonthFromValue_(student.birth);
        if (birthMonth === birthMonthQuery) {
          score += 145;
          matches.push(buildSimpleMatchInfo_('생년월일', student.birth));
        }
      }

      if (queryDigits.length >= 4) {
        const digitFields = [
          ['학생 전화', student.studentPhone],
          ['부 전화', student.fatherPhone],
          ['모 전화', student.motherPhone],
          ['생년월일', student.birth],
          ['학번', student.studentNo]
        ];

        digitFields.forEach(item => {
          const label = item[0];
          const value = item[1];
          const digits = normalizeSimpleSearchDigits_(value);
          if (!digits) return;

          if (digits === queryDigits) {
            score += 150;
            matches.push(buildSimpleMatchInfo_(label, value));
          } else if (digits.indexOf(queryDigits) >= 0) {
            score += 95 + Math.min(20, queryDigits.length);
            matches.push(buildSimpleMatchInfo_(label, value));
          }
        });
      }

      const textFields = [
        ['학번', student.studentNo],
        ['이름', student.name],
        ['출신중', student.school],
        ['전형', student.track],
        ['농어촌', student.rural],
        ['특별', student.special],
        ['희망학과1', student.major1],
        ['희망학과2', student.major2],
        ['주소', student.address],
        ['부 성명', student.fatherName],
        ['모 성명', student.motherName]
      ];

      textFields.forEach(item => {
        const label = item[0];
        const value = item[1];
        const textScore = scoreSimpleTextMatch_(queryNorm, value);
        if (textScore > 0) {
          score += textScore;
          matches.push(buildSimpleMatchInfo_(label, value));
        }
      });
    }

    if (score > 0) {
      const seen = {};
      const uniqueMatches = matches.filter(text => {
        if (!text) return false;
        if (seen[text]) return false;
        seen[text] = true;
        return true;
      });

      results.push({
        studentNo: student.studentNo,
        name: student.name,
        naesin: naesinText,
        matchInfo: uniqueMatches.slice(0, 4).join(' / '),
        score: score
      });
    }
  });

  results.sort((a, b) => {
    const aNaesin = toNumber_(a.naesin);
    const bNaesin = toNumber_(b.naesin);

    if (naesinQuery) {
      if (aNaesin !== null && bNaesin !== null && aNaesin !== bNaesin) return aNaesin - bNaesin;
      if (aNaesin !== null && bNaesin === null) return -1;
      if (aNaesin === null && bNaesin !== null) return 1;
      return String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko', { numeric: true });
    }

    if (b.score !== a.score) return b.score - a.score;
    if (aNaesin !== null && bNaesin !== null && aNaesin !== bNaesin) return aNaesin - bNaesin;
    return String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko', { numeric: true });
  });

  const rows = results.slice(0, 80).map(item => [
    item.studentNo,
    item.name,
    item.naesin,
    item.matchInfo || ''
  ]);

  const result = {
    mode: 'simple',
    title: '학생 정보 기반 통합 전수 검색',
    query: query,
    headers: ['학번', '이름', '내신', '일치 정보'],
    rows: rows
  };

  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, result, 180);
  return result;
}


function mobileSubjectSearch(payload) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const month = normalizeSubjectMonth_(payload && payload.month);
  const group = String(payload && payload.group || '').trim();
  const subjects = normalizeSubjectList_(payload);

  if (subjects.length === 0) throw new Error('과목을 선택해 주세요.');

  const subjectKey = subjects.join('|');
  const cacheKey = 'subjectResult_v11_' + month + '_' + group + '_' + subjectKey;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
  if (!rawSheet) throw new Error(month + '월 모의고사 데이터 탭이 없습니다.');

  const lastRow = rawSheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 3) {
    return {
      mode: 'subject',
      title: month + '월 ' + subjectKey,
      subjectGroup: group,
      subjects: subjects,
      headers: [],
      rows: []
    };
  }

  // 실제 데이터가 있는 A:AL까지만 읽음. getDataRange()보다 빠름.
  const raw = rawSheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 38).getDisplayValues();
  let rows = [];
  subjects.forEach(subject => {
    rows = rows.concat(buildSubjectRowsFromRaw_(raw, subject, group));
  });

  if (subjects.length >= 2) {
    rows.sort(compareSubjectRowsForMulti_);
  } else {
    rows.sort(compareSubjectRows_);
  }

  const ranked = rows.map((row, index) => {
    row.rank = index + 1;
    return row;
  });

  const isKoreanOrMath = group === '국어' || group === '수학';
  const isMultiSubject = subjects.length >= 2;
  const naesinMap = buildNaesinByStudentNo_(ss);
  const abbrMap = buildAbbrMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName));
  const subjectTitle = subjects.join(', ');
  const trend = subjects.length === 1 ? buildSubjectCountTrend_(ss, month, subjects[0], group) : null;
  const title = trend ? `${month}월 ${subjects[0]}(${trend.display})` : `${month}월 ${subjectTitle}`;

  const result = {
    mode: 'subject',
    title: title,
    month: month,
    subjectGroup: group,
    subjects: subjects,
    analysisSubject: subjects[0] || '',
    analysisEnabled: subjects.length > 0 && subjects[0] !== '한국사' && (group !== '탐구' || subjects.length === 1),
    subjectTrend: trend,
    isMultiSubject: isMultiSubject,
    headers: isKoreanOrMath
      ? (isMultiSubject
        ? ['순위', '학번', '이름', '과목', '공통', '선택', '총점', '백분위', '등급']
        : ['순위', '학번', '이름(내신)', '공통', '선택', '총점', '백분위', '등급'])
      : (isMultiSubject
        ? ['순위', '학번', '이름', '과목', '총점', '백분위', '등급']
        : ['순위', '학번', '이름(내신)', '총점', '백분위', '등급']),
    rows: ranked.map(item => {
      const subjectText = abbreviateSubjectForSubjectTable_(item.subject, abbrMap);

      if (isKoreanOrMath) {
        return isMultiSubject
          ? [item.rank, item.studentNo, buildSubjectDisplayName_(item, naesinMap, isMultiSubject), subjectText, item.common, item.selected, item.total, item.percentile, item.grade]
          : [item.rank, item.studentNo, buildSubjectDisplayName_(item, naesinMap, isMultiSubject), item.common, item.selected, item.total, item.percentile, item.grade];
      }

      return isMultiSubject
        ? [item.rank, item.studentNo, item.name, subjectText, item.total, item.percentile, item.grade]
        : [item.rank, item.studentNo, buildSubjectDisplayName_(item, naesinMap, false), item.total, item.percentile, item.grade];
    })
  };

  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, result, 180);
  return result;
}


function abbreviateSubjectForSubjectTable_(subject, abbrMap) {
  const text = String(subject == null ? '' : subject).trim();
  if (!text) return '';

  if (abbrMap && abbrMap[text]) return abbrMap[text];

  const fallback = {
    '화법과작문': '화작',
    '언어와매체': '언매',
    '확률과통계': '확통',
    '미적분': '미적',
    '기하': '기하',
    '생활과윤리': '생윤',
    '윤리와사상': '윤사',
    '사회문화': '사문',
    '정치와법': '정법',
    '동아시아사': '동사',
    '세계사': '세계사',
    '한국지리': '한지',
    '세계지리': '세지',
    '경제': '경제',
    '물리학1': '물1',
    '물리학2': '물2',
    '화학1': '화1',
    '화학2': '화2',
    '생명과학1': '생1',
    '생명과학2': '생2',
    '지구과학1': '지1',
    '지구과학2': '지2',
    '한국사': '한국사',
    '영어': '영어'
  };

  return fallback[text] || text;
}

function normalizeSubjectList_(payload) {
  if (!payload) return [];

  const values = Array.isArray(payload.subjects)
    ? payload.subjects
    : [payload.subject];

  return values
    .map(v => canonicalSubjectName_(v))
    .filter(v => v !== '')
    .filter((v, idx, arr) => arr.indexOf(v) === idx);
}

function normalizeSubjectKey_(value) {
  let text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text) return '';

  if (typeof text.normalize === 'function') {
    text = text.normalize('NFKC');
  }

  text = text.toUpperCase();
  text = text.replace(/Ⅱ|II/g, '2');
  text = text.replace(/Ⅰ|I/g, '1');
  text = text.replace(/[·ㆍ∙･・]/g, '');
  text = text.replace(/[\s\-_./,，:;|\()（）\[\]{}<>]+/g, '');
  text = text.replace(/과목/g, '');

  return text;
}

function getSubjectAliasMap_() {
  const groups = {
    '화법과작문': ['화법과작문', '화법과 작문', '화작'],
    '언어와매체': ['언어와매체', '언어와 매체', '언매'],
    '확률과통계': ['확률과통계', '확률과 통계', '확통'],
    '미적분': ['미적분', '미적'],
    '기하': ['기하'],
    '영어': ['영어'],
    '생활과윤리': ['생활과윤리', '생활과 윤리', '생윤'],
    '윤리와사상': ['윤리와사상', '윤리와 사상', '윤사'],
    '사회문화': ['사회문화', '사회 문화', '사회·문화', '사회 · 문화', '사문'],
    '정치와법': ['정치와법', '정치와 법', '정법'],
    '세계사': ['세계사'],
    '동아시아사': ['동아시아사', '동아시아 사', '동사'],
    '한국지리': ['한국지리', '한국 지리', '한지'],
    '세계지리': ['세계지리', '세계 지리', '세지'],
    '경제': ['경제'],
    '물리학1': ['물리학1', '물리학Ⅰ', '물리학I', '물리1', '물리Ⅰ', '물리I', '물1'],
    '물리학2': ['물리학2', '물리학Ⅱ', '물리학II', '물리2', '물리Ⅱ', '물리II', '물2'],
    '화학1': ['화학1', '화학Ⅰ', '화학I', '화1'],
    '화학2': ['화학2', '화학Ⅱ', '화학II', '화2'],
    '생명과학1': ['생명과학1', '생명과학Ⅰ', '생명과학I', '생명1', '생명Ⅰ', '생명I', '생1'],
    '생명과학2': ['생명과학2', '생명과학Ⅱ', '생명과학II', '생명2', '생명Ⅱ', '생명II', '생2'],
    '지구과학1': ['지구과학1', '지구과학Ⅰ', '지구과학I', '지구1', '지구Ⅰ', '지구I', '지1'],
    '지구과학2': ['지구과학2', '지구과학Ⅱ', '지구과학II', '지구2', '지구Ⅱ', '지구II', '지2'],
    '한국사': ['한국사', '한국 사']
  };

  const map = {};
  Object.keys(groups).forEach(canonical => {
    groups[canonical].forEach(alias => {
      map[normalizeSubjectKey_(alias)] = canonical;
    });
  });
  return map;
}

function canonicalSubjectName_(value) {
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text) return '';

  const key = normalizeSubjectKey_(text);
  const map = getSubjectAliasMap_();
  return map[key] || text;
}

function isSameSubjectName_(a, b) {
  const keyA = normalizeSubjectKey_(canonicalSubjectName_(a));
  const keyB = normalizeSubjectKey_(canonicalSubjectName_(b));
  return keyA !== '' && keyA === keyB;
}

function normalizeSubjectMonth_(month) {
  const value = Number(month);
  if (!SUBJECT_MONTHS.includes(value)) {
    throw new Error('교과용 조회 월은 3월, 5월, 6월, 7월, 9월, 10월, 11월만 가능합니다.');
  }
  return value;
}

function buildSubjectRowsFromRaw_(raw, subject, group) {
  const rows = [];

  for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
    const row = raw[i];
    if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;

    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[4]);

    if (!year || !classNum || !number || !name) continue;

    const studentNo = makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);

    if (group === '국어') {
      const rawSubject = canonicalSubjectName_(row[5]);
      if (!isSameSubjectName_(rawSubject, subject)) continue;
      const total = trimCell_(row[8]);
      if (!total) continue;
      rows.push({
        studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
        subject: rawSubject,
        common: trimCell_(row[6]),
        selected: trimCell_(row[7]),
        total: total,
        percentile: trimCell_(row[10]),
        grade: trimCell_(row[11])
      });
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '수학') {
      const rawSubject = canonicalSubjectName_(row[12]);
      if (!isSameSubjectName_(rawSubject, subject)) continue;
      const total = trimCell_(row[15]);
      if (!total) continue;
      rows.push({
        studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
        subject: rawSubject,
        common: trimCell_(row[13]),
        selected: trimCell_(row[14]),
        total: total,
        percentile: trimCell_(row[17]),
        grade: trimCell_(row[18])
      });
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '영어') {
      const total = trimCell_(row[19]);
      if (!total) continue;
      rows.push({
        studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
        subject: '영어',
        total: total,
        percentile: trimCell_(row[21]),
        grade: trimCell_(row[22])
      });
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '탐구') {
      if (subject === '한국사') {
        const total = trimCell_(row[34]);       // AI열 한국사 총점
        if (total) {
          rows.push({
            studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
            subject: '한국사',
            total: total,
            percentile: trimCell_(row[36]),   // AK열 한국사 백분위
            grade: trimCell_(row[37])         // AL열 한국사 등급
          });
        }
        continue;
      }

      const subject1 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[24]);
      const total1 = trimCell_(row[25]);
      if (isSameSubjectName_(subject1, subject) && total1) {
        rows.push({
          studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
          subject: subject1,
          total: total1,
          percentile: trimCell_(row[27]),
          grade: trimCell_(row[28])
        });
      }

      const subject2 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[29]);
      const total2 = trimCell_(row[30]);
      if (isSameSubjectName_(subject2, subject) && total2) {
        rows.push({
          studentNo: studentNo, name: name,
          subject: subject2,
          total: total2,
          percentile: trimCell_(row[32]),
          grade: trimCell_(row[33])
        });
      }
    }
  }

  return rows;
}

function buildSubjectCountTrend_(ss, selectedMonth, subject, group) {
  const months = SUBJECT_MONTHS.filter(month => month <= Number(selectedMonth) && !!ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month)));
  const counts = [];
  const enrollmentsByMonth = {};

  months.forEach(month => {
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    const raw = lastRow >= 3 ? sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 38).getDisplayValues() : [];
    const enrollment = buildSubjectEnrollmentMap_(raw, subject, group);
    enrollmentsByMonth[month] = enrollment;
    counts.push(Object.keys(enrollment).length);
  });

  const lossRows = [];
  if (months.length >= 2) {
    const prevMonth = months[months.length - 2];
    const currentMonth = months[months.length - 1];
    const prevEnrollment = enrollmentsByMonth[prevMonth] || {};
    const currentEnrollment = enrollmentsByMonth[currentMonth] || {};
    const currentRawMap = buildRawRowMapForSubjectMonth_(ss, currentMonth);

    Object.keys(prevEnrollment)
      .filter(studentNo => !currentEnrollment[studentNo])
      .sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko'))
      .forEach(studentNo => {
        const prev = prevEnrollment[studentNo];
        const currentSubject = getCurrentSubjectForPreviousSlot_(currentRawMap[studentNo], group, prev.slot);
        lossRows.push({
          studentNo: studentNo,
          name: prev.name,
          fromSubject: subject,
          toSubject: currentSubject || '미응시',
          text: `${studentNo} ${prev.name} ${subject} → ${currentSubject || '미응시'}`
        });
      });
  }

  return {
    months: months,
    counts: counts,
    display: counts.join('→'),
    lossRows: lossRows
  };
}

function buildSubjectEnrollmentMap_(raw, subject, group) {
  const map = {};
  if (!raw || raw.length < 3) return map;

  for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
    const row = raw[i];
    if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;

    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    const name = trimCell_(row[4]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number || !name) continue;

    const studentNo = makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);

    if (group === '국어') {
      if (isSameSubjectName_(row[5], subject) && trimCell_(row[8])) {
        map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'korean' };
      }
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '수학') {
      if (isSameSubjectName_(row[12], subject) && trimCell_(row[15])) {
        map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'math' };
      }
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '영어') {
      if (subject === '영어' && trimCell_(row[19])) {
        map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'english' };
      }
      continue;
    }

    if (group === '탐구') {
      if (subject === '한국사') {
        if (trimCell_(row[34])) map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'history' };
        continue;
      }

      if (isSameSubjectName_(row[24], subject) && trimCell_(row[25])) {
        map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'inq1' };
      }
      if (isSameSubjectName_(row[29], subject) && trimCell_(row[30])) {
        map[studentNo] = { studentNo, name, slot: 'inq2' };
      }
    }
  }

  return map;
}

function buildRawRowMapForSubjectMonth_(ss, month) {
  const result = {};
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
  if (!sheet) return result;

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 3) return result;

  const raw = sheet.getRange(1, 1, lastRow, 38).getDisplayValues();
  for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
    const row = raw[i];
    if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;
    const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
    const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
    const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
    if (!year || !classNum || !number) continue;
    result[makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number)] = row;
  }
  return result;
}

function getCurrentSubjectForPreviousSlot_(row, group, slot) {
  if (!row) return '미응시';

  if (group === '국어') return canonicalSubjectName_(row[5]) || '미응시';
  if (group === '수학') return canonicalSubjectName_(row[12]) || '미응시';
  if (group === '영어') return trimCell_(row[19]) ? '영어' : '미응시';

  if (group === '탐구') {
    if (slot === 'history') return trimCell_(row[34]) ? '한국사' : '미응시';
    if (slot === 'inq1') return canonicalSubjectName_(row[24]) || '미응시';
    if (slot === 'inq2') return canonicalSubjectName_(row[29]) || '미응시';
  }

  return '미응시';
}

function compareSubjectRows_(a, b) {
  const totalA = toSortNumber_(a.total);
  const totalB = toSortNumber_(b.total);
  if (totalA !== totalB) return totalB - totalA;

  const pctA = toSortNumber_(a.percentile);
  const pctB = toSortNumber_(b.percentile);
  if (pctA !== pctB) return pctB - pctA;

  return String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko');
}

function compareSubjectRowsForMulti_(a, b) {
  const pctA = toSortNumber_(a.percentile);
  const pctB = toSortNumber_(b.percentile);
  if (pctA !== pctB) return pctB - pctA;

  const subjectCompare = String(a.subject || '').localeCompare(String(b.subject || ''), 'ko');
  if (subjectCompare !== 0) return subjectCompare;

  return String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko');
}


/***********************
 * 월별표 전체 재구성
 * - 내신석차연명부 전체 학생을 모든 월별표에 포함
 * - 해당 월 미응시자는 과목·점수·등급 '-' / 3개합·2개합 99
 ***********************/
function repairAllMonthlyTablesWithAllMasterStudents_() {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);

  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    ensureBaseSheets_(ss);

    const studentMap = buildStudentMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName));
    const abbrMap = buildAbbrMap_(ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.abbrSheetName));
    const months = SUBJECT_MONTHS.filter(month => !!ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month)));

    let mergedRows = [];

    months.forEach(month => {
      const rawSheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
      const rawValues = rectangularize_(rawSheet.getDataRange().getDisplayValues());
      const tableRows = buildMonthlyTableRows_(rawValues, month, studentMap, abbrMap);

      const tableSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getTableSheetName_(month));
      writeTableSheet_(tableSheet, tableRows);
      sortMonthlyTable_(tableSheet);
      formatScoreLikeSheet_(tableSheet);

      for (let classNum = 1; classNum <= 8; classNum++) {
        const classSheet = createFreshSheet_(ss, getClassSheetName_(month, classNum));
        writeClassSheet_(classSheet, month, classNum);
        SpreadsheetApp.flush();
        formatScoreLikeSheet_(classSheet);
      }

      mergedRows = mergedRows.concat(tableRows);
    });

    const upper = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
    rewriteUpperData_(upper, mergedRows);
    updateMonthlyVisibility_(ss, months.length ? Math.max.apply(null, months) : null);
    finalizeBaseSheets_(ss);
    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();

    return 'OK';
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

/***********************
 * 빠른 조회용 캐시
 ***********************/
const RUNTIME_CACHE_VERSION_KEY = 'RUNTIME_CACHE_VERSION';

function getRuntimeCacheVersion_() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  let version = props.getProperty(RUNTIME_CACHE_VERSION_KEY);
  if (!version) {
    version = String(new Date().getTime());
    props.setProperty(RUNTIME_CACHE_VERSION_KEY, version);
  }
  return version;
}

function bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_() {
  try {
    PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties().setProperty(
      RUNTIME_CACHE_VERSION_KEY,
      String(new Date().getTime())
    );
  } catch (e) {}
}

function makeRuntimeCacheKey_(key) {
  const raw = 'v' + getRuntimeCacheVersion_() + '_' + String(key || '');
  // Apps Script CacheService key length limit 대응
  return raw.length <= 240 ? raw : raw.substring(0, 240);
}

function getCachedJson_(key) {
  try {
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const runtimeKey = makeRuntimeCacheKey_(key);
    const cached = cache.get(runtimeKey);
    if (cached) return JSON.parse(cached);

    const metaText = cache.get(runtimeKey + '_meta');
    if (!metaText) return null;

    const meta = JSON.parse(metaText);
    const count = Number(meta.count || 0);
    if (!count) return null;

    const chunkKeys = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) chunkKeys.push(runtimeKey + '_c' + i);
    const chunks = cache.getAll(chunkKeys);
    let joined = '';
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      const part = chunks[runtimeKey + '_c' + i];
      if (part == null) return null;
      joined += part;
    }
    return JSON.parse(joined);
  } catch (e) {
    return null;
  }
}

function putCachedJson_(key, value, seconds) {
  try {
    const ttl = seconds || 300;
    const text = JSON.stringify(value);
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    const runtimeKey = makeRuntimeCacheKey_(key);

    // CacheService 단일 값 제한에 맞으면 그대로 저장
    if (text.length <= 90000) {
      cache.put(runtimeKey, text, ttl);
      return;
    }

    // 큰 데이터는 조각 캐시로 저장. 대학지원/정보/명렬표처럼 큰 조회의 반복 로딩 속도를 높임.
    const chunkSize = 80000;
    const count = Math.ceil(text.length / chunkSize);
    if (count > 20) return; // 너무 큰 데이터는 캐시하지 않음

    const items = {};
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      items[runtimeKey + '_c' + i] = text.substring(i * chunkSize, (i + 1) * chunkSize);
    }
    cache.putAll(items, ttl);
    cache.put(runtimeKey + '_meta', JSON.stringify({ count: count }), ttl);
  } catch (e) {}
}

function repairAll() {
  return repairAllMonthlyTablesWithAllMasterStudents_();
}

function applyGradeFontStyle_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  // G, J, L, O, R열: 국등급, 수등급, 영등급, 탐1등급, 탐2등급
  const gradeCols = [7, 10, 12, 15, 18];

  gradeCols.forEach(col => {
    sheet
      .getRange(2, col, lastRow - 1, 1)
      .setFontSize(13)
      .setFontWeight('bold');
  });
}

function applyGradeFontStyleToAllScoreSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const tableRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const classRegex = /^[1-8]반\((\d+)월\)$/;

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();

    if (
      name === CONFIG.upperSheetName ||
      tableRegex.test(name) ||
      classRegex.test(name)
    ) {
      applyGradeFontStyle_(sheet);
    }
  });

  return 'OK';
}

function applyGradeColorStyle_(sheet) {
  if (!sheet) return;

  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;

  // G, J, L, O, R열: 국등급, 수등급, 영등급, 탐1등급, 탐2등급
  const gradeCols = [7, 10, 12, 15, 18];

  gradeCols.forEach(col => {
    const range = sheet.getRange(2, col, lastRow - 1, 1);
    const values = range.getDisplayValues();

    const fontColors = values.map(row => {
      const value = String(row[0] || '').trim();
      return [(value === '1' || value === '2') ? '#ff0000' : '#000000'];
    });

    range
      .setFontColors(fontColors)
      .setFontSize(13)
      .setFontWeight('bold');
  });
}

function applyGradeColorStyleToAllScoreSheets_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();

  const tableRegex = /^\((\d+)월\)모의고사표$/;
  const classRegex = /^[1-8]반\((\d+)월\)$/;

  ss.getSheets().forEach(sheet => {
    const name = sheet.getName();

    if (
      name === CONFIG.upperSheetName ||
      tableRegex.test(name) ||
      classRegex.test(name)
    ) {
      applyGradeColorStyle_(sheet);
    }
  });

  return 'OK';
}
function fixUpperColorsNow() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();

  const sheetName = CONFIG.upperSheetName || '학생별 누적표';

  let sheet = null;
  const sheets = ss.getSheets();

  for (let i = 0; i < sheets.length; i++) {
    if (sheets[i].getName() === sheetName) {
      sheet = sheets[i];
      break;
    }
  }

  if (!sheet) {
    throw new Error(sheetName + ' 탭을 찾지 못했습니다.');
  }

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), CONFIG.tableHeaders.length);

  if (lastRow < 2) {
    return '학생별 누적표에 데이터가 없습니다.';
  }

  const numRows = lastRow - 1;
  const numCols = CONFIG.tableHeaders.length;

  const range = sheet.getRange(2, 1, numRows, numCols);
  const values = range.getDisplayValues();

  // 월 목록: 최근 월부터 정렬
  const months = [...new Set(
    values
      .map(row => Number(row[0]))
      .filter(v => !isNaN(v))
  )].sort((a, b) => b - a);

  const monthColorMap = {};
  months.forEach((month, index) => {
    if (index === 0) {
      monthColorMap[month] = '#0000ff'; // 최근 월: 파란색
    } else if (index === 1) {
      monthColorMap[month] = '#7030a0'; // 두 번째: 보라색
    } else if (index === 2) {
      monthColorMap[month] = '#00b050'; // 세 번째: 초록색
    } else {
      monthColorMap[month] = '#000000'; // 네 번째부터: 검은색
    }
  });

  const fontColors = values.map(row => {
    const month = Number(row[0]);
    const rowColor = monthColorMap[month] || '#000000';
    return new Array(numCols).fill(rowColor);
  });

  range.setFontColors(fontColors);

  // 등급 열은 항상 13포인트, 굵게, 1·2등급 빨간색
  const gradeCols = [7, 10, 12, 15, 18]; // G, J, L, O, R

  gradeCols.forEach(col => {
    const gradeRange = sheet.getRange(2, col, numRows, 1);
    const gradeValues = gradeRange.getDisplayValues();

    const gradeColors = gradeValues.map(row => {
      const v = String(row[0] || '').trim();
      return [(v === '1' || v === '2') ? '#ff0000' : '#000000'];
    });

    gradeRange
      .setFontSize(13)
      .setFontWeight('bold')
      .setFontColors(gradeColors);
  });

  return 'OK';
}

  return fixUpperColorsNow();
