/***********************
 * 상담 기록 기능
 ***********************/
const COUNSEL_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '상담',
  // 선생님이 만든 헤드 구조를 그대로 사용합니다.
  // 앱 내부 수정/삭제를 위해 삭제여부만 H열에 추가합니다.
  headers: ['상담ID', '입력일시', '학번', '이름', '상담일자', '상담항목', '상담내용', '삭제여부'],
  categories: ['전공', '대학', '정시', '생활', '선도', '기타']
};

function ensureCounselSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(COUNSEL_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(COUNSEL_CONFIG.sheetName);

  const lastCol = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.length);
  const current = sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues()[0];
  const isNewHeader = COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.some((h, i) => String(current[i] || '').trim() !== h);

  if (isNewHeader) {
    // 기존에 선생님이 만든 상담ID | 입력일시 | 학번 | 이름 | 상담일자 | 상담항목 | 상담내용 구조를 우선 맞춥니다.
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers]);
  }

  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.length)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  safeHideSheet_(ss, sheet);
  return sheet;
}

function getStudentNameForCounsel_(ss, studentNo) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.upperSheetName);
  if (sheet && sheet.getLastRow() >= 2) {
    const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getDisplayValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
      if (String(values[i][1] || '').trim() === String(studentNo)) return String(values[i][2] || '').trim();
    }
  }
  const master = ss.getSheetByName(CONFIG.masterSheetName);
  if (master) {
    const map = buildStudentMap_(master);
    const found = Object.values(map).find(s => String(s.studentNo) === String(studentNo));
    if (found) return found.name;
  }
  return '';
}

function makeCounselId_() {
  return 'C' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMddHHmmssSSS') + '_' + Math.floor(Math.random() * 100000);
}

function mobileGetCounseling(studentNo) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const no = String(studentNo || '').trim();
  if (!no) throw new Error('학번 정보가 없습니다.');

  const sheet = ensureCounselSheet_();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const name = getStudentNameForCounsel_(ss, no);
  const today = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd');

  if (lastRow < 2) {
    return { studentNo: no, name: name, today: today, records: [] };
  }

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  const records = [];
  values.forEach((row, idx) => {
    const rowNo = String(row[2] || '').trim();        // C 학번
    const deleted = String(row[7] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === 'TRUE'; // H 삭제여부
    if (rowNo !== no || deleted) return;
    records.push({
      rowIndex: idx + 2,
      counselId: String(row[0] || '').trim(),
      createdAt: String(row[1] || '').trim(),
      studentNo: rowNo,
      name: String(row[3] || '').trim(),
      date: String(row[4] || '').trim(),
      category: String(row[5] || '').trim(),
      content: String(row[6] || '').trim()
    });
  });

  records.sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.date !== b.date) return String(b.date).localeCompare(String(a.date));
    return String(b.createdAt).localeCompare(String(a.createdAt));
  });

  return { studentNo: no, name: name, today: today, records: records };
}

function mobileSaveCounseling(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ensureCounselSheet_();
    const no = String(payload && payload.studentNo || '').trim();
    const date = String(payload && payload.date || '').trim();
    const entries = Array.isArray(payload && payload.entries) ? payload.entries : [];
    if (!no) throw new Error('학번 정보가 없습니다.');
    if (!date) throw new Error('상담일자를 선택해 주세요.');

    const name = getStudentNameForCounsel_(ss, no);
    const now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
    const rows = [];
    entries.forEach(item => {
      const category = String(item && item.category || '').trim();
      const content = String(item && item.content || '').trim();
      if (!category || !content) return;
      rows.push([makeCounselId_(), now, no, name, date, category, content, '']);
    });
    if (rows.length === 0) throw new Error('저장할 상담 내용을 입력해 주세요.');
    sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, rows.length, COUNSEL_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues(rows);
    return mobileGetCounseling(no);
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function mobileUpdateCounseling(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const sheet = ensureCounselSheet_();
    const rowIndex = Number(payload && payload.rowIndex);
    const no = String(payload && payload.studentNo || '').trim();
    const date = String(payload && payload.date || '').trim();
    const category = String(payload && payload.category || '').trim();
    const content = String(payload && payload.content || '').trim();
    if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2) throw new Error('수정할 상담 기록을 찾지 못했습니다.');
    if (!date || !category || !content) throw new Error('상담일자, 항목, 내용을 모두 입력해 주세요.');
    // E 상담일자, F 상담항목, G 상담내용
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 5, 1, 3).setValues([[date, category, content]]);
    return mobileGetCounseling(no);
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function mobileDeleteCounseling(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const sheet = ensureCounselSheet_();
    const rowIndex = Number(payload && payload.rowIndex);
    const no = String(payload && payload.studentNo || '').trim();
    if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2) throw new Error('삭제할 상담 기록을 찾지 못했습니다.');
    // H 삭제여부
    sheet.getRange(rowIndex, 8).setValue('TRUE');
    return mobileGetCounseling(no);
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function setupNewFeatureSheets() {
  ensureCounselSheet_();
  ensureCollegePdfSheet_();
  hideStaticSheets_(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet());
  return 'OK';
}

/***********************
 * 대학 정보 파일(PDF/이미지) 업로드/보기
 ***********************/
const COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '대학정보',
  folderName: '대학정보_파일',
  folderIdPropertyKey: 'COLLEGE_PDF_FOLDER_ID',
  headers: ['파일ID', '파일명', '업로드일시', '파일유형', 'MIME유형']
};

function showCollegePdfUploadDialog() {
  const html = HtmlService.createHtmlOutputFromFile('CollegePdfUploadDialog')
    .setWidth(520)
    .setHeight(380);
  SpreadsheetApp.getUi().showModalDialog(html, '대학 정보 업로드');
}

function ensureCollegePdfSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.sheetName);

  // 기존 3열 구조도 새 구조에 맞춰 자동 확장한다.
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.headers]);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.headers.length)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center');
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  safeHideSheet_(ss, sheet);
  return sheet;
}

function getOrCreateCollegePdfFolder_() {
  const props = PropertiesService.getDocumentProperties();
  const savedId = props.getProperty(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.folderIdPropertyKey);
  if (savedId) {
    try { return DriveApp.getFolderById(savedId); } catch (e) {}
  }
  const ssFile = DriveApp.getFileById(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getId());
  const parent = ssFile.getParents().hasNext() ? ssFile.getParents().next() : DriveApp.getRootFolder();
  const folder = parent.createFolder(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.folderName);
  props.setProperty(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.folderIdPropertyKey, folder.getId());
  return folder;
}

function processCollegePdfUpload(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    if (!payload || !payload.base64 || !payload.fileName) {
      throw new Error('업로드 파일 정보가 올바르지 않습니다.');
    }

    const fileName = String(payload.fileName || '').trim();
    const lowerName = fileName.toLowerCase();
    const isPdf = lowerName.endsWith('.pdf');
    const isImage = /\.(jpg|jpeg|png|webp|gif)$/.test(lowerName);

    if (!isPdf && !isImage) {
      throw new Error('PDF 또는 이미지 파일만 업로드할 수 있습니다.');
    }

    const sheet = ensureCollegePdfSheet_();
    const folder = getOrCreateCollegePdfFolder_();

    const bytes = Utilities.base64Decode(payload.base64);
    const mimeType = getCollegeInfoMimeType_(fileName, payload.mimeType);
    const fileType = isPdf ? 'PDF' : 'IMAGE';
    const blob = Utilities.newBlob(bytes, mimeType, fileName);
    const file = folder.createFile(blob).setName(fileName);
    file.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);

    const uploadedAt = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
    const nextRow = Math.max(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 2);

    // 대학 정보 파일은 기존 파일을 지우지 않고 누적 저장한다.
    sheet.getRange(nextRow, 1, 1, COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.headers.length)
      .setValues([[file.getId(), fileName, uploadedAt, fileType, mimeType]]);
    safeHideSheet_(SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), sheet);

    bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
    return { status: 'SUCCESS', fileId: file.getId(), fileName: fileName, fileType: fileType };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function getCollegeInfoMimeType_(fileName, uploadedMimeType) {
  const lowerName = String(fileName || '').toLowerCase();
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.pdf')) return MimeType.PDF;
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.jpg') || lowerName.endsWith('.jpeg')) return 'image/jpeg';
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.png')) return 'image/png';
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.webp')) return 'image/webp';
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.gif')) return 'image/gif';
  return uploadedMimeType || MimeType.BINARY;
}

function inferCollegeInfoFileType_(fileName, savedFileType) {
  const explicit = String(savedFileType || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (explicit === 'PDF' || explicit === 'IMAGE') return explicit;

  const lowerName = String(fileName || '').toLowerCase();
  if (lowerName.endsWith('.pdf')) return 'PDF';
  if (/\.(jpg|jpeg|png|webp|gif)$/.test(lowerName)) return 'IMAGE';
  return 'PDF';
}

function mobileGetCollegePdfInfo() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return { exists: false, files: [] };

  const numCols = Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), COLLEGE_PDF_CONFIG.headers.length);
  const values = sheet
    .getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, numCols)
    .getDisplayValues();

  // 중요: 사용자가 업로드한 순서 그대로 보여주기 위해 시트 행 순서를 유지한다.
  // 이미지 미리보기는 Drive의 uc 링크가 깨지는 경우가 있어 thumbnail 링크를 사용한다.
  const files = values
    .map((row, index) => {
      const fileId = String(row[0] || '').trim();
      if (!fileId) return null;

      const fileName = String(row[1] || '').trim() || '대학 정보 파일';
      const uploadedAt = String(row[2] || '').trim();
      const fileType = inferCollegeInfoFileType_(fileName, row[3]);

      return {
        rowIndex: index + 2,
        fileId: fileId,
        fileName: fileName,
        uploadedAt: uploadedAt,
        fileType: fileType,
        mimeType: String(row[4] || '').trim(),
        previewUrl: fileType === 'IMAGE'
          ? 'https://drive.google.com/thumbnail?id=' + fileId + '&sz=w2000'
          : 'https://drive.google.com/file/d/' + fileId + '/preview',
        openUrl: 'https://drive.google.com/file/d/' + fileId + '/view?usp=sharing'
      };
    })
    .filter(item => item !== null);

  if (!files.length) return { exists: false, files: [] };

  // 기존 화면 코드와의 호환을 위해 첫 번째 업로드 파일 정보도 최상위에 함께 내려준다.
  return Object.assign({ exists: true, files: files }, files[0]);
}




/** =========================
 * 수시 지원 현황: 대학지원 탭 직접 붙여넣기 방식
 * - 대학지원 A:AB 기준
 * - 17752 조회 / 9810138 조회+수정
 * ========================= */
const COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '대학지원',
  memoSheetName: '대학지원메모',
  editPassword: '9810138',
  headers: ['학번', '이름', '내신', '지역', '대학명', '유형', '전형명', '모집단위', '1단계', '면접', '최종', '최저', '1차', '2차', '예비'],
  col: {
    grade: 1, classNum: 2, number: 3, name: 4, naesin: 5, region: 6,
    university: 7, admissionType: 8, detailType: 9, major: 11,
    step1Date: 15, interviewDate: 16, finalDate: 17, minimum: 18,
    result1: 19, result2: 20, rejectReason: 21, reserve: 22
  }
};

function mobileGetCollegeApplyInitData() {
  const cached = getCachedJson_('collegeApplyInitData_fast');
  if (cached) return cached;

  const rows = getCollegeApplyRows_();
  const regionSet = {};
  const universityMap = {};

  rows.forEach(item => {
    if (item.region) regionSet[item.region] = true;
    if (item.rawUniversity) {
      universityMap[item.rawUniversity] = {
        raw: item.rawUniversity,
        display: item.rawUniversity,
        shortName: item.university || item.rawUniversity
      };
    }
  });

  const universities = Object.values(universityMap)
    .sort((a, b) => a.display.localeCompare(b.display, 'ko'));

  const result = {
    regions: Object.keys(regionSet).sort((a, b) => a.localeCompare(b, 'ko')),
    universities: universities,
    count: rows.length
  };

  putCachedJson_('collegeApplyInitData_fast', result, 600);
  return result;
}

function mobileGetCollegeApplyUniversityMatches(query) {
  const terms = splitCollegeApplyTerms_(query);
  if (!terms.length) return { needsSelection: false, groups: [] };

  const rows = getCollegeApplyRows_();
  const groups = terms.map(term => {
    const normTerm = normalizeSearchText_(term);
    const map = {};
    rows.forEach(row => {
      const raw = row.rawUniversity || '';
      if (!raw) return;
      const display = row.university || raw;
      const searchText = normalizeSearchText_(raw + ' ' + display);
      if (!searchText.includes(normTerm)) return;
      if (!map[raw]) map[raw] = { raw: raw, display: display };
    });
    const options = Object.values(map).sort((a, b) => a.display.localeCompare(b.display, 'ko'));
    return { term: term, options: options };
  });

  return {
    needsSelection: groups.some(g => g.options.length > 1),
    groups: groups
  };
}

function mobileSearchCollegeApply(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const filters = {
    studentNo: String(payload.studentNo || '').trim(),
    name: String(payload.name || '').trim(),
    region: String(payload.region || '').trim(),
    universityQuery: String(payload.universityQuery || '').trim(),
    selectedUniversities: Array.isArray(payload.selectedUniversities) ? payload.selectedUniversities.map(String) : [],
    admissionType: String(payload.admissionType || '').trim(),
    detailType: String(payload.detailType || '').trim(),
    major: String(payload.major || '').trim(),
    topInterview: payload.topInterview === true,
    topNaesin: payload.topNaesin === true,
    medical: payload.medical === true,
    sortMode: String(payload.sortMode || '').trim()
  };

  const cacheKey = 'collegeApplySearch_' + JSON.stringify(filters);
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) {
    cached.canEdit = payload.canEdit === true;
    return cached;
  }

  const rows = getCollegeApplyRows_();
  let result = rows.filter(row => matchesCollegeApplyFilters_(row, filters));
  sortCollegeApplyRows_(result, filters.sortMode, filters.topInterview, filters.topNaesin, filters.medical);

  const response = {
    headers: COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.headers,
    count: result.length,
    canEdit: payload.canEdit === true,
    rows: result.map(row => ({
      rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
      studentNo: row.studentNo,
      classNum: row.classNum,
      name: row.name,
      naesin: row.naesinText,
      region: row.region,
      university: row.university,
      admissionType: row.admissionType,
      detailType: row.detailType,
      major: row.major,
      step1Date: row.step1DateText,
      interviewDate: row.interviewDateText,
      finalDate: row.finalDateText,
      minimumMark: row.minimum ? 'O' : '',
      minimumText: row.minimum,
      result1: row.result1,
      result2: row.result2,
      reserve: row.reserve
    }))
  };

  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, response, 300);
  return response;
}


function mobileGetCollegeApplyUniversityStats() {
  const cached = getCachedJson_('collegeApplyUniversityStats_fast');
  if (cached) return cached;

  const rows = getCollegeApplyRows_();
  const targets = getCollegeApplyTopUniversityTargets_();
  const result = targets.map(target => {
    const matched = rows.filter(row => matchesCollegeApplyTopUniversity_(row, target));
    matched.sort((a, b) => {
      const na = a.naesin === null ? 999 : a.naesin;
      const nb = b.naesin === null ? 999 : b.naesin;
      if (na !== nb) return na - nb;
      return String(a.studentNo || '').localeCompare(String(b.studentNo || ''), 'ko');
    });
    return {
      key: target.key,
      label: target.label,
      count: matched.length,
      rows: matched.map(row => ({
        rowIndex: row.rowIndex,
        studentNo: row.studentNo,
        name: row.name,
        naesin: row.naesinText,
        detailType: row.detailType,
        major: row.major,
        step1Date: row.step1DateText,
        interviewDate: row.interviewDateText,
        finalDate: row.finalDateText,
        minimumMark: row.minimum ? 'O' : '',
        minimumText: row.minimum,
        result1: row.result1,
        result2: row.result2,
        reserve: row.reserve
      }))
    };
  });
  const response = { universities: result };
  putCachedJson_('collegeApplyUniversityStats_fast', response, 300);
  return response;
}

function getCollegeApplyTopUniversityTargets_() {
  return [
    { key: 'seoul', label: '서울대', patterns: ['서울대학교'] },
    { key: 'yonsei', label: '연세대', patterns: ['연세대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'korea', label: '고려대', patterns: ['고려대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'kaist', label: '카이스트', patterns: ['한국과학기술원', 'KAIST', '카이스트'] },
    { key: 'postech', label: '포스텍', patterns: ['포항공과대학교', 'POSTECH', '포스텍'] },
    { key: 'sogang', label: '서강대', patterns: ['서강대학교'] },
    { key: 'skku', label: '성균관대', patterns: ['성균관대학교'] },
    { key: 'hanyang', label: '한양대', patterns: ['한양대학교'] },
    { key: 'cau', label: '중앙대', patterns: ['중앙대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'khu', label: '경희대', patterns: ['경희대학교'] },
    { key: 'hufs', label: '한국외대', patterns: ['한국외국어대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'uos', label: '시립대', patterns: ['서울시립대학교'] },
    { key: 'ewha', label: '이화여대', patterns: ['이화여자대학교'] },
    { key: 'konkuk', label: '건국대', patterns: ['건국대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'dongguk', label: '동국대', patterns: ['동국대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울', '고양'] },
    { key: 'hongik', label: '홍익대', patterns: ['홍익대학교'], campusInclude: ['서울'] },
    { key: 'sookmyung', label: '숙명여대', patterns: ['숙명여자대학교'] }
  ];
}

function matchesCollegeApplyTopUniversity_(rowOrRawUniversity, target) {
  const row = (rowOrRawUniversity && typeof rowOrRawUniversity === 'object') ? rowOrRawUniversity : null;
  const raw = row ? String(row.rawUniversity || '') : String(rowOrRawUniversity || '');
  const region = row ? String(row.region || '') : '';
  const normalized = raw.replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase();
  const patternMatched = (target.patterns || []).some(p => normalized.indexOf(String(p).replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase()) !== -1);
  if (!patternMatched) return false;
  if (target.campusInclude && target.campusInclude.length) {
    const campusMatched = target.campusInclude.some(c => normalized.indexOf(String(c).replace(/\s+/g, '').toLowerCase()) !== -1);
    const regionMatched = target.campusInclude.some(c => String(region).replace(/\s+/g, '').indexOf(String(c).replace(/\s+/g, '')) !== -1);
    return campusMatched || regionMatched;
  }
  return true;
}

function mobileUpdateCollegeApplyEditable(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  if (String(payload.password || '').trim() !== COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.editPassword) {
    throw new Error('수정 권한이 없습니다.');
  }

  const rowIndex = Number(payload.rowIndex);
  const field = String(payload.field || '').trim();
  const value = String(payload.value == null ? '' : payload.value).trim();

  const colMap = {
    result1: COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.result1,
    result2: COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.result2,
    reserve: COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.reserve
  };

  if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2 || !colMap[field]) {
    throw new Error('수정 대상이 올바르지 않습니다.');
  }

  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) throw new Error('대학지원 탭이 없습니다.');
  sheet.getRange(rowIndex, colMap[field]).setValue(value);
  bumpRuntimeCacheVersion_();
  return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
}

function mobileGetCollegeApplyMemo(rowIndex) {
  rowIndex = Number(rowIndex);
  if (!rowIndex) return { memo: '' };
  const sheet = ensureCollegeApplyMemoSheet_();
  const data = sheet.getLastRow() >= 2 ? sheet.getRange(2, 1, sheet.getLastRow() - 1, 3).getValues() : [];
  for (let i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
    if (Number(data[i][0]) === rowIndex) return { memo: String(data[i][1] || '') };
  }
  return { memo: '' };
}

function mobileSaveCollegeApplyMemo(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  if (String(payload.password || '').trim() !== COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.editPassword) {
    throw new Error('수정 권한이 없습니다.');
  }
  const rowIndex = Number(payload.rowIndex);
  const memo = String(payload.memo == null ? '' : payload.memo);
  if (!rowIndex || rowIndex < 2) throw new Error('메모 대상이 올바르지 않습니다.');

  const sheet = ensureCollegeApplyMemoSheet_();
  const now = Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow >= 2) {
    const keys = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 1).getValues();
    for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      if (Number(keys[i][0]) === rowIndex) {
        sheet.getRange(i + 2, 2, 1, 2).setValues([[memo, now]]);
        return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
      }
    }
  }
  sheet.appendRow([rowIndex, memo, now]);
  return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
}

function ensureCollegeApplyMemoSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.memoSheetName);
  if (!sheet) sheet = ss.insertSheet(COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.memoSheetName);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, 3).setValues([['행번호', '면접메모', '수정일시']]);
  return sheet;
}

function getCollegeApplyRows_() {
  const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet().getSheetByName(COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 2) return [];

  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = Math.max(22, Math.min(Math.max(sheet.getLastColumn(), 22), 22));
  const cacheKey = 'collegeApplyRows_' + lastRow + '_' + lastCol;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol).getValues();
  const displayValues = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, lastCol).getDisplayValues();

  const rows = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const valueRow = values[i];
    const displayRow = displayValues[i];
    if (displayRow.every(v => String(v || '').trim() === '')) continue;

    const grade = extractNumberText_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.grade - 1]);
    const classNum = extractNumberText_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.classNum - 1]);
    const number = extractNumberText_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.number - 1]);
    const studentNo = (grade && classNum && number) ? makeStudentNo_(grade, classNum, number) : '';
    const rawUniversity = trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.university - 1]);
    const rawAdmissionType = trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.admissionType - 1]);
    const rawDetailType = trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.detailType - 1]);

    const row = {
      rowIndex: i + 2,
      studentNo: studentNo,
      classNum: classNum,
      name: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.name - 1]),
      naesin: toNumber_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.naesin - 1]),
      naesinText: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.naesin - 1]),
      region: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.region - 1]),
      rawUniversity: rawUniversity,
      university: shortenCollegeApplyUniversity_(rawUniversity),
      rawAdmissionType: rawAdmissionType,
      admissionType: shortenCollegeApplyAdmissionType_(rawAdmissionType),
      rawDetailType: rawDetailType,
      detailType: shortenCollegeApplyDetailType_(rawDetailType),
      major: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.major - 1]),
      step1DateText: formatCollegeApplyDate_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.step1Date - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.step1Date - 1]),
      interviewDateText: formatCollegeApplyDate_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.interviewDate - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.interviewDate - 1]),
      finalDateText: formatCollegeApplyDate_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.finalDate - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.finalDate - 1]),
      step1DateSort: parseCollegeApplyDateSort_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.step1Date - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.step1Date - 1]),
      interviewDateSort: parseCollegeApplyDateSort_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.interviewDate - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.interviewDate - 1]),
      finalDateSort: parseCollegeApplyDateSort_(valueRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.finalDate - 1], displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.finalDate - 1]),
      minimum: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.minimum - 1]),
      result1: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.result1 - 1]),
      result2: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.result2 - 1]),
      reserve: trimCell_(displayRow[COLLEGE_APPLY_CONFIG.col.reserve - 1])
    };
    rows.push(row);
  }
  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, rows, 600);
  return rows;
}

function matchesCollegeApplyFilters_(row, filters) {
  if (filters.topInterview) {
    if (row.naesin === null || row.naesin > 3.5) return false;
    if (!row.interviewDateSort) return false;
    const today = new Date();
    const start = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth(), today.getDate()).getTime();
    const end = start + 20 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000;
    if (row.interviewDateSort < start || row.interviewDateSort > end) return false;
  }

  if (filters.topNaesin) {
    if (row.naesin === null || row.naesin > 3.5) return false;
  }

  if (filters.medical) {
    const majorText = normalizeSearchText_(row.major || '');
    const targets = ['의예과', '의과대학', '의학과', '치의예과', '약학과', '한의예과', '수의예과'].map(normalizeSearchText_);
    if (!targets.some(t => majorText.indexOf(t) !== -1)) return false;
  }

  if (filters.studentNo) {
    const studentFilter = normalizeSearchText_(filters.studentNo);
    const classMatch = String(filters.studentNo).trim().match(/^(\d{1,2})\s*반$/);
    if (classMatch) {
      if (String(row.classNum) !== String(Number(classMatch[1]))) return false;
    } else if (!normalizeSearchText_(row.studentNo).includes(studentFilter)) {
      return false;
    }
  }
  if (filters.name && !normalizeSearchText_(row.name).includes(normalizeSearchText_(filters.name))) return false;
  if (filters.region && filters.region !== 'ALL' && row.region !== filters.region) return false;
  if (filters.admissionType && filters.admissionType !== '전체' && row.admissionType !== filters.admissionType) return false;
  if (filters.detailType && !normalizeSearchText_(row.detailType + ' ' + row.rawDetailType).includes(normalizeSearchText_(filters.detailType))) return false;
  if (filters.major && !normalizeSearchText_(row.major).includes(normalizeSearchText_(filters.major))) return false;

  if (filters.selectedUniversities && filters.selectedUniversities.length) {
    if (!filters.selectedUniversities.includes(row.rawUniversity)) return false;
  } else if (filters.universityQuery) {
    const terms = splitCollegeApplyTerms_(filters.universityQuery).map(normalizeSearchText_).filter(Boolean);
    if (terms.length) {
      const searchText = normalizeSearchText_(row.rawUniversity + ' ' + row.university);
      if (!terms.some(term => searchText.includes(term))) return false;
    }
  }
  return true;
}

function sortCollegeApplyRows_(rows, sortMode, topInterview, topNaesin, medical) {
  const EMPTY_DATE = 9999999999999;
  const byNaesinStudent = (a, b) => {
    const na = a.naesin === null ? 999 : a.naesin;
    const nb = b.naesin === null ? 999 : b.naesin;
    if (na !== nb) return na - nb;
    return String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko');
  };
  const byUniversity = (a, b) => String(a.rawUniversity || a.university).localeCompare(String(b.rawUniversity || b.university), 'ko');
  const byNaesin = (a, b) => (a.naesin === null ? 999 : a.naesin) - (b.naesin === null ? 999 : b.naesin);
  const byMajor = (a, b) => String(a.major || '').localeCompare(String(b.major || ''), 'ko');
  const byDetail = (a, b) => String(a.rawDetailType || a.detailType || '').localeCompare(String(b.rawDetailType || b.detailType || ''), 'ko');
  const byName = (a, b) => String(a.name || '').localeCompare(String(b.name || ''), 'ko');
  const byInterviewDate = (a, b) => (a.interviewDateSort || EMPTY_DATE) - (b.interviewDateSort || EMPTY_DATE);

  if (topInterview) {
    rows.sort((a, b) => byInterviewDate(a, b) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesinStudent(a, b));
    return;
  }

  if (topNaesin) {
    rows.sort(byNaesinStudent);
    return;
  }

  if (medical) {
    rows.sort((a, b) => byNaesin(a, b) || byName(a, b) || byUniversity(a, b));
    return;
  }

  if (sortMode === 'step1Date') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => (a.step1DateSort || EMPTY_DATE) - (b.step1DateSort || EMPTY_DATE) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesin(a, b));
  } else if (sortMode === 'interviewDate') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => (a.interviewDateSort || EMPTY_DATE) - (b.interviewDateSort || EMPTY_DATE) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesin(a, b));
  } else if (sortMode === 'finalDate') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => (a.finalDateSort || EMPTY_DATE) - (b.finalDateSort || EMPTY_DATE) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesin(a, b));
  } else if (sortMode === 'result1') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => getCollegeApplyResultSortRank_(a.result1) - getCollegeApplyResultSortRank_(b.result1) || byInterviewDate(a, b) || byUniversity(a, b) || byDetail(a, b));
  } else if (sortMode === 'result2') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => getCollegeApplyResultSortRank_(a.result2) - getCollegeApplyResultSortRank_(b.result2) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesin(a, b) || byMajor(a, b));
  } else if (sortMode === 'reserve') {
    rows.sort((a, b) => getLastNumberForSort_(a.reserve) - getLastNumberForSort_(b.reserve) || byUniversity(a, b) || byNaesin(a, b));
  } else {
    rows.sort(byNaesinStudent);
  }
}

function getCollegeApplyResultSortRank_(value) {
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text) return 9;
  if (text.indexOf('불') !== -1) return 2;
  if (text.indexOf('합') !== -1 || text.indexOf('최초') !== -1 || text.indexOf('등록') !== -1) return 1;
  return 8;
}

function splitCollegeApplyTerms_(text) {
  return String(text || '').split(',').map(v => v.trim()).filter(Boolean);
}

function normalizeSearchText_(text) {
  return String(text || '').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '').replace(/[()（）\[\]{}]/g, '');
}

function shortenCollegeApplyUniversity_(name) {
  const original = trimCell_(name);
  if (!original) return '';

  // 대학지원 원자료에는 '가천대 학교(메디컬)'처럼 대학명 내부에 공백이 섞인 경우가 있음.
  // 표시용 축약은 공백을 먼저 제거한 값으로 처리해야 '대학교 → 대' 변환이 안정적으로 적용된다.
  const normalized = original.replace(/\s+/g, '');

  const special = [
    ['한양대학교(ERICA)', '에리카'],
    ['울산과학기술원', '유니스트'],
    ['대구경북과학기술원', '디지스트'],
    ['광주과학기술원', '지스트'],
    ['건국대학교(글로컬)', '건대글로컬'],
    ['동국대학교(WISE)', '동국WISE'],
    ['한국외국어대학교', '한국외대'],
    ['서울시립대학교', '시립대'],
    ['국군간호사관학교', '국간사'],
    ['연세대학교(미래)', '연세미래'],
    ['고려대학교(세종)', '고려세종'],
    ['홍익대학교(세종)', '홍익세종'],
    ['한국예술종합학교', '한예종'],
    ['국립한국교통대학교', '국립교통대'],
    ['국립한국교통대', '국립교통대'],
    ['한국교통대학교', '국립교통대'],
    ['한국교통대', '국립교통대'],
    ['한국에너지공과대학교', '켄택'],
    ['한국에너지공과대', '켄택'],
    ['국립금오공과대학교', '국립금오공대'],
    ['국립금오공과대', '국립금오공대'],
    ['한서대학교-항공학부', '한서대항공'],
    ['한서대-항공학부', '한서대항공'],
    ['한서대학교항공학부', '한서대항공'],
    ['한서대항공학부', '한서대항공'],
    ['중부대학교(고양)-고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양'],
    ['중부대(고양)-고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양'],
    ['중부대학교(고양)고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양'],
    ['중부대학교(금산)-충청캠퍼스', '중부대금산'],
    ['중부대(금산)-충청캠퍼스', '중부대금산'],
    ['중부대학교(금산)충청캠퍼스', '중부대금산'],
    ['중부대학교-고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양캠'],
    ['중부대-고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양캠'],
    ['중부대학교고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양캠'],
    ['중부대고양캠퍼스', '중부대고양캠'],
    ['중부대학교-충청캠퍼스', '중부대충청캠'],
    ['중부대-충청캠퍼스', '중부대충청캠'],
    ['중부대학교충청캠퍼스', '중부대충청캠'],
    ['중부대충청캠퍼스', '중부대충청캠']
  ];
  for (let i = 0; i < special.length; i++) {
    const key = special[i][0].replace(/\s+/g, '');
    if (normalized.indexOf(key) !== -1) return special[i][1];
  }

  let base = normalized.replace(/\([^)]*\)/g, '').trim();
  base = base.replace(/여자/g, '여');
  base = base.replace(/교육대학교/g, '교대');
  base = base.replace(/교육대/g, '교대');
  base = base.replace(/대학교/g, '대');
  return base;
}

function shortenCollegeApplyAdmissionType_(text) {
  const t = trimCell_(text);
  if (t.indexOf('교과') !== -1) return '교과';
  if (t.indexOf('종합') !== -1) return '종합';
  if (t.indexOf('논술') !== -1) return '논술';
  if (t.indexOf('실기') !== -1) return '실기';
  return t;
}

function shortenCollegeApplyDetailType_(text) {
  const t = trimCell_(text);
  if (!t) return '';
  let result = '';
  if (t.indexOf('기회') !== -1) result = '기회';
  else if (t.indexOf('농어촌') !== -1) result = '농';
  else if (t.indexOf('학교장추천') !== -1) result = '학추';
  else if (t.indexOf('논술') !== -1) result = '논술';
  else if (t.indexOf('실기') !== -1) result = '실기';
  else {
    const matches = [...t.matchAll(/\(([^()]*)\)/g)];
    result = matches.length ? matches[matches.length - 1][1] : t;
  }
  return trimCollegeApplyText_(result, 8);
}

function trimCollegeApplyText_(text, maxLen) {
  const value = String(text == null ? '' : text).trim();
  if (!value) return '';
  return Array.from(value).slice(0, maxLen).join('');
}

function formatCollegeApplyDate_(value, display) {
  const time = parseCollegeApplyDateSort_(value, display);
  if (!time) return '';
  return Utilities.formatDate(new Date(time), Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'M/d');
}

function parseCollegeApplyDateSort_(value, display) {
  if (value instanceof Date && !isNaN(value.getTime())) {
    if (isCollegeApplyEmptyDateSentinel_(value.getMonth() + 1, value.getDate())) return 0;
    return new Date(value.getFullYear(), value.getMonth(), value.getDate()).getTime();
  }

  const text = String(display || value || '').trim();
  if (!text) return 0;

  let m = text.match(/(\d{4})\s*[-./년]\s*(\d{1,2})\s*[-./월]\s*(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) {
    if (isCollegeApplyEmptyDateSentinel_(Number(m[2]), Number(m[3]))) return 0;
    return new Date(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]) - 1, Number(m[3])).getTime();
  }

  m = text.match(/(\d{1,2})\s*[-./월]\s*(\d{1,2})/);
  if (m) {
    if (isCollegeApplyEmptyDateSentinel_(Number(m[1]), Number(m[2]))) return 0;
    const y = new Date().getFullYear();
    return new Date(y, Number(m[1]) - 1, Number(m[2])).getTime();
  }

  return 0;
}

function isCollegeApplyEmptyDateSentinel_(month, day) {
  return Number(month) === 12 && Number(day) === 31;
}

function getLastNumberForSort_(text) {
  const matches = String(text || '').match(/\d+/g);
  if (!matches || !matches.length) return 999999;
  return Number(matches[matches.length - 1]);
}

/***********************
 * 반 명렬표 기능
 * - 학생 명단: 학생사진 탭 기준
 * - 전화번호: 정보 탭 J열 연락처 기준
 * - 저장: 저장할 때마다 새 명렬표로 저장
 ***********************/
const CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '명렬표관리',
  headers: ['저장ID', '반', '저장명', '제목1', '제목2', '제목3', '제목4', '학번', '이름', '체크1', '체크2', '체크3', '메모', '저장일시']
};

function ensureClassRosterSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.sheetName);
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers]);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  } else if (sheet.getLastRow() < 1) {
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers]);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  } else {
    // 예전 명렬표관리 탭이 3개 항목 구조였더라도 새 4개 항목 구조로 헤더를 맞춤.
    sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers]);
    sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  }
  try { sheet.hideSheet(); } catch (e) {}
  return sheet;
}

function mobileGetClassRosterBase(classValue) {
  const classNum = String(classValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();
  if (!classNum || classNum === '0') throw new Error('반을 먼저 선택해 주세요.');

  return {
    classValue: classNum,
    students: getClassRosterStudents_(classNum),
    savedList: mobileListClassRosters(classNum)
  };
}

function getClassRosterStudents_(classNum) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const photoSheet = ss.getSheetByName(PHOTO_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!photoSheet) return [];

  const lastRow = photoSheet.getLastRow();
  const lastCol = photoSheet.getLastColumn();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];

  const cacheKey = 'classRosterStudents_' + classNum + '_' + lastRow + '_' + lastCol;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const infoMap = buildInfoMap_(ss);
  const values = photoSheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, PHOTO_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  const byStudent = {};

  values.forEach(row => {
    const studentNo = trimCell_(row[1]); // B 학번
    const rowClass = trimCell_(row[3]);  // D 반
    const name = trimCell_(row[5]);      // F 이름
    if (!studentNo || !name) return;
    if (String(Number(rowClass)) !== String(Number(classNum))) return;
    if (!byStudent[studentNo]) {
      const info = infoMap[studentNo] || {};
      byStudent[studentNo] = {
        studentNo: studentNo,
        name: name,
        phone: trimCell_(info.studentPhone)
      };
    }
  });

  const students = Object.values(byStudent).sort((a, b) => String(a.studentNo).localeCompare(String(b.studentNo), 'ko'));
  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, students, 600);
  return students;
}


function mobileSaveClassRoster(payload) {
  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const classNum = String(payload && payload.classValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();
    if (!classNum) throw new Error('반 정보가 없습니다.');

    const title1 = trimCell_(payload.title1);
    const title2 = trimCell_(payload.title2);
    const title3 = trimCell_(payload.title3);
    const title4 = trimCell_(payload.title4);
    const rows = Array.isArray(payload && payload.rows) ? payload.rows : [];
    if (rows.length === 0) throw new Error('저장할 명렬표 내용이 없습니다.');

    const sheet = ensureClassRosterSheet_();
    const now = new Date();
    const saveId = Utilities.getUuid();
    const titleParts = [title1, title2, title3, title4].filter(v => String(v || '').trim() !== '');
    const saveName = Utilities.formatDate(now, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'MM/dd') + (titleParts.length ? '(' + titleParts.join(' ') + ')' : '');
    const savedAt = Utilities.formatDate(now, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss');

    const appendRows = rows.map(item => [
      saveId,
      classNum,
      saveName,
      title1,
      title2,
      title3,
      title4,
      trimCell_(item.studentNo),
      trimCell_(item.name),
      item.check1 ? 'TRUE' : '',
      item.check2 ? 'TRUE' : '',
      item.check3 ? 'TRUE' : '',
      trimCell_(item.memo),
      savedAt
    ]);

    sheet.getRange(sheet.getLastRow() + 1, 1, appendRows.length, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues(appendRows);
    try { sheet.hideSheet(); } catch (e) {}

    return {
      status: 'SUCCESS',
      saveId: saveId,
      saveName: saveName,
      savedList: mobileListClassRosters(classNum)
    };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function mobileListClassRosters(classValue) {
  const classNum = String(classValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();
  const sheet = ensureClassRosterSheet_();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return [];

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  const map = {};
  values.forEach(row => {
    const saveId = trimCell_(row[0]);
    const rowClass = trimCell_(row[1]);
    if (!saveId || String(Number(rowClass)) !== String(Number(classNum))) return;
    map[saveId] = {
      saveId: saveId,
      classValue: rowClass,
      saveName: trimCell_(row[2]),
      savedAt: trimCell_(row[13]) || trimCell_(row[11])
    };
  });

  return Object.values(map).sort((a, b) => String(b.savedAt).localeCompare(String(a.savedAt), 'ko'));
}

function mobileLoadClassRoster(saveId) {
  const id = String(saveId || '').trim();
  if (!id) throw new Error('불러올 명렬표를 선택해 주세요.');

  const sheet = ensureClassRosterSheet_();
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) throw new Error('저장된 명렬표가 없습니다.');

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CLASS_ROSTER_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  const matched = values.filter(row => trimCell_(row[0]) === id);
  if (matched.length === 0) throw new Error('저장된 명렬표를 찾지 못했습니다.');

  const first = matched[0];
  return {
    saveId: id,
    classValue: trimCell_(first[1]),
    saveName: trimCell_(first[2]),
    title1: trimCell_(first[3]),
    title2: trimCell_(first[4]),
    title3: trimCell_(first[5]),
    title4: trimCell_(first[6]),
    rows: matched.map(row => {
      const isNewSchema = !!trimCell_(row[13]);
      return {
        studentNo: trimCell_(isNewSchema ? row[7] : row[6]),
        name: trimCell_(isNewSchema ? row[8] : row[7]),
        check1: String(isNewSchema ? row[9] : row[8]).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE',
        check2: String(isNewSchema ? row[10] : row[9]).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE',
        check3: isNewSchema ? String(row[11]).toUpperCase() === 'TRUE' : false,
        memo: trimCell_(isNewSchema ? row[12] : row[10])
      };
    })
  };
}

/***********************
 * 명렬표 임시 저장 기능
 * - 저장 버튼과 별개로 현재 화면 상태를 임시 보관
 * - 같은 로그인 키와 반 기준으로 30시간 내 복원
 ***********************/
const CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '명렬표임시저장',
  headers: ['임시키', '반', '제목1', '제목2', '제목3', '제목4', '데이터JSON', '만료시각', '수정시각']
};

function ensureClassRosterDraftSheet_() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.sheetName);
  }
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.headers]);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(1);
  try { sheet.hideSheet(); } catch (e) {}
  return sheet;
}

function cleanupClassRosterDraftSheet_(sheet) {
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return;
  const now = Date.now();
  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  for (let i = values.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    const expiresAt = Number(values[i][7]);
    if (expiresAt && expiresAt <= now) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
    }
  }
}

function normalizeClassRosterDraftKey_(value) {
  return String(value || '17752').trim() || '17752';
}

function mobileSaveClassRosterDraft(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const draftKey = normalizeClassRosterDraftKey_(payload.draftKey);
  const classNum = String(payload.classValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();
  if (!classNum) throw new Error('반 정보가 없습니다.');

  const expiresAt = Number(payload.expiresAt) || (Date.now() + 30 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
  const modifiedAt = Number(payload.modifiedAt) || Date.now();
  const rows = Array.isArray(payload.rows) ? payload.rows : [];
  const dataJson = JSON.stringify({ rows: rows, modifiedAt: modifiedAt });

  const lock = LockService.getDocumentLock();
  lock.waitLock(30000);
  try {
    const sheet = ensureClassRosterDraftSheet_();
    cleanupClassRosterDraftSheet_(sheet);
    const rowValues = [
      draftKey,
      classNum,
      String(payload.title1 || '제목1'),
      String(payload.title2 || '제목2'),
      String(payload.title3 || '제목3'),
      String(payload.title4 || '제목4'),
      dataJson,
      String(expiresAt),
      String(modifiedAt)
    ];

    const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
    if (lastRow >= 2) {
      const keys = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, 2).getDisplayValues();
      for (let i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
        if (trimCell_(keys[i][0]) === draftKey && String(Number(keys[i][1])) === String(Number(classNum))) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 2, 1, 1, CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.headers.length).setValues([rowValues]);
          return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
        }
      }
    }
    sheet.appendRow(rowValues);
    return { status: 'SUCCESS' };
  } finally {
    lock.releaseLock();
  }
}

function mobileLoadClassRosterDraft(payload) {
  payload = payload || {};
  const draftKey = normalizeClassRosterDraftKey_(payload.draftKey);
  const classNum = String(payload.classValue || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '').trim();
  if (!classNum) return null;

  const sheet = ensureClassRosterDraftSheet_();
  cleanupClassRosterDraftSheet_(sheet);
  const lastRow = sheet.getLastRow();
  if (lastRow < 2) return null;

  const values = sheet.getRange(2, 1, lastRow - 1, CLASS_ROSTER_DRAFT_CONFIG.headers.length).getDisplayValues();
  for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) {
    const row = values[i];
    if (trimCell_(row[0]) !== draftKey) continue;
    if (String(Number(row[1])) !== String(Number(classNum))) continue;

    const expiresAt = Number(row[7]);
    if (expiresAt && expiresAt <= Date.now()) {
      sheet.deleteRow(i + 2);
      return null;
    }

    let data = { rows: [], modifiedAt: Number(row[8]) || Date.now() };
    try {
      data = JSON.parse(row[6] || '{}') || data;
    } catch (e) {}

    return {
      classValue: classNum,
      title1: trimCell_(row[2]) || '제목1',
      title2: trimCell_(row[3]) || '제목2',
      title3: trimCell_(row[4]) || '제목3',
      title4: trimCell_(row[5]) || '제목4',
      rows: Array.isArray(data.rows) ? data.rows : [],
      expiresAt: expiresAt,
      modifiedAt: Number(data.modifiedAt || row[8]) || Date.now()
    };
  }
  return null;
}



/************************************************************
 * 교과 상세 분석
 * - 기존 기능과 시트 구조를 건드리지 않고 별도 탭/별도 웹 화면으로만 추가
 * - 내신 기준: 전학년 내신 5.00 이내(1.00~5.00)
 * - 예정 월은 표시하지 않고 실제 원자료 탭이 존재하는 월만 표시
 ************************************************************/
const SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG = {
  sheetName: '교과 상세 분석',
  dropdownCell: 'B2',
  academicYearLabel: '2026학년도',
  naesinMax: 5.00,
  colors: {
    navy: '#0d2a5e',
    blue: '#2563eb',
    paleBlue: '#dbeafe',
    paleYellow: '#fff2cc',
    paleGray: '#f8fafc',
    line: '#cbd5e1',
    text: '#0f172a',
    muted: '#64748b',
    white: '#ffffff'
  }
};

const SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_KOREAN = ['화법과작문', '언어와매체'];
const SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_MATH = ['확률과통계', '미적분', '기하'];
const SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SOCIAL = ['경제', '사회문화', '생활과윤리', '윤리와사상', '정치와법', '세계사', '동아시아사', '한국지리', '세계지리'];
const SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SCIENCE = ['물리학1', '물리학2', '화학1', '화학2', '생명과학1', '생명과학2', '지구과학1', '지구과학2'];

function getSubjectAnalysisSubjectList_() {
  return SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_KOREAN
    .concat(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_MATH)
    .concat(['영어'])
    .concat(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SOCIAL)
    .concat(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SCIENCE);
}

function getSubjectAnalysisGroup_(subject) {
  const normalized = canonicalSubjectName_(subject);
  if (SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_KOREAN.indexOf(normalized) !== -1) return '국어';
  if (SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_MATH.indexOf(normalized) !== -1) return '수학';
  if (normalized === '영어') return '영어';
  if (SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SOCIAL.indexOf(normalized) !== -1 || SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SCIENCE.indexOf(normalized) !== -1) return '탐구';
  return '';
}

function isSubjectAnalysisScience_(subject) {
  return SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SCIENCE.indexOf(canonicalSubjectName_(subject)) !== -1;
}

function isSubjectAnalysisSocial_(subject) {
  return SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_SOCIAL.indexOf(canonicalSubjectName_(subject)) !== -1;
}

function getSubjectAnalysisAvailableMonths_(ss, selectedMonth) {
  const limit = selectedMonth == null || selectedMonth === '' ? 99 : Number(selectedMonth);
  return SUBJECT_MONTHS
    .filter(month => month <= limit && !!ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month)))
    .sort((a, b) => a - b);
}

function getSubjectAnalysisRawRows_(ss, month) {
  const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(getDataSheetName_(month));
  if (!sheet || sheet.getLastRow() < 3) return [];
  return sheet.getRange(1, 1, sheet.getLastRow(), 38).getDisplayValues();
}

function getSubjectAnalysisStudentNo_(row) {
  if (!row) return '';
  const year = trimCell_(row[1]);
  const classNum = trimCell_(row[2]);
  const number = trimCell_(row[3]);
  if (!year || !classNum || !number) return '';
  return makeStudentNo_(year, classNum, number);
}

function isSubjectAnalysisNaesinEligible_(naesinMap, studentNo) {
  const value = toNumber_(naesinMap && studentNo ? naesinMap[studentNo] : '');
  return value !== null && value > 0 && value <= SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.naesinMax;
}

function hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(value) {
  return trimCell_(value) !== '';
}

function getSubjectAnalysisRatio_(count, denominator) {
  if (!denominator) return null;
  return Math.round((Number(count) / Number(denominator)) * 1000) / 10;
}

function formatSubjectAnalysisRatio_(ratio) {
  if (ratio === null || ratio === undefined || isNaN(Number(ratio))) return '-';
  return Number(ratio).toFixed(1) + '%';
}

function makeSubjectAnalysisCountRatioCell_(count, denominator) {
  const ratio = getSubjectAnalysisRatio_(count, denominator);
  return {
    count: Number(count) || 0,
    denominator: Number(denominator) || 0,
    ratio: ratio,
    primary: (Number(count) || 0) + '명',
    secondary: formatSubjectAnalysisRatio_(ratio),
    text: (Number(count) || 0) + '명 / ' + formatSubjectAnalysisRatio_(ratio)
  };
}

function makeSubjectAnalysisCountCell_(count) {
  return {
    count: Number(count) || 0,
    denominator: 0,
    ratio: null,
    primary: (Number(count) || 0) + '명',
    secondary: '',
    text: (Number(count) || 0) + '명'
  };
}

function makeSubjectAnalysisRatioCell_(count, denominator) {
  const ratio = getSubjectAnalysisRatio_(count, denominator);
  return {
    count: Number(count) || 0,
    denominator: Number(denominator) || 0,
    ratio: ratio,
    primary: formatSubjectAnalysisRatio_(ratio),
    secondary: denominator ? '(' + count + '/' + denominator + '명)' : '',
    text: formatSubjectAnalysisRatio_(ratio) + (denominator ? ' (' + count + '/' + denominator + '명)' : '')
  };
}

function rowHasSubjectAnalysisDomainExam_(row, group) {
  if (group === '국어') return hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[8]);
  if (group === '수학') return hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[15]);
  if (group === '영어') return hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[19]);
  return false;
}

function rowHasSubjectAnalysisSubjectExam_(row, subject, group) {
  subject = canonicalSubjectName_(subject);

  if (group === '국어') {
    return isSameSubjectName_(row[5], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[8]);
  }
  if (group === '수학') {
    return isSameSubjectName_(row[12], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[15]);
  }
  if (group === '영어') {
    return subject === '영어' && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[19]);
  }
  if (group === '탐구') {
    const slot1 = isSameSubjectName_(row[24], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[25]);
    const slot2 = isSameSubjectName_(row[29], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[30]);
    return slot1 || slot2;
  }
  return false;
}

function getSubjectAnalysisGrade_(row, subject, group) {
  subject = canonicalSubjectName_(subject);

  if (group === '국어' && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[8])) return trimCell_(row[11]);
  if (group === '수학' && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[15])) return trimCell_(row[18]);
  if (group === '영어' && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[19])) return trimCell_(row[22]);

  if (group === '탐구') {
    if (isSameSubjectName_(row[24], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[25])) return trimCell_(row[28]);
    if (isSameSubjectName_(row[29], subject) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[30])) return trimCell_(row[33]);
  }
  return '';
}

function rowHasAnySubjectAnalysisInquiry_(row) {
  const subject1 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[24]);
  const subject2 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[29]);
  return (
    ((isSubjectAnalysisSocial_(subject1) || isSubjectAnalysisScience_(subject1)) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[25])) ||
    ((isSubjectAnalysisSocial_(subject2) || isSubjectAnalysisScience_(subject2)) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[30]))
  );
}

function rowHasSubjectAnalysisInquiryArea_(row, area) {
  const subject1 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[24]);
  const subject2 = canonicalSubjectName_(row[29]);
  const checker = area === 'science' ? isSubjectAnalysisScience_ : isSubjectAnalysisSocial_;
  return (
    (checker(subject1) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[25])) ||
    (checker(subject2) && hasSubjectAnalysisValue_(row[30]))
  );
}

function buildSubjectAnalysisChoiceSection_(months, rawByMonth, naesinMap, group) {
  const choices = group === '국어' ? SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_KOREAN : SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_MATH;
  const monthStats = {};

  months.forEach(month => {
    const denominatorMap = {};
    const choiceMaps = {};
    choices.forEach(choice => choiceMaps[choice] = {});

    const raw = rawByMonth[month] || [];
    for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
      const row = raw[i];
      if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;
      const studentNo = getSubjectAnalysisStudentNo_(row);
      if (!studentNo || !isSubjectAnalysisNaesinEligible_(naesinMap, studentNo)) continue;
      if (!rowHasSubjectAnalysisDomainExam_(row, group)) continue;

      denominatorMap[studentNo] = true;
      choices.forEach(choice => {
        if (rowHasSubjectAnalysisSubjectExam_(row, choice, group)) choiceMaps[choice][studentNo] = true;
      });
    }

    monthStats[month] = {
      denominator: Object.keys(denominatorMap).length,
      counts: {}
    };
    choices.forEach(choice => {
      monthStats[month].counts[choice] = Object.keys(choiceMaps[choice]).length;
    });
  });

  return {
    visible: true,
    title: '내신 5.00 이내 선택 현황',
    headers: ['과목'].concat(months.map(month => month + '월')),
    rows: choices.map(choice => ({
      label: choice,
      cells: months.map(month => makeSubjectAnalysisCountRatioCell_(monthStats[month].counts[choice], monthStats[month].denominator))
    })),
    note: '비율은 해당 월 내신 5.00 이내 ' + group + ' 영역 응시자 중 각 선택과목 응시자의 비율입니다.'
  };
}

function buildSubjectAnalysisInquirySection_(months, rawByMonth, naesinMap, subject) {
  const targetArea = isSubjectAnalysisScience_(subject) ? 'science' : 'social';
  const targetAreaLabel = targetArea === 'science' ? '과학탐구' : '사회탐구';
  const stats = {};

  months.forEach(month => {
    const selectedMap = {};
    const areaMap = {};
    const allInquiryMap = {};
    const raw = rawByMonth[month] || [];

    for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
      const row = raw[i];
      if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;
      const studentNo = getSubjectAnalysisStudentNo_(row);
      if (!studentNo || !isSubjectAnalysisNaesinEligible_(naesinMap, studentNo)) continue;

      if (rowHasAnySubjectAnalysisInquiry_(row)) allInquiryMap[studentNo] = true;
      if (rowHasSubjectAnalysisInquiryArea_(row, targetArea)) areaMap[studentNo] = true;
      if (rowHasSubjectAnalysisSubjectExam_(row, subject, '탐구')) selectedMap[studentNo] = true;
    }

    stats[month] = {
      selected: Object.keys(selectedMap).length,
      area: Object.keys(areaMap).length,
      all: Object.keys(allInquiryMap).length
    };
  });

  return {
    visible: true,
    title: '내신 5.00 이내 ' + subject + ' 선택 현황',
    headers: ['구분'].concat(months.map(month => month + '월')),
    rows: [
      {
        label: '선택 인원',
        cells: months.map(month => makeSubjectAnalysisCountCell_(stats[month].selected))
      },
      {
        label: targetAreaLabel + ' 선택자 중 비율',
        cells: months.map(month => makeSubjectAnalysisRatioCell_(stats[month].selected, stats[month].area))
      },
      {
        label: '전체 탐구 선택자 중 비율',
        cells: months.map(month => makeSubjectAnalysisRatioCell_(stats[month].selected, stats[month].all))
      }
    ],
    note: '선택 인원과 비율은 모두 내신 5.00 이내 학생을 대상으로 산출합니다. 사회탐구 비율은 내신 5.00 이내 사회탐구 응시자 수를, 전체 탐구 비율은 내신 5.00 이내 사회·과학탐구 응시자 수를 분모로 계산합니다.'
  };
}

function buildSubjectAnalysisGradeSection_(months, rawByMonth, subject, group) {
  const rows = months.map(month => {
    const raw = rawByMonth[month] || [];
    const examinees = {};
    const gradeMaps = { 1: {}, 2: {}, 3: {}, 4: {} };

    for (let i = 2; i < raw.length; i++) {
      const row = raw[i];
      if (!row || isEffectivelyBlankRow_(row)) continue;
      const studentNo = getSubjectAnalysisStudentNo_(row);
      if (!studentNo) continue;

      const hasExam = group === '탐구'
        ? rowHasSubjectAnalysisSubjectExam_(row, subject, group)
        : rowHasSubjectAnalysisDomainExam_(row, group);
      if (!hasExam) continue;

      examinees[studentNo] = true;
      const grade = Number(getSubjectAnalysisGrade_(row, subject, group));
      if (gradeMaps[grade]) gradeMaps[grade][studentNo] = true;
    }

    const denominator = Object.keys(examinees).length;
    return {
      label: month + '월',
      cells: [1, 2, 3, 4].map(grade => makeSubjectAnalysisCountRatioCell_(Object.keys(gradeMaps[grade]).length, denominator))
    };
  });

  let denominatorText = '';
  if (group === '탐구') denominatorText = '해당 월 ' + subject + ' 응시자';
  else denominatorText = '해당 월 ' + group + ' 영역 전체 응시자';

  return {
    visible: true,
    title: '모의고사 등급 분포 비교',
    headers: ['월', '1등급', '2등급', '3등급', '4등급'],
    rows: rows,
    note: '각 비율의 분모는 ' + denominatorText + '입니다. 이 표는 내신과 관계없이 전체 응시자를 대상으로 계산합니다.'
  };
}

function buildSubjectAnalysisData_(ss, subject, selectedMonth) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  subject = canonicalSubjectName_(subject);

  const allowed = getSubjectAnalysisSubjectList_();
  if (allowed.indexOf(subject) === -1) throw new Error('교과 상세 분석 대상 과목이 아닙니다.');

  const group = getSubjectAnalysisGroup_(subject);
  const months = getSubjectAnalysisAvailableMonths_(ss, selectedMonth);
  if (!months.length) throw new Error('분석할 모의고사 원자료가 없습니다.');

  const latestMonth = months[months.length - 1];
  const rawByMonth = {};
  months.forEach(month => rawByMonth[month] = getSubjectAnalysisRawRows_(ss, month));

  const naesinMap = buildNaesinByStudentNo_(ss);
  let selectionSection = null;
  if (group === '국어' || group === '수학') {
    selectionSection = buildSubjectAnalysisChoiceSection_(months, rawByMonth, naesinMap, group);
  } else if (group === '탐구') {
    selectionSection = buildSubjectAnalysisInquirySection_(months, rawByMonth, naesinMap, subject);
  }

  const gradeSection = buildSubjectAnalysisGradeSection_(months, rawByMonth, subject, group);
  let trend = null;
  let title = latestMonth + '월 ' + subject;

  if (group !== '영어') {
    trend = buildSubjectCountTrend_(ss, latestMonth, subject, group);
    if (trend && trend.display) title += '(' + trend.display + ')';
  }

  return {
    mode: 'subjectAnalysis',
    academicYearLabel: SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.academicYearLabel,
    naesinLabel: '내신 5.00 이내',
    subject: subject,
    subjectGroup: group,
    selectedMonth: latestMonth,
    months: months,
    title: title,
    subjectTrend: trend,
    selectionSection: selectionSection,
    gradeSection: gradeSection
  };
}

function mobileGetSubjectAnalysis(payload) {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const month = normalizeSubjectMonth_(payload && payload.month);
  const subject = canonicalSubjectName_(payload && payload.subject);
  const cacheKey = 'subjectAnalysis_v3_' + month + '_' + subject;
  const cached = getCachedJson_(cacheKey);
  if (cached) return cached;

  const result = buildSubjectAnalysisData_(ss, subject, month);
  putCachedJson_(cacheKey, result, 300);
  return result;
}

function ensureSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  let sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.sheetName);
  if (!sheet) {
    sheet = ss.insertSheet(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.sheetName);
    sheet.setTabColor(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.colors.blue);
  }
  return sheet;
}

function safeEnsureSubjectAnalysisSheetOnOpen_() {
  try {
    const ss = SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
    const sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.sheetName);
    if (!sheet || !trimCell_(sheet.getRange(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.dropdownCell).getDisplayValue())) {
      refreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss);
    }
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('교과 상세 분석 탭 초기화 실패: ' + e);
  }
}

function safeRefreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss, subject) {
  try {
    refreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), subject);
  } catch (e) {
    console.error('교과 상세 분석 탭 갱신 실패: ' + e);
  }
}

function onEdit(e) {
  try {
    if (!e || !e.range) return;
    const sheet = e.range.getSheet();
    if (sheet.getName() !== SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.sheetName) return;
    if (e.range.getA1Notation() !== SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.dropdownCell) return;
    safeRefreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(e.source || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet(), e.value || e.range.getDisplayValue());
  } catch (err) {
    console.error('교과 상세 분석 드롭다운 처리 실패: ' + err);
  }
}

function refreshSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss, requestedSubject) {
  ss = ss || SpreadsheetApp.getActiveSpreadsheet();
  const sheet = ensureSubjectAnalysisSheet_(ss);
  const subjects = getSubjectAnalysisSubjectList_();

  let subject = canonicalSubjectName_(requestedSubject || sheet.getRange(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.dropdownCell).getDisplayValue());
  if (subjects.indexOf(subject) === -1) subject = subjects[0];

  const months = getSubjectAnalysisAvailableMonths_(ss, null);
  const totalCols = Math.max(6, months.length + 1);
  const maxRows = Math.max(sheet.getMaxRows(), 40);
  const maxCols = Math.max(sheet.getMaxColumns(), totalCols);

  const wholeRange = sheet.getRange(1, 1, maxRows, maxCols);
  wholeRange.breakApart();
  wholeRange.clear();
  sheet.setConditionalFormatRules([]);
  sheet.setHiddenGridlines(true);
  sheet.setFrozenRows(5);
  sheet.setTabColor(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.colors.blue);

  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
  sheet.getRange(1, 1).setValue('교과 상세 분석');
  sheet.getRange(2, 1).setValue('교과 선택');
  sheet.getRange(2, 2).setValue(subject);
  sheet.getRange(2, 2).setDataValidation(
    SpreadsheetApp.newDataValidation()
      .requireValueInList(subjects, true)
      .setAllowInvalid(false)
      .build()
  );
  sheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
  sheet.getRange(3, 1).setValue(SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.academicYearLabel + ' · 내신 5.00 이내 기준 · 실제 데이터가 있는 월만 표시');

  const c = SUBJECT_ANALYSIS_CONFIG.colors;
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, 1, totalCols)
    .setBackground(c.navy)
    .setFontColor(c.white)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setFontSize(18)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setRowHeight(1, 42);

  sheet.getRange(2, 1, 1, 2)
    .setBackground(c.paleBlue)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setFontSize(11)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setRowHeight(2, 34);

  sheet.getRange(3, 1, 1, totalCols)
    .setFontColor(c.muted)
    .setFontSize(10)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setRowHeight(3, 26);

  if (!months.length) {
    sheet.getRange(5, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
    sheet.getRange(5, 1).setValue('분석할 모의고사 원자료가 없습니다.');
    sheet.getRange(5, 1).setHorizontalAlignment('center').setFontColor(c.muted).setFontSize(12);
    return;
  }

  const data = buildSubjectAnalysisData_(ss, subject, months[months.length - 1]);
  sheet.getRange(5, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
  sheet.getRange(5, 1).setValue(data.title);
  sheet.getRange(5, 1)
    .setBackground(c.blue)
    .setFontColor(c.white)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setFontSize(15)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setRowHeight(5, 38);

  let nextRow = 7;
  if (data.selectionSection && data.selectionSection.visible) {
    nextRow = writeSubjectAnalysisSectionToSheet_(sheet, nextRow, data.selectionSection, totalCols, c.paleBlue, c);
    nextRow += 2;
  }

  writeSubjectAnalysisSectionToSheet_(sheet, nextRow, data.gradeSection, totalCols, c.paleYellow, c);

  sheet.setColumnWidth(1, 230);
  for (let col = 2; col <= totalCols; col++) sheet.setColumnWidth(col, 125);
  sheet.getRange(1, 1, Math.max(sheet.getLastRow(), 1), totalCols).setFontFamily('Arial');
}

function writeSubjectAnalysisSectionToSheet_(sheet, startRow, section, totalCols, headerColor, colors) {
  const headers = section.headers || [];
  const rows = section.rows || [];
  const usedCols = Math.max(1, headers.length);

  sheet.getRange(startRow, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
  sheet.getRange(startRow, 1).setValue(section.title || '');
  sheet.getRange(startRow, 1)
    .setBackground(colors.navy)
    .setFontColor(colors.white)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setFontSize(12)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('left')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle');
  sheet.setRowHeight(startRow, 32);

  sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, 1, 1, usedCols).setValues([headers]);
  sheet.getRange(startRow + 1, 1, 1, usedCols)
    .setBackground(headerColor)
    .setFontWeight('bold')
    .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, colors.line, SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
  sheet.setRowHeight(startRow + 1, 34);

  if (rows.length) {
    const values = rows.map(row => {
      const cells = [row.label || ''];
      (row.cells || []).forEach(cell => {
        const primary = trimCell_(cell && cell.primary);
        const secondary = trimCell_(cell && cell.secondary);
        cells.push(secondary ? primary + '\n' + secondary : primary);
      });
      while (cells.length < usedCols) cells.push('');
      return cells;
    });

    sheet.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, values.length, usedCols).setValues(values);
    sheet.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, values.length, usedCols)
      .setBackground(colors.white)
      .setHorizontalAlignment('center')
      .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
      .setWrap(true)
      .setBorder(true, true, true, true, true, true, colors.line, SpreadsheetApp.BorderStyle.SOLID);
    sheet.getRange(startRow + 2, 1, values.length, 1).setBackground(colors.paleGray).setFontWeight('bold');
    for (let i = 0; i < values.length; i++) sheet.setRowHeight(startRow + 2 + i, 52);
  }

  const noteRow = startRow + 2 + rows.length;
  sheet.getRange(noteRow, 1, 1, totalCols).merge();
  sheet.getRange(noteRow, 1).setValue('※ ' + (section.note || ''));
  sheet.getRange(noteRow, 1)
    .setFontColor(colors.muted)
    .setFontSize(9)
    .setHorizontalAlignment('left')
    .setVerticalAlignment('middle')
    .setWrap(true);
  sheet.setRowHeight(noteRow, 34);

  return noteRow;
}

    <div class="guide">
      엑셀 원점수 파일 내용을 구글시트의 <b>(월)모의고사 데이터</b> 탭에 먼저 붙여넣은 뒤 실행하세요.<br>
      탭 이름 예: <b>(3월)모의고사 데이터</b><br>
      붙여넣기 위치: <b>A1</b><br>
      원본의 1~2행 헤더와 A~AL열 전체를 그대로 붙여넣어야 합니다.<br>
      처리 완료 후 원자료 탭은 자동으로 숨김 처리됩니다.
    </div>

    <div class="row">
      <label for="month">월 선택</label>
      <select id="month">
        <option value="3">3월</option>
        <option value="5">5월</option>
        <option value="6">6월</option>
        <option value="7">7월</option>
        <option value="9">9월</option>
        <option value="10">10월</option>
        <option value="11">11월</option>
      </select>
    </div>

    <div class="row">
      <button id="runBtn" type="button" onclick="startProcess()">붙여넣기 확인 및 변환</button>
    </div>

    <div id="status" class="status"></div>
    <div id="duplicateArea" class="status warn"></div>

    <script>
      function setStatus(text, isWarn) {
        const el = document.getElementById('status');
        el.textContent = text || '';
        el.className = 'status' + (isWarn ? ' warn' : '');
      }

      function clearDuplicateArea() {
        document.getElementById('duplicateArea').innerHTML = '';
      }

      function startProcess() {
        clearDuplicateArea();
        const month = document.getElementById('month').value;
        const btn = document.getElementById('runBtn');

        setStatus('월별표 존재 여부를 확인 중입니다...');
        btn.disabled = true;

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(exists) {
            if (exists) {
              const ok = confirm('동일 월의 모의고사표가 이미 존재합니다.\n붙여넣은 원자료 기준으로 덮어씌우겠습니까?');
              if (!ok) {
                btn.disabled = false;
                setStatus('처리가 취소되었습니다.', true);
                return;
              }
            }
            runPastedProcess(month, exists);
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            btn.disabled = false;
            setStatus(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err), true);
          })
          .checkMonthExists(month);
      }

      function runPastedProcess(month, overwrite) {
        setStatus('붙여넣은 원자료를 변환하는 중입니다...');

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            document.getElementById('runBtn').disabled = false;
            handleResult(result);
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            document.getElementById('runBtn').disabled = false;
            setStatus(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err), true);
          })
          .processPastedMockData({
            month: month,
            overwrite: overwrite
          });
      }

      function handleResult(result) {
        if (!result) {
          setStatus('처리 결과를 받지 못했습니다.', true);
          return;
        }

        if (result.status === 'SUCCESS') {
          alert('완료되었습니다.');
          google.script.host.close();
          return;
        }

        if (result.status === 'DUPLICATES') {
          setStatus('중복 학생이 발견되어 처리가 취소되었습니다.', true);
          const area = document.getElementById('duplicateArea');
          const items = result.duplicates.map(function(item) {
            return '<li>' + item.studentNo + ' / ' + item.name + '</li>';
          }).join('');
          area.innerHTML = '중복 학생 목록<ul>' + items + '</ul><div style="margin-top:12px;"><button type="button" onclick="google.script.host.close()">닫기</button></div>';
          return;
        }

        if (result.status === 'MONTH_EXISTS') {
          setStatus('동일 월 데이터가 이미 존재합니다. 다시 시도해 주세요.', true);
          return;
        }

        setStatus('처리에 실패했습니다.', true);
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

  <head>
    <base target="_top">
    <style>

  </head>
  <body>
    <div class="row">
      <label for="month">삭제할 월</label>
      <select id="month">
        <option value="3">3월</option>
        <option value="5">5월</option>
        <option value="6">6월</option>
        <option value="7">7월</option>
        <option value="9">9월</option>
        <option value="10">10월</option>
        <option value="11">11월</option>
      </select>
    </div>

    <div class="row">
      <button onclick="removeMonth()">해당 월 데이터 삭제</button>
    </div>

    <div id="status" class="status"></div>

    <script>
      function setStatus(text, isWarn) {
        const el = document.getElementById('status');
        el.textContent = text || '';
        el.className = 'status' + (isWarn ? ' warn' : '');
      }

      function removeMonth() {
        const month = document.getElementById('month').value;
        const ok = confirm(month + '월 데이터를 삭제하시겠습니까?\n(월)모의고사 데이터 원자료 탭, 월별표, 반별표, 학생별 누적표의 해당 월 데이터가 함께 삭제됩니다.');
        if (!ok) return;

        setStatus('삭제 중입니다.');
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            if (result.status === 'DELETED') {
              alert('완료되었습니다.');
              google.script.host.close();
            } else if (result.status === 'NOT_FOUND') {
              setStatus(result.month + '월 데이터가 존재하지 않습니다.', true);
            } else {
              setStatus('삭제에 실패했습니다.', true);
            }
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            setStatus(err.message || String(err), true);
          })
          .deleteMonthData(month);
      }
    </script>
  </body>
</html>

      function setBackButton() {
        const btn = document.getElementById('backBtn');
        btn.disabled = appHistory.length <= 1;
      }

      function setModeSwitchButton(sectionName) {
        const btn = document.getElementById('modeSwitchBtn');
        if (!btn) return;

        const show =
          isLoggedIn &&
          (sectionName === 'search' || sectionName === 'subject' || sectionName === 'result');

        if (!show) {
          btn.style.display = 'none';
          return;
        }

        btn.style.display = '';
        btn.textContent = currentMode === 'subject' ? '담임용으로 전환' : '교과용으로 전환';
      }

      function showSection(sectionName, pushHistory = true) {
        document.body.classList.toggle('login-active', sectionName === 'login');
        document.body.classList.toggle('home-active', sectionName === 'home');
        document.getElementById('loginSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('homeSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('searchSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('subjectSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('simpleSearchSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('resultSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('counselSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('collegePdfSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('classRosterSection').classList.add('hidden');
        document.getElementById('collegeApplySection').classList.add('hidden');

        if (sectionName === 'login') document.getElementById('loginSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'home') document.getElementById('homeSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'search') document.getElementById('searchSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'subject') document.getElementById('subjectSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'simpleSearch') document.getElementById('simpleSearchSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'result') document.getElementById('resultSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'subjectAnalysis') document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'counsel') document.getElementById('counselSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'collegePdf') document.getElementById('collegePdfSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'classRoster') document.getElementById('classRosterSection').classList.remove('hidden');
        if (sectionName === 'collegeApply') document.getElementById('collegeApplySection').classList.remove('hidden');

        if (pushHistory) {
          const last = appHistory[appHistory.length - 1];
          if (last !== sectionName) appHistory.push(sectionName);
        }

        setBackButton();
        setModeSwitchButton(sectionName);
        if (sectionName === 'search') setStatus('searchStatus', '');
        if (sectionName === 'subject') setStatus('subjectStatus', '');
        if (sectionName === 'simpleSearch') setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '');
        if (sectionName === 'collegeApply') setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', '');
        window.scrollTo({ top: 0, behavior: 'smooth' });
      }

      function goBack() {
        if (currentResult && currentResult.mode === 'student' && resultBackStack.length > 0) {
          const prevResult = resultBackStack.pop();
          renderResult(prevResult);
          showSection('result', false);
          return;
        }

        if (appHistory.length <= 1) return;

        appHistory.pop();
        let prev = appHistory[appHistory.length - 1];

        // 로그인 이후에는 뒤로가기로 로그인 화면에 돌아가지 않음
        if (isLoggedIn && prev === 'login') {
          prev = 'home';
          appHistory[appHistory.length - 1] = 'home';
        }

        showSection(prev, false);
      }

      function setStatus(id, text) {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el) el.textContent = text || '';
      }

      function makeRequestCacheKey_(name, payload) {
        try {
          return name + ':' + JSON.stringify(payload || {});
        } catch (e) {
          return name + ':' + String(new Date().getTime());
        }
      }

      function getCachedRequest_(key) {
        return mobileRequestCache[key] || null;
      }

      function putCachedRequest_(key, value) {
        if (!key || !value) return;
        mobileRequestCache[key] = value;
      }

      function runNextTick_(fn) {
        setTimeout(fn, 0);
      }

      function saveLoginSession_(password, access) {
        try {
          const expiresAt = Date.now() + LOGIN_SESSION_HOURS * 60 * 60 * 1000;
