          localStorage.setItem(LOGIN_SESSION_STORAGE_KEY, JSON.stringify({
            password: String(password || ''),
            canEditCollegeApply: !!(access && access.canEditCollegeApply),
            expiresAt: expiresAt
          }));
        } catch (e) {}
      }

      function readLoginSession_() {
        try {
          const raw = localStorage.getItem(LOGIN_SESSION_STORAGE_KEY);
          if (!raw) return null;
          const session = JSON.parse(raw);
          if (!session || !session.password || !session.expiresAt || Number(session.expiresAt) <= Date.now()) {
            localStorage.removeItem(LOGIN_SESSION_STORAGE_KEY);
            return null;
          }
          return session;
        } catch (e) {
          try { localStorage.removeItem(LOGIN_SESSION_STORAGE_KEY); } catch (ignore) {}
          return null;
        }
      }

      function restoreLoginSession_() {
        const session = readLoginSession_();
        if (!session) return false;

        isLoggedIn = true;
        loginPasswordValue = String(session.password || '');
        collegeApplyCanEdit = session.canEditCollegeApply === true;
        setStatus('loginStatus', '자료를 불러오는 중입니다...');
        loadInitData('home');
        return true;
      }

      function login() {
        loginAndOpenMode('home');
      }

      function loginAndOpenMode(mode) {
        pendingLoginMode = mode || 'home';

        if (isLoggedIn) {
          openModeAfterLogin_(pendingLoginMode);
          return;
        }

        const password = document.getElementById('password').value.trim();
        setStatus('loginStatus', '');

        if (!password) {
          setStatus('loginStatus', '비밀번호를 입력해 주세요.');
          return;
        }

        setStatus('loginStatus', '로그인 확인 중입니다...');

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(access) {
            if (!access || !access.ok) {
              setStatus('loginStatus', '비밀번호가 올바르지 않습니다.');
              return;
            }

            isLoggedIn = true;
            loginPasswordValue = password;
            collegeApplyCanEdit = access.canEditCollegeApply === true;
            saveLoginSession_(password, access);
            setStatus('loginStatus', '자료를 불러오는 중입니다...');
            loadInitData(pendingLoginMode);
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            setStatus('loginStatus', err.message || String(err));
          })
          .mobileGetLoginAccess(password);
      }

      function loadInitData(nextMode) {
        if (initDataLoaded) {
          openModeAfterLogin_(nextMode || 'home');
          return;
        }

        if (initDataLoading) {
          initDataWaitQueue.push(nextMode || 'home');
          return;
        }

        initDataLoading = true;
        initDataWaitQueue.push(nextMode || 'home');

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
            populateMonths(data.months || []);
            populateMiddleSchools(data.middleSchools || []);
            populateSubjectMonths(data.subjectMonths || data.months || []);
            renderSubjectButtons();
            initDataLoaded = true;
            initDataLoading = false;

            const queue = initDataWaitQueue.slice();
            initDataWaitQueue = [];
            openModeAfterLogin_(queue[queue.length - 1] || 'home');
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            initDataLoading = false;
            initDataWaitQueue = [];
            setStatus('loginStatus', err.message || String(err));
          })
          .mobileGetInitData();
      }

      function openModeAfterLogin_(mode) {
        setStatus('loginStatus', '');

        if (mode === 'homeroom') {
          currentMode = 'homeroom';
          appHistory = ['home'];
          showSection('search');
          return;
        }

        if (mode === 'subject') {
          currentMode = 'subject';
          appHistory = ['home'];
          showSection('subject');
          return;
        }

        if (mode === 'simple') {
          currentMode = 'simple';
          appHistory = ['home'];
          showSection('simpleSearch');
          return;
        }

        if (mode === 'collegeApply') {
          currentMode = 'collegeApply';
          appHistory = ['home'];
          openCollegeApplyMode();
          return;
        }

        appHistory = ['home'];
        showSection('home', false);
      }

      restoreLoginSession_();

      function populateMonths(months) {
        const select = document.getElementById('monthSelect');
        select.innerHTML = '';

        months.forEach(function(item) {
          const option = document.createElement('option');
          option.value = item.value;
          option.textContent = item.label;
          select.appendChild(option);
        });
      }

      function populateMiddleSchools(items) {
        const select = document.getElementById('middleSchoolSelect');
        if (!select) return;
        select.innerHTML = '';
        const list = items && items.length ? items : [{ value: 'ALL', label: 'ALL(전체)' }];
        list.forEach(function(item) {
          const option = document.createElement('option');
          option.value = item.value;
          option.textContent = item.label;
          select.appendChild(option);
        });
        select.value = 'ALL';
      }

      function populateSubjectMonths(months) {
        const select = document.getElementById('subjectMonthSelect');
        if (!select) return;
        select.innerHTML = '';
        const fixedOrder = [3, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10, 11];
        const available = (months || [])
          .filter(item => fixedOrder.includes(Number(item.value)))
          .sort((a, b) => fixedOrder.indexOf(Number(a.value)) - fixedOrder.indexOf(Number(b.value)));
        available.forEach(function(item) {
          const option = document.createElement('option');
          option.value = item.value;
          option.textContent = item.label;
          select.appendChild(option);
        });
        if (available.length > 0) select.value = available[available.length - 1].value;
      }

      function openHomeroomMode() {
        currentMode = 'homeroom';
        if (isLoggedIn) {
          showSection('search');
        } else {
          loginAndOpenMode('homeroom');
        }
      }

      function openSubjectMode() {
        currentMode = 'subject';
        if (isLoggedIn) {
          showSection('subject');
        } else {
          loginAndOpenMode('subject');
        }
      }

      function openSimpleSearchMode() {
        currentMode = 'simple';
        if (isLoggedIn) {
          showSection('simpleSearch');
        } else {
          loginAndOpenMode('simple');
        }
      }

      function switchMode() {
        if (!isLoggedIn) return;

        resultBackStack = [];
        currentResult = null;
        document.getElementById('chartsArea').innerHTML = '';
        document.getElementById('resultTable').innerHTML = '';

        if (currentMode === 'subject') {
          currentMode = 'homeroom';
          showSection('search');
        } else {
          currentMode = 'subject';
          showSection('subject');
        }
      }

      const SUBJECT_GROUPS = [
        { group: '국어', items: ['화법과작문', '언어와매체'] },
        { group: '수학', items: ['확률과통계', '미적분', '기하'] },
        { group: '영어', items: ['영어'] },
        { group: '탐구', items: ['경제', '사회문화', '생활과윤리', '윤리와사상', '정치와법', '세계사', '동아시아사', '한국지리', '세계지리', '물리학1', '물리학2', '화학1', '화학2', '생명과학1', '생명과학2', '지구과학1', '지구과학2', '한국사'] }
      ];

      function renderSubjectButtons() {
        const area = document.getElementById('subjectButtons');
        if (!area) return;
        area.innerHTML = SUBJECT_GROUPS.map(function(group) {
          const isMulti = group.group === '국어' || group.group === '수학' || group.group === '탐구';
          const title = escapeHtml(group.group) + (isMulti ? ' <span class="subject-multi-note">(다중 선택 가능)</span>' : '');
          const buttons = group.items.map(function(subject) {
            return '<button type="button" class="subject-chip" data-group="' + escapeHtml(group.group) + '" data-subject="' + escapeHtml(subject) + '" onclick="selectSubject(\'' + escapeJsAttr(group.group) + '\', \'' + escapeJsAttr(subject) + '\')">' + escapeHtml(subject) + '</button>';
          }).join('');
          return '<div class="subject-group"><h3 class="subject-group-title">' + title + '</h3><div class="subject-chip-grid">' + buttons + '</div></div>';
        }).join('');
      }
      function selectSubject(group, subject) {
        const isMultiGroup = group === '국어' || group === '수학' || group === '탐구';

        if (selectedSubjectGroup && selectedSubjectGroup !== group) {
          selectedSubjects = [];
        }

        selectedSubjectGroup = group;

        if (isMultiGroup) {
          const idx = selectedSubjects.indexOf(subject);
          if (idx >= 0) {
            selectedSubjects.splice(idx, 1);
          } else {
            selectedSubjects.push(subject);
          }
        } else {
          selectedSubjects = selectedSubjects[0] === subject ? [] : [subject];
        }

        if (selectedSubjects.length === 0) {
          selectedSubjectGroup = '';
          selectedSubjectName = '';
          document.getElementById('selectedSubjectGroup').value = '';
          document.getElementById('selectedSubjectName').value = '';
          document.getElementById('subjectSelectedText').textContent = '과목을 선택해 주세요.';
        } else {
          selectedSubjectName = selectedSubjects.join(', ');
          document.getElementById('selectedSubjectGroup').value = selectedSubjectGroup;
          document.getElementById('selectedSubjectName').value = selectedSubjectName;
          document.getElementById('subjectSelectedText').textContent = selectedSubjectGroup + ' / ' + selectedSubjects.join(', ');
        }

        document.querySelectorAll('.subject-chip').forEach(function(btn) {
          const btnGroup = btn.getAttribute('data-group');
          const btnSubject = btn.getAttribute('data-subject');
          const selected = btnGroup === selectedSubjectGroup && selectedSubjects.includes(btnSubject);
          btn.classList.toggle('selected', selected);
        });
      }
      
      function searchSimpleData() {
        setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '');
        const input = document.getElementById('simpleSearchInput');
        const query = input ? input.value.trim() : '';

        if (!query) {
          setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '검색어를 입력해 주세요.');
          return;
        }

        setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '조회 중입니다...');

        const payload = { query: query };
        const cacheKey = makeRequestCacheKey_('mobileSimpleSearch', payload);
        const cached = getCachedRequest_(cacheKey);

        if (cached) {
          setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '');
          resultBackStack = [];
          currentMode = 'simple';
          renderResult(cached);
          showSection('result');
          return;
        }

        runNextTick_(function() {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
              putCachedRequest_(cacheKey, result);
              setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', '');
              resultBackStack = [];
              currentMode = 'simple';
              renderResult(result);
              showSection('result');
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
              setStatus('simpleSearchStatus', err.message || String(err));
            })
            .mobileSimpleSearch(payload);
        });
      }

function searchSubjectData() {
        setStatus('subjectStatus', '');
        const month = document.getElementById('subjectMonthSelect').value;
        const group = selectedSubjectGroup || document.getElementById('selectedSubjectGroup').value;
        const subjects = selectedSubjects.slice();

        if (!month) {
          setStatus('subjectStatus', '모의고사 월을 선택해 주세요.');
          return;
        }
        if (!group || subjects.length === 0) {
          setStatus('subjectStatus', '과목을 선택해 주세요.');
          return;
        }

        setStatus('subjectStatus', '조회 중입니다...');

        const payload = { month: month, group: group, subjects: subjects };
        const cacheKey = makeRequestCacheKey_('mobileSubjectSearch', payload);
        const cached = getCachedRequest_(cacheKey);

        if (cached) {
          setStatus('subjectStatus', '');
          resultBackStack = [];
          renderResult(cached);
          showSection('result');
          return;
        }

        runNextTick_(function() {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
              putCachedRequest_(cacheKey, result);
              resultBackStack = [];
              renderResult(result);
              showSection('result');
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
              setStatus('subjectStatus', err.message || String(err));
            })
            .mobileSubjectSearch(payload);
        });
      }
      // 글자를 다시 입력하면 선택했던 특정 학생 정보를 초기화
      function clearSelection() {
        selectedStudentNo = '';
        selectedSuggestionLabel = '';
      }

      // 검색 버튼 클릭 시 메인 로직
      function searchData() {
        setStatus('searchStatus', '');

        const nameKeyword = document.getElementById('nameInput').value.trim();
        const month = document.getElementById('monthSelect').value;
        const classValue = document.getElementById('classSelect').value;
        const middleSchool = document.getElementById('middleSchoolSelect') ? document.getElementById('middleSchoolSelect').value : 'ALL';

        if (!nameKeyword && !classValue) {
          setStatus('searchStatus', '반을 선택하거나 이름을 입력해 주세요.');
          return;
        }

        // 이름이 입력되었으나 아직 팝업에서 특정 학생을 선택하지 않은 경우 (동명이인 확인 필요)
        if (nameKeyword && !selectedStudentNo) {
          const suggestionKey = nameKeyword;
          const cachedSuggestions = mobileNameSuggestionCache[suggestionKey];

          const handleSuggestions = function(items) {
            if (items && items.length > 1) {
              // 여러 명일 경우 동명이인 팝업창 띄움
              showNameModal(items, nameKeyword);
            } else if (items && items.length === 1) {
              // 1명뿐이면 학생이름(반)을 보여 주지 않고 바로 상세 화면으로 이동
              selectedStudentNo = items[0].studentNo;
              selectedSuggestionLabel = items[0].name || nameKeyword;
              document.getElementById('nameInput').value = nameKeyword;
              executeSearch(month, classValue, nameKeyword, selectedStudentNo, middleSchool);
            } else {
              // 검색된 이름이 없는 경우
              executeSearch(month, classValue, nameKeyword, '', middleSchool);
            }
          };

          if (cachedSuggestions) {
            handleSuggestions(cachedSuggestions);
            return;
          }

          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(items) {
              mobileNameSuggestionCache[suggestionKey] = items || [];
              handleSuggestions(items || []);
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
              setStatus('searchStatus', '동명이인 확인 중 오류가 발생했습니다.');
            })
            .mobileGetNameSuggestions(nameKeyword);
        } else {
          // 이미 특정 학생이 선택되어 있거나, 이름 없이 반 전체 조회를 할 경우
          executeSearch(month, classValue, nameKeyword, selectedStudentNo, middleSchool);
        }
      }

      // 팝업창(모달) 보여주기
      function showNameModal(students, keyword) {
        const list = document.getElementById('modalList');
        list.innerHTML = ''; // 기존 목록 초기화
        
        students.forEach(s => {
          const div = document.createElement('div');
          div.className = 'modal-list-item';
          div.textContent = s.label;
          div.onclick = function() {
            // 학생을 선택하면
            selectedStudentNo = s.studentNo;
            selectedSuggestionLabel = s.label;
            document.getElementById('nameInput').value = s.label;
            closeNameModal(); // 팝업 닫기
            searchData(); // 즉시 성적 조회 재실행
          };
          list.appendChild(div);
        });

        document.getElementById('nameModal').classList.remove('hidden');
      }

      // 팝업창 닫기 (취소 버튼용)
      function closeNameModal() {
        const modal = document.getElementById('nameModal');
        const title = modal ? modal.querySelector('.modal-title') : null;
        if (modal) modal.classList.add('hidden');
        if (title) {
          title.classList.remove('small-title');
          title.innerHTML = '동명이인 입니다.<br>학생을 선택해주세요.';
        }
      }

      // 실제 성적 결과 조회 통신 로직
      function executeSearch(month, classValue, nameKeyword, studentNo, middleSchool) {
        setStatus('searchStatus', '조회 중입니다...');

        const payload = {
          month: month,
          classValue: classValue,
          middleSchool: middleSchool || 'ALL',
          nameKeyword: studentNo ? selectedSuggestionLabel : nameKeyword,
          studentNo: studentNo
        };
        const cacheKey = makeRequestCacheKey_('mobileSearch', payload);
        const cached = getCachedRequest_(cacheKey);

        if (cached) {
          setStatus('searchStatus', '');
          resultBackStack = [];
          if (cached && cached.mode === 'class') classSortMode = 'naesin';
          renderResult(cached);
          showSection('result');
          return;
        }

        runNextTick_(function() {
          google.script.run
            .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
              putCachedRequest_(cacheKey, result);
              resultBackStack = [];
              if (result && result.mode === 'class') classSortMode = 'naesin';
              renderResult(result);
              showSection('result');
            })
            .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
              setStatus('searchStatus', err.message || String(err));
            })
            .mobileSearch(payload);
        });
      }

      function isClassSortApplicable(result) {
        if (!result || result.mode !== 'class') return false;
        return !String(result.title || '').includes('전체');
      }

      function clearClassSortButton(headerEl) {
        if (!headerEl) return;
        headerEl.classList.remove('class-sort-header');
        const oldBtn = headerEl.querySelector('.class-sort-btn');
        if (oldBtn) oldBtn.remove();
      }

      function updateClassSortButton(headerEl, result) {
        if (!headerEl) return;
        clearClassSortButton(headerEl);

        if (!isClassSortApplicable(result)) return;

        headerEl.classList.add('class-sort-header');
        const btn = document.createElement('button');
        btn.type = 'button';
        btn.className = 'class-sort-btn';
        btn.textContent = classSortMode === 'naesin' ? '번호순 정렬' : '내신순 정렬';
        btn.onclick = toggleClassSortMode;
        headerEl.appendChild(btn);
      }

      function toggleClassSortMode() {
        if (!currentResult || currentResult.mode !== 'class') return;
        classSortMode = classSortMode === 'naesin' ? 'number' : 'naesin';
        renderResult(currentResult);
      }

      function renderResult(result) {
        currentResult = result || null;

        const titleEl = document.getElementById('resultTitle');
        const headerEl = titleEl ? titleEl.closest('.panel-header') : null;

        if (result && result.mode === 'student') {
          if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = '';
          if (headerEl) headerEl.style.display = 'none';
        } else {
          if (titleEl) {
            if (result && result.mode === 'subject') {
              titleEl.innerHTML = buildSubjectTitleHtml(result);
            } else if (result && result.mode === 'class') {
              titleEl.textContent = buildClassTitleWithCounts(result);
            } else {
              titleEl.textContent = result && result.title ? result.title : '';
            }
          }
          if (headerEl) headerEl.style.display = '';
        }

        updateClassSortButton(headerEl, result);

        const studentInfoHtml = result && result.mode === 'student'
          ? buildStudentInfoHtml(result.studentInfo)
          : '';

        document.getElementById('resultTable').innerHTML =
          studentInfoHtml + buildTableHtml(result.mode, result.headers || [], result.rows || [], result.title || '');

        const chartsArea = document.getElementById('chartsArea');
        chartsArea.innerHTML = '';

        if (result.mode === 'student' && result.charts && result.charts.length) {
          result.charts.forEach(function(chart, index) {
            const card = document.createElement('div');
            card.className = 'chart-card';

            const title = document.createElement('h3');
            title.className = 'section-title';
            title.textContent = chart.title;

            const box = document.createElement('div');
            box.className = 'chart-box';
            box.id = 'chart_' + index;

            card.appendChild(title);
            card.appendChild(box);
            chartsArea.appendChild(card);
          });

          drawChartsWhenReady(result.charts);
        }
      }

      function buildClassTitleWithCounts(result) {
        const baseTitle = String(result && result.title ? result.title : '');
        const rows = Array.isArray(result && result.rows) ? result.rows : [];
        const total = rows.length;
        const attended = rows.filter(function(row) {
          const gradeValues = [row[3], row[4], row[5], row[6], row[7]];
          return gradeValues.some(function(value) {
            const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
            return text !== '' && text !== '99' && text !== '-';
          });
        }).length;

        const countText = '(총원 ' + total + '명 중 ' + attended + '명 응시)';
        if (!baseTitle) return countText;
        if (baseTitle.includes('총원 ')) return baseTitle;

        const filterSep = baseTitle.indexOf(' / ');
        const mainTitle = filterSep >= 0 ? baseTitle.substring(0, filterSep) : baseTitle;
        const filterTitle = filterSep >= 0 ? baseTitle.substring(filterSep) : '';

        return mainTitle + '\n' + countText + filterTitle;
      }

      function buildSubjectTitleHtml(result) {
        const trend = result && result.subjectTrend ? result.subjectTrend : null;
        const rawTitle = String(result && result.title ? result.title : '');
        const monthText = rawTitle.split('(')[0];
        const canOpenAnalysis = !!(result && result.analysisEnabled && result.analysisSubject && result.analysisSubject !== '한국사');
        const baseHtml = canOpenAnalysis
          ? '<button type="button" class="subject-analysis-title-link" onclick="openSubjectAnalysis()">' + escapeHtml(monthText) + '</button>'
          : escapeHtml(monthText);

        if (!trend || !trend.counts || !trend.counts.length) return baseHtml;

        const counts = trend.counts.map(function(v) { return String(v); });
        const lastIndex = counts.length - 1;
        const chain = counts.map(function(count, idx) {
          if (idx === lastIndex && trend.lossRows && trend.lossRows.length) {
            return '<button type="button" class="subject-count-link" onclick="showSubjectChangeList()">' + escapeHtml(count) + '</button>';
          }
          return escapeHtml(count);
        }).join('→');

        return baseHtml + '(' + chain + ')';
      }

      function openSubjectAnalysis() {
        if (!currentResult || currentResult.mode !== 'subject') return;
        const subject = String(currentResult.analysisSubject || (currentResult.subjects && currentResult.subjects[0]) || '').trim();
        const month = Number(currentResult.month || document.getElementById('subjectMonthSelect').value);
        if (!subject || subject === '한국사' || !month) return;

        const titleEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisTitle');
        const metaEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisMeta');
        const contentEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisContent');
        if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = month + '월 ' + subject;
        if (metaEl) metaEl.textContent = '2026학년도 · 내신 5.00 이내 기준';
        if (contentEl) contentEl.innerHTML = '<div class="subject-analysis-loading">분석 자료를 불러오는 중입니다...</div>';

        showSection('subjectAnalysis');

        const payload = { month: month, subject: subject };
        const cacheKey = makeRequestCacheKey_('mobileGetSubjectAnalysis', payload);
        const cached = getCachedRequest_(cacheKey);
        if (cached) {
          renderSubjectAnalysis(cached);
          return;
        }

        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            putCachedRequest_(cacheKey, result);
            renderSubjectAnalysis(result);
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            if (contentEl) contentEl.innerHTML = '<div class="subject-analysis-empty">' + escapeHtml(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)) + '</div>';
          })
          .mobileGetSubjectAnalysis(payload);
      }

      function renderSubjectAnalysis(result) {
        const titleEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisTitle');
        const metaEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisMeta');
        const contentEl = document.getElementById('subjectAnalysisContent');
        if (!contentEl) return;

        if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = result && result.title ? result.title : '';
        if (metaEl) {
          const year = result && result.academicYearLabel ? result.academicYearLabel : '2026학년도';
          const naesin = result && result.naesinLabel ? result.naesinLabel : '내신 5.00 이내';
          metaEl.textContent = year + ' · ' + naesin + ' 기준';
        }

        let html = '';
        if (result && result.selectionSection && result.selectionSection.visible) {
          html += buildSubjectAnalysisSectionHtml(result.selectionSection, false);
        }
        if (result && result.gradeSection && result.gradeSection.visible) {
          html += buildSubjectAnalysisSectionHtml(result.gradeSection, true);
        }
        contentEl.innerHTML = html || '<div class="subject-analysis-empty">표시할 분석 자료가 없습니다.</div>';
      }

      function buildSubjectAnalysisSectionHtml(section, isGrade) {
        const headers = Array.isArray(section && section.headers) ? section.headers : [];
        const rows = Array.isArray(section && section.rows) ? section.rows : [];
        const tableClass = isGrade ? 'subject-analysis-table grade-table' : 'subject-analysis-table';
        const head = '<thead><tr>' + headers.map(function(header) {
          return '<th>' + escapeHtml(header) + '</th>';
        }).join('') + '</tr></thead>';

        const body = '<tbody>' + rows.map(function(row) {
          const cells = Array.isArray(row && row.cells) ? row.cells : [];
          return '<tr>' +
            '<td class="subject-analysis-row-label">' + escapeHtml(row && row.label ? row.label : '') + '</td>' +
            cells.map(function(cell) {
              const primary = cell && cell.primary != null ? String(cell.primary) : '';
              const secondary = cell && cell.secondary != null ? String(cell.secondary) : '';
              return '<td>' +
                '<div class="subject-analysis-cell-primary">' + escapeHtml(primary) + '</div>' +
                (secondary ? '<div class="subject-analysis-cell-secondary">' + escapeHtml(secondary) + '</div>' : '') +
              '</td>';
            }).join('') +
          '</tr>';
        }).join('') + '</tbody>';

        return '<section class="subject-analysis-card">' +
          '<h3 class="subject-analysis-card-title">' + escapeHtml(section && section.title ? section.title : '') + '</h3>' +
          '<div class="subject-analysis-table-wrap"><table class="' + tableClass + '">' + head + body + '</table></div>' +
          '<div class="subject-analysis-note">※ ' + escapeHtml(section && section.note ? section.note : '') + '</div>' +
        '</section>';
      }

      function showSubjectChangeList() {
        if (!currentResult || !currentResult.subjectTrend) return;
        const rows = currentResult.subjectTrend.lossRows || [];
        const modal = document.getElementById('nameModal');
        const list = document.getElementById('modalList');
        const title = modal ? modal.querySelector('.modal-title') : null;
        if (!modal || !list) return;

        if (title) {
          title.classList.add('small-title');
          title.innerHTML = '선택 과목 변경 학생';
        }

        if (!rows.length) {
          list.innerHTML = '<div class="subject-loss-list"><div class="subject-loss-item">변경 학생이 없습니다.</div></div>';
        } else {
          list.innerHTML = '<div class="subject-loss-list">' + rows.map(function(row) {
            return '<div class="subject-loss-item">' + escapeHtml(row.text || '') + '</div>';
          }).join('') + '</div>';
        }

        modal.classList.remove('hidden');
      }

      function getStudentMonthColorIndex(month, monthColorMap) {
        const key = String(month == null ? '' : month).trim();
        if (!key) return 3;
        if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(monthColorMap, key)) return monthColorMap[key];
        return 3;
      }

      function buildStudentMonthColorMap(rows) {
        const months = [];
        (rows || []).forEach(function(row) {
          const month = Number(row && row[0]);
          if (!isNaN(month) && months.indexOf(month) < 0) months.push(month);
        });
        months.sort(function(a, b) { return b - a; });
        const map = {};
        months.forEach(function(month, idx) {
          map[String(month)] = idx < 3 ? idx : 3;
        });
        return map;
      }

      function buildTableHtml(mode, headers, rows, title) {
        if (!rows || !rows.length) {
          if (mode === 'simple') {
            return buildSimpleSearchEmptyHtml();
          }

          const emptyText = mode === 'class' ? '해당 학생이 없습니다.' : '조회된 데이터가 없습니다.';
          return '<div class="empty-box">' + escapeHtml(emptyText) + '</div>';
        }
        if (mode === 'subject') return buildSubjectTableHtml(headers, rows);
        if (mode === 'simple') return buildSimpleSearchTableHtml(headers, rows);

        let finalHeaders = headers.slice();
        let tableClass = 'table';
        let colGroup = '';
        const isAllClassView = mode === 'class' && String(title || '').includes('전체');
        const studentMonthColorMap = mode === 'student' ? buildStudentMonthColorMap(rows) : {};
        let renderRows = rows.slice();
        if (mode === 'class' && !isAllClassView && classSortMode === 'number') {
          renderRows.sort(function(a, b) {
            const aNo = String(a && a[0] != null ? a[0] : '');
            const bNo = String(b && b[0] != null ? b[0] : '');
            return aNo.localeCompare(bNo, 'ko', { numeric: true });
          });
        }
        if (mode === 'class') {
          finalHeaders = isAllClassView ? ['반', '이름', '내신', '국', '수', '영', '탐1', '탐2'] : ['번호', '이름', '내신', '국', '수', '영', '탐1', '탐2'];
          tableClass = 'table compact-class';
          colGroup = '<colgroup><col style="width: 12%;"><col style="width: 24%;"><col style="width: 14%;"><col style="width: 10%;"><col style="width: 10%;"><col style="width: 10%;"><col style="width: 10%;"><col style="width: 10%;"></colgroup>';
        } else {
          tableClass = 'table scrollable-table';
        }
        const head = '<thead>' + finalHeaders.map(function(h) { return '<th>' + escapeHtml(h) + '</th>'; }).join('') + '</thead>';
        const bodyRows = renderRows.map(function(row) {
          if (mode === 'class') {
            const studentNo = String(row[0] == null ? '' : row[0]).trim();
            const lastTwo = studentNo ? studentNo.slice(-2).padStart(2, '0') : '';
            const classNum = studentNo.length >= 2 ? String(Number(studentNo.substring(1, 2))) : '';
            const firstValue = isAllClassView ? classNum : lastTwo;
            const displayRow = [firstValue, row[1], row[2], row[3], row[4], row[5], row[6], row[7]];
            return '<tr>' + displayRow.map(function(cell, idx) {
              let val = String(cell == null ? '' : cell).trim();
              let cellClass = '';
              if ((val === '1' || val === '2') && [3, 4, 5, 6, 7].includes(idx)) cellClass = ' class="text-red-grade"';
              if (idx === 1 && studentNo) return '<td><button type="button" class="student-name-btn" onclick="openStudentDetail(\'' + escapeJsAttr(studentNo) + '\')">' + escapeHtml(val) + '</button></td>';
              return '<td' + cellClass + '>' + escapeHtml(val) + '</td>';
            }).join('') + '</tr>';
          }
          const studentColorClass = mode === 'student'
            ? ' student-month-recent-' + getStudentMonthColorIndex(row[0], studentMonthColorMap)
            : '';
          const currentStudentNo = mode === 'student' ? String(row[1] == null ? '' : row[1]).trim() : '';
          const rowIndex = renderRows.indexOf(row);
          const prevRow = mode === 'student' && rowIndex > 0 ? renderRows[rowIndex - 1] : null;
          const prevStudentNo = prevRow ? String(prevRow[1] == null ? '' : prevRow[1]).trim() : '';
          const breakClass = mode === 'student' && prevStudentNo && currentStudentNo && prevStudentNo !== currentStudentNo
            ? ' student-break-row'
            : '';

          return '<tr class="' + (studentColorClass + breakClass).trim() + '">' + row.map(function(cell, idx) {
            let val = String(cell == null ? '' : cell).trim();
            let cellClass = '';
            if (mode === 'student' && idx === 1 && val.length === 5 && val.charAt(1) === '0') val = val.charAt(0) + val.substring(2);
            if ((val === '1' || val === '2') && mode === 'student' && [5, 7, 8, 10, 12].includes(idx)) cellClass = ' class="text-red-grade"';
            return '<td' + cellClass + '>' + escapeHtml(val) + '</td>';
          }).join('') + '</tr>';
        }).join('');
        const noteHtml = mode === 'student' ? '<div class="mock-absence-note">※ 미응시한 과목의 데이터는 &#39;99&#39;로 표현합니다.</div>' : '';
        return '<div class="table-responsive-wrap"><table class="' + tableClass + '">' + colGroup + head + '<tbody>' + bodyRows + '</tbody></table></div>' + noteHtml;
      }

      
      
      function buildSimpleSearchEmptyHtml() {
        return '' +
          '<div class="empty-box simple-empty-box">' +
            '<div class="simple-empty-title">조회된 데이터가 없습니다.</div>' +
            '<div class="simple-empty-guide">' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-title">검색 방법</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>전화번호</b>: 1234, 8880처럼 일부 번호 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>내신</b>: 1.5 또는 1.0~2.3처럼 소수점 포함 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>출생월</b>: 3월, 8월처럼 숫자 뒤에 월 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>주소</b>: 금호어울림, 한강신도시 등 일부 단어 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>출신중</b>: 고촌중, 신곡중 등 일부 학교명 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>희망 학과</b>: 간호, 경영, 컴퓨터 등 일부 단어 입력</div>' +
              '<div class="simple-empty-guide-line"><b>이름</b>: 학생 이름, 부모 성명 일부 입력</div>' +
            '</div>' +
          '</div>';
      }

function buildSimpleSearchTableHtml(headers, rows) {
        const finalHeaders = headers && headers.length ? headers : ['학번', '이름', '내신', '일치 정보'];
        const head = '<thead>' + finalHeaders.map(function(h) { return '<th>' + escapeHtml(h) + '</th>'; }).join('') + '</thead>';

        const body = (rows || []).map(function(row) {
          const studentNo = String(row[0] == null ? '' : row[0]).trim();
          const name = String(row[1] == null ? '' : row[1]).trim();
          const naesin = String(row[2] == null ? '' : row[2]).trim();
          const matchInfo = String(row[3] == null ? '' : row[3]).trim();

          return '<tr>' +
            '<td title="' + escapeHtml(studentNo) + '">' + escapeHtml(studentNo) + '</td>' +
            '<td class="simple-name-cell"><button type="button" class="student-name-btn simple-name-btn" onclick="openStudentDetail(\'' + escapeJsAttr(studentNo) + '\')">' + escapeHtml(name) + '</button></td>' +
            '<td title="' + escapeHtml(naesin) + '">' + escapeHtml(naesin) + '</td>' +
            '<td class="simple-match-cell" title="' + escapeHtml(matchInfo) + '">' + escapeHtml(matchInfo) + '</td>' +
          '</tr>';
        }).join('');

        return '<div class="table-responsive-wrap simple-search-table-wrap"><table class="table simple-search-table">' +
          '<colgroup><col style="width:18%"><col style="width:22%"><col style="width:14%"><col style="width:46%"></colgroup>' +
          head + '<tbody>' + body + '</tbody></table></div>';
      }

function buildSubjectTableHtml(headers, rows) {
        const hasSubjectCol = headers.indexOf('과목') >= 0;
        const head = '<thead>' + headers.map(function(h) { return '<th>' + escapeHtml(h) + '</th>'; }).join('') + '</thead>';
        const gradeIdx = headers.indexOf('등급');
        const studentNoIdx = headers.indexOf('학번');
        const nameIdx = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return String(h || '').indexOf('이름') === 0; });
        const rankIdx = headers.indexOf('순위');
        const subjectIdx = headers.indexOf('과목');
        const tableClass = hasSubjectCol
          ? 'table subject-result-table subject-result-compact subject-result-multi'
          : 'table subject-result-table subject-result-compact';
        const colGroup = buildSubjectColGroup(headers);

        const body = rows.map(function(row) {
          const grade = String(row[gradeIdx] == null ? '' : row[gradeIdx]).trim();
          const isTop = grade === '1' || grade === '2';
          const studentNo = String(row[studentNoIdx] == null ? '' : row[studentNoIdx]).trim();

          return '<tr' + (isTop ? ' class="subject-good-row"' : '') + '>' + row.map(function(cell, idx) {
            const val = String(cell == null ? '' : cell).trim();
            if (idx === rankIdx) {
              return '<td class="subject-rank-cell" title="' + escapeHtml(val) + '">' + escapeHtml(val) + '</td>';
            }
            if (idx === nameIdx && studentNo) {
              return '<td class="subject-name-cell"><button type="button" class="student-name-btn subject-name-fixed" title="' + escapeHtml(val) + '" onclick="openStudentDetail(\'' + escapeJsAttr(studentNo) + '\')">' + escapeHtml(shortenSubjectName(val)) + '</button></td>';
            }
            if (idx === subjectIdx) {
              return '<td class="subject-abbr-cell" title="' + escapeHtml(val) + '">' + escapeHtml(val) + '</td>';
            }
            return '<td title="' + escapeHtml(val) + '">' + escapeHtml(val) + '</td>';
          }).join('') + '</tr>';
        }).join('');
        return '<div class="table-responsive-wrap subject-table-wrap"><table class="' + tableClass + '">' + colGroup + head + '<tbody>' + body + '</tbody></table></div>';
      }

      function buildSubjectColGroup(headers) {
        const count = headers.length;
        if (count === 9) {
          return '<colgroup><col style="width:7%"><col style="width:13%"><col style="width:15%"><col style="width:9%"><col style="width:9%"><col style="width:9%"><col style="width:11%"><col style="width:16%"><col style="width:11%"></colgroup>';
        }
        if (count === 8) {
          return '<colgroup><col style="width:7%"><col style="width:14%"><col style="width:23%"><col style="width:10%"><col style="width:10%"><col style="width:12%"><col style="width:16%"><col style="width:8%"></colgroup>';
        }
        if (count === 7) {
          return '<colgroup><col style="width:8%"><col style="width:15%"><col style="width:19%"><col style="width:12%"><col style="width:15%"><col style="width:20%"><col style="width:11%"></colgroup>';
        }
        if (count === 6) {
          return '<colgroup><col style="width:8%"><col style="width:15%"><col style="width:28%"><col style="width:15%"><col style="width:22%"><col style="width:12%"></colgroup>';
        }
        return '';
      }

      function shortenSubjectName(name) {
        const text = String(name == null ? '' : name).trim();
        if (text.length <= 9) return text;
        return text.slice(0, 9) + '…';
      }


function openStudentDetail(studentNo) {
  setStatus('searchStatus', '');
  setStatus('resultStatus', '조회 중입니다...');

  const prevResult = currentResult && (currentResult.mode === 'class' || currentResult.mode === 'subject')
    ? currentResult
    : null;

  const payload = {
    studentNo: studentNo,
    nameKeyword: '',
    month: '',
    classValue: ''
  };
  const cacheKey = makeRequestCacheKey_('mobileSearch', payload);
  const cached = getCachedRequest_(cacheKey);

  if (cached) {
    setStatus('resultStatus', '');
    if (prevResult) {
      resultBackStack.push(prevResult);
    }
    renderResult(cached);
    showSection('result');
    return;
  }

  runNextTick_(function() {
    google.script.run
      .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
        setStatus('resultStatus', '');
        putCachedRequest_(cacheKey, result);

        if (prevResult) {
          resultBackStack.push(prevResult);
        }

        renderResult(result);
        showSection('result');
      })
      .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
        setStatus('resultStatus', '');
        setStatus('searchStatus', err.message || String(err));
      })
      .mobileSearch(payload);
  });
}

function buildStudentInfoHtml(info) {
  if (!info) return '';

  const photoHtml = info.photoDataUrl
    ? '<img class="student-photo" src="' + info.photoDataUrl + '" alt="학생 사진">'
    : '<div class="student-photo-placeholder">사진 없음</div>';

  const extra = info.info || {};
  const addressText = cleanInfoValue(extra.address);
  const birthText = formatBirth6(extra.birth);
  const schoolText = buildMiddleSchoolText(extra.school);
  const parentPhone = buildParentPhoneText(extra.motherPhone, extra.fatherPhone);
  const programHtml = buildProgramHtml(extra.rural, extra.special);
  const majorText = buildMajorText(extra.major1, extra.major2);

  const titleText = buildStudentTitleWithBirth_(info.title || '', birthText);
  const studentPhoneText = cleanInfoValue(extra.studentPhone);
  const studentPhoneDigits = studentPhoneText.replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
  let titleHtml = escapeHtml(titleText);

  if (studentPhoneText && studentPhoneDigits) {
    titleHtml = titleHtml.replace(
      escapeHtml(studentPhoneText),
      '<a class="student-phone-link" href="tel:' + escapeHtml(studentPhoneDigits) + '" aria-label="' + escapeHtml(studentPhoneText + ' 전화 걸기') + '">' + escapeHtml(studentPhoneText) + '</a>'
    );
  }

  return '<div class="student-info-card">'
    + '<div class="student-detail-head">'
    + '<div class="student-detail-title">' + titleHtml + '</div>'
    + (addressText ? '<div class="student-detail-address">' + escapeHtml(addressText) + '</div>' : '')
    + '</div>'
    + '<div class="student-profile-wrap">'
    + '<div class="student-photo-wrap">' + photoHtml + '<button type="button" class="consult-open-btn" onclick="openCounseling(\'' + escapeJsAttr(info.studentNo || '') + '\')">상담 내용 보기</button></div>'
    + '<div class="student-side-info">'
    + buildSideLineHtml('출신중', schoolText)
    + buildSideLineHtml('보호자', parentPhone)
    + buildSideLineHtml('전형', programHtml || '-', true)
    + buildSideLineHtml('희망학과', escapeHtml(majorText || '-'), true)
    + '</div>'
    + '</div>'
    + buildGradeMatrixHtml(info.gradeMatrix || {}, info.naesin)
    + '</div>';
}



function openCounseling(studentNo) {
  counselFromCollegeApply = false;
  const no = String(studentNo || '').trim();
  if (!no) return;
  setStatus('counselStatus', '상담 내용을 불러오는 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      currentCounselData = data || { studentNo: no, records: [] };
      counselEditMode = false;
      renderCounseling(data);
      showSection('counsel');
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err));
    })
    .mobileGetCounseling(no);
}


function openCollegeApplyCounseling(studentNo) {
  const no = String(studentNo || '').trim();
  if (!no) return;
  counselFromCollegeApply = true;
  setStatus('counselStatus', '면접 상담 내용을 불러오는 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      currentCounselData = data || { studentNo: no, records: [] };
      counselEditMode = collegeApplyCanEdit === true;
      renderCounseling(data);
      showSection('counsel');
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
      alert(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err));
    })
    .mobileGetCounseling(no);
}

function renderCounseling(data) {
  currentCounselData = data || currentCounselData || { records: [] };
  const title = document.getElementById('counselStudentTitle');
  const list = document.getElementById('counselRecordList');
  const dateInput = document.getElementById('counselDateInput');
  const editBtn = document.getElementById('counselEditToggle');
  const inputCard = document.querySelector('.counsel-input-card');
  if (title) title.textContent = (currentCounselData.studentNo || '') + (currentCounselData.name ? ' ' + currentCounselData.name : '');
  if (dateInput) dateInput.value = currentCounselData.today || new Date().toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  if (editBtn) {
    editBtn.textContent = counselEditMode ? '수정 종료' : '기존 상담 수정';
    editBtn.style.display = (counselFromCollegeApply && !collegeApplyCanEdit) ? 'none' : '';
  }
  if (inputCard) inputCard.style.display = (counselFromCollegeApply && !collegeApplyCanEdit) ? 'none' : '';
  renderCounselInputs();

  const records = currentCounselData.records || [];
  if (!records.length) {
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-box">상담 기록이 없습니다.</div>';
    return;
  }
  list.innerHTML = records.map(function(rec) {
    const rowIndex = String(rec.rowIndex || '');
    if (counselEditMode) {
      return '<div class="counsel-record" data-row="' + escapeHtml(rowIndex) + '">'
        + '<div class="counsel-record-head">' + escapeHtml(rec.date || '') + ' / ' + escapeHtml(rec.category || '') + '</div>'
        + '<input type="date" class="counsel-date-input" id="counselEditDate_' + escapeHtml(rowIndex) + '" value="' + escapeHtml(rec.date || '') + '">'
        + '<textarea id="counselEditContent_' + escapeHtml(rowIndex) + '">' + escapeHtml(rec.content || '') + '</textarea>'
        + '<div class="counsel-record-actions">'
        + '<button type="button" class="counsel-small-btn" onclick="updateCounseling(\'' + escapeJsAttr(rowIndex) + '\', \'' + escapeJsAttr(rec.category || '') + '\')">저장</button>'
        + '<button type="button" class="counsel-small-btn counsel-delete-btn" onclick="deleteCounseling(\'' + escapeJsAttr(rowIndex) + '\')">삭제</button>'
        + '</div></div>';
    }
    return '<div class="counsel-record">'
      + '<div class="counsel-record-head">' + escapeHtml(rec.date || '') + ' / ' + escapeHtml(rec.category || '') + '</div>'
      + '<div class="counsel-record-body">' + escapeHtml(rec.content || '') + '</div>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function renderCounselInputs() {
  const area = document.getElementById('counselInputs');
  if (!area) return;
  const cats = counselFromCollegeApply ? ['면접'] : ['수시', '정시', '면접', '생활'];
  area.innerHTML = cats.map(function(cat) {
    return '<div class="counsel-input-row">'
      + '<div class="counsel-input-label">' + escapeHtml(cat) + '</div>'
      + '<textarea class="counsel-input-textarea" id="counselInput_' + escapeHtml(cat) + '" placeholder="' + escapeHtml(cat) + ' 상담 내용을 입력하세요."></textarea>'
      + '</div>';
  }).join('');
}

function toggleCounselEditMode() {
  counselEditMode = !counselEditMode;
  renderCounseling(currentCounselData);
}

function saveCounseling() {
  if (!currentCounselData || !currentCounselData.studentNo) return;
  const date = document.getElementById('counselDateInput').value;
  const cats = counselFromCollegeApply ? ['면접'] : ['수시', '정시', '면접', '생활'];
  const entries = cats.map(function(cat) {
    const el = document.getElementById('counselInput_' + cat);
    return { category: cat, content: el ? el.value.trim() : '' };
  }).filter(function(item) { return item.content; });
  setStatus('counselStatus', '저장 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      setStatus('counselStatus', '저장되었습니다.');
      currentCounselData = data;
      renderCounseling(data);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { setStatus('counselStatus', err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)); })
    .mobileSaveCounseling({ studentNo: currentCounselData.studentNo, date: date, entries: entries });
}

function updateCounseling(rowIndex, category) {
  if (!currentCounselData || !currentCounselData.studentNo) return;
  const dateEl = document.getElementById('counselEditDate_' + rowIndex);
  const contentEl = document.getElementById('counselEditContent_' + rowIndex);
  const date = dateEl ? dateEl.value : '';
  const content = contentEl ? contentEl.value.trim() : '';
  setStatus('counselStatus', '수정 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      setStatus('counselStatus', '수정되었습니다.');
      currentCounselData = data;
      renderCounseling(data);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { setStatus('counselStatus', err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)); })
    .mobileUpdateCounseling({ rowIndex: rowIndex, studentNo: currentCounselData.studentNo, date: date, category: category, content: content });
}

function deleteCounseling(rowIndex) {
  if (!currentCounselData || !currentCounselData.studentNo) return;
  if (!confirm('이 상담 기록을 삭제하시겠습니까?')) return;
  setStatus('counselStatus', '삭제 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
      setStatus('counselStatus', '삭제되었습니다.');
      currentCounselData = data;
      renderCounseling(data);
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { setStatus('counselStatus', err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)); })
    .mobileDeleteCounseling({ rowIndex: rowIndex, studentNo: currentCounselData.studentNo });
}

function openCollegePdf() {
  setStatus('collegePdfStatus', '대학 정보 파일를 불러오는 중입니다.');
  google.script.run
    .withSuccessHandler(function(info) {
      renderCollegePdf(info || {});
      showSection('collegePdf');
    })
    .withFailureHandler(function(err) { alert(err && err.message ? err.message : String(err)); })
    .mobileGetCollegePdfInfo();
}

function renderCollegePdf(info) {
  const infoEl = document.getElementById('collegePdfInfo');
  const viewer = document.getElementById('collegePdfViewer');
  setStatus('collegePdfStatus', '');

  const files = info && Array.isArray(info.files) && info.files.length
    ? info.files
    : (info && info.exists ? [info] : []);

  window.currentCollegePdfFiles = files;

  if (!files.length) {
    if (infoEl) infoEl.textContent = '';
    if (viewer) viewer.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-box">업로드된 대학 정보 파일이 없습니다.</div>';
    return;
  }

  if (infoEl) infoEl.textContent = '업로드된 대학 정보 파일 ' + files.length + '개';
  renderSelectedCollegePdf(0);
}

function renderSelectedCollegePdf(index) {
  const viewer = document.getElementById('collegePdfViewer');
  const files = window.currentCollegePdfFiles || [];
  const file = files[index] || files[0];
  if (!viewer || !file) return;

  const fileListHtml = files.length > 1
    ? '<div class="college-pdf-list">' + files.map(function(item, idx) {
        const activeClass = idx === index ? ' active' : '';
        const label = (item.fileName || '대학 정보 파일');
        return '<button type="button" class="college-pdf-item' + activeClass + '" onclick="renderSelectedCollegePdf(' + idx + ')">' + escapeHtml(label) + '</button>';
      }).join('') + '</div>'
    : '';

  const currentLabel = (file.fileName || '대학 정보 파일');
  const isImage = String(file.fileType || '').toUpperCase() === 'IMAGE';
  const previewHtml = isImage
    ? '<img class="college-image-preview" src="' + escapeHtml(file.previewUrl || '') + '" alt="' + escapeHtml(file.fileName || '대학 정보 이미지') + '" onerror="this.outerHTML=\'<div class=&quot;college-image-fallback&quot;>이미지 미리보기를 불러오지 못했습니다.<br>위의 [새 창으로 크게 보기]를 눌러 확인해 주세요.</div>\'">'
    : '<iframe class="pdf-frame" src="' + escapeHtml(file.previewUrl || '') + '"></iframe>';

  viewer.innerHTML = fileListHtml
    + '<div class="college-pdf-current">' + escapeHtml(currentLabel) + '</div>'
    + '<a class="pdf-open-btn" href="' + escapeHtml(file.openUrl || '#') + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">새 창으로 크게 보기</a>'
    + previewHtml;
}

function buildStudentTitleWithBirth_(title, birthText) {
  const base = cleanInfoValue(title);
  const birth = cleanInfoValue(birthText);

  if (!birth) return base;
  if (!base) return birth;
  if (base.includes(birth)) return base;

  return base + ' / ' + birth;
}

function buildSideLineHtml(label, value, rawHtml) {
  const text = cleanInfoValue(value) || '-';
  return '<div class="student-side-line">'
    + '<span class="student-field-label">' + escapeHtml(label) + '</span>'
    + '<span class="student-field-value">' + (rawHtml ? text : escapeHtml(text)) + '</span>'
    + '</div>';
}

function buildWideLineHtml(label, valueHtml, rawHtml) {
  const content = valueHtml || '-';
  return '<div class="student-wide-line">'
    + '<span class="student-field-label">' + escapeHtml(label) + '</span>'
    + '<span class="student-field-value">' + (rawHtml ? content : escapeHtml(content)) + '</span>'
    + '</div>';
}

function formatBirth6(value) {
  const text = cleanInfoValue(value).replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
  if (!text) return '';
  if (text.length >= 6) return text.slice(-6);
  return text.padStart(6, '0');
}

function buildMiddleSchoolText(value) {
  const text = cleanInfoValue(value);
  if (!text) return '';
  return text.includes('졸업') ? text : text + ' 졸업';
}

function buildParentPhoneText(motherPhone, fatherPhone) {
  const mother = cleanInfoValue(motherPhone);
  const father = cleanInfoValue(fatherPhone);
  if (mother) return '모 ' + mother;
  if (father) return '부 ' + father;
  return '';
}

function buildProgramHtml(rural, special) {
  const ruralValue = cleanInfoValue(rural);
  const specialValue = cleanInfoValue(special);
  const parts = [];

  if (ruralValue) {
    parts.push('<span class="student-blue">' + escapeHtml(ruralValue) + '</span>');
  }
  if (specialValue && specialValue !== ruralValue) {
    parts.push(escapeHtml(specialValue));
  }

  return parts.join(', ');
}

function buildMajorText(major1, major2) {
  const raw = [cleanInfoValue(major1), cleanInfoValue(major2)].filter(Boolean);
  if (!raw.length) return '';

  const hasReal = raw.some(function(v) { return v !== '미정'; });
  const filtered = raw.filter(function(v) {
    return hasReal ? v !== '미정' : true;
  });

  const unique = [];
  filtered.forEach(function(v) {
    if (!unique.includes(v)) unique.push(v);
  });

  return unique.join(', ');
}

function cleanInfoValue(value) {
  const text = String(value == null ? '' : value).trim();
  if (!text || text === '-') return '';
  return text;
}

function buildGradeMatrixHtml(matrix, fallbackNaesin) {
  const overall = cleanInfoValue(matrix.overall) || cleanInfoValue(fallbackNaesin);

  return '<div class="grade-matrix-wrap">'
    + '<table class="grade-matrix">'
    + '<thead><tr>'
    + '<th class="grade-overall-cell">' + escapeHtml(overall) + '</th>'
    + '<th>1학기</th>'
    + '<th>2학기</th>'
    + '<th>전학기</th>'
    + '</tr></thead>'
    + '<tbody>'
    + buildGradeRowHtml('1학년', matrix.g1s1, matrix.g1s2, matrix.g1all)
    + buildGradeRowHtml('2학년', matrix.g2s1, matrix.g2s2, matrix.g2all)
    + buildGradeRowHtml('3학년', matrix.g3s1, matrix.g3s2, matrix.g3all)
    + '</tbody></table></div>';
}

function buildGradeRowHtml(label, v1, v2, v3) {
  return '<tr>'
    + '<th>' + escapeHtml(label) + '</th>'
    + '<td>' + escapeHtml(cleanInfoValue(v1)) + '</td>'
    + '<td>' + escapeHtml(cleanInfoValue(v2)) + '</td>'
    + '<td>' + escapeHtml(cleanInfoValue(v3)) + '</td>'
    + '</tr>';
}

function escapeHtml(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value)
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/'/g, '&#39;');
}

function escapeJsAttr(value) {
  return String(value == null ? '' : value)
    .replace(/\\/g, '\\\\')
    .replace(/'/g, "\\'")
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;');
}

      function drawChartsWhenReady(charts) {
        if (!charts || !charts.length) return;
        if (!window.google || !google.charts) return;

        if (chartsLoaded) {
          drawCharts(charts);
          return;
        }

        google.charts.load('current', { packages: ['corechart'] });
        google.charts.setOnLoadCallback(function() {
          chartsLoaded = true;
          drawCharts(charts);
        });
      }

      function drawCharts(charts) {
        charts.forEach(function(chart, index) {
          const data = new google.visualization.DataTable();
          data.addColumn('number', 'Index');
          data.addColumn('number', '등급');
          // ★ 차트 점(Point)의 색상 스타일 지정
          data.addColumn({type: 'string', role: 'style'});

          const fixedMonths = [3, 5, 6, 7, 9, 10, 11];
          const chartXPositions = [1.5, 2.5, 3.5, 4.5, 5.5, 6.5, 7.5];

          fixedMonths.forEach(function(m, i) {
            const point = (chart.points || []).find(p => Number(p.month) === m);
            let gradeVal = null; 
            let pointStyle = null; 
            
            if (point) {
              gradeVal = Number(point.grade);
              
              // ★ 1, 2등급일 경우 빨간색 점(#EF4444), 나머지는 기본 파란색 점(#3B82F6) 적용
              if (gradeVal === 1 || gradeVal === 2) {
                pointStyle = 'point { fill-color: #EF4444; }';
              } else {
                pointStyle = 'point { fill-color: #3B82F6; }';
              }

              if (gradeVal > 7) gradeVal = 7; 
            }
            
            data.addRow([chartXPositions[i], gradeVal, pointStyle]); 
          });

          const options = {
            legend: { position: 'none' },
            backgroundColor: 'transparent',
            chartArea: { left: 48, right: 16, top: 22, bottom: 38, width: '84%', height: '74%' },
            hAxis: { 
              ticks: [
                {v: 1.5, f: '3월'}, 
                {v: 2.5, f: '5월'}, 
                {v: 3.5, f: '6월'}, 
                {v: 4.5, f: '7월'}, 
                {v: 5.5, f: '9월'}, 
                {v: 6.5, f: '10월'}, 
                {v: 7.5, f: '수능'}
              ],
              viewWindow: { min: 1, max: 8 },
              textStyle: { fontSize: 12, color: '#64748B', bold: true }, 
              gridlines: { color: '#CBD5E1' } 
            },
            vAxis: {
              direction: -1,
              viewWindow: { min: 0.5, max: 7.5 }, 
              ticks: [
                {v: 1, f: '1'}, {v: 2, f: '2'}, {v: 3, f: '3'}, 
                {v: 4, f: '4'}, {v: 5, f: '5'}, {v: 6, f: '6'}, 
                {v: 7, f: '7~9'} 
              ],
              textStyle: { fontSize: 12, color: '#64748B', bold: true }, 
              gridlines: { color: '#E2E8F0' }
            },
            width: '100%',
            height: 300, 
            pointSize: 10, 
            lineWidth: 3,  
            colors: ['#000000'], // ★ 선 색상만 굵은 검은색으로 고정
            interpolateNulls: true, 
            animation:{
              startup: true,
              duration: 1000,
              easing: 'out',
            }
          };

          const target = document.getElementById('chart_' + index);
          const chartObj = new google.visualization.LineChart(target);
          chartObj.draw(data, options);
        });
      }
    

      function openCollegeApplyMode() {
        if (!isLoggedIn) {
          setStatus('loginStatus', '수시 지원 현황은 비밀번호 입력 후 이용할 수 있습니다.');
          showSection('login');
          return;
        }
        currentMode = 'collegeApply';
        showSection('collegeApply');
        loadCollegeApplyInitData_();
      }

      function loadCollegeApplyInitData_() {
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(data) {
            const regionSelect = document.getElementById('collegeApplyRegion');
            if (regionSelect) {
              regionSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="ALL">전체</option>';
              (data.regions || []).forEach(function(region) {
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = region;
                opt.textContent = region;
                regionSelect.appendChild(opt);
              });
            }

            renderCollegeApplyUniversityDropdown_(data.universities || []);
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', err.message || String(err));
          })
          .mobileGetCollegeApplyInitData();
      }

      function renderCollegeApplyUniversityDropdown_(universities) {
        const panel = document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityPanel');
        if (!panel) return;
        panel.innerHTML = '';
        (universities || []).forEach(function(item, index) {
          const id = 'collegeApplyUniv_' + index;
          const label = document.createElement('label');
          label.className = 'college-apply-univ-option-row';
          label.innerHTML = '<input type="checkbox" class="college-apply-univ-check" value="' + escapeAttr_(item.raw) + '" onchange="updateCollegeApplyUniversityToggleText()"><span>' + escapeHtml_(item.raw) + '</span>';
          panel.appendChild(label);
        });
        updateCollegeApplyUniversityToggleText();
      }

      function toggleCollegeApplyUniversityDropdown(event) {
        if (event) event.stopPropagation();
        const panel = document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityPanel');
        if (!panel) return;
        panel.classList.toggle('open');
      }

      document.addEventListener('click', function(event) {
        const panel = document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityPanel');
        const wrap = document.querySelector('.college-apply-univ-wrap');
        if (!panel || !wrap) return;
        if (!wrap.contains(event.target)) panel.classList.remove('open');
      });

      function updateCollegeApplyUniversityToggleText() {
        const btn = document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityToggle');
        if (!btn) return;
        const selected = getSelectedCollegeApplyUniversities_();
        if (!selected.length) {
          btn.textContent = '전체';
        } else if (selected.length === 1) {
          btn.textContent = selected[0];
        } else {
          btn.textContent = selected.length + '개 대학 선택';
        }
      }

      function getSelectedCollegeApplyUniversities_() {
        return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.college-apply-univ-check:checked')).map(function(input) { return input.value; }).filter(Boolean);
      }

      function collectCollegeApplyPayload_() {
        const selectedUniversities = getSelectedCollegeApplyUniversities_();
        collegeApplySelectedUniversities = selectedUniversities.slice();
        return {
          studentNo: document.getElementById('collegeApplyStudentNo').value.trim(),
          name: document.getElementById('collegeApplyName').value.trim(),
          region: document.getElementById('collegeApplyRegion').value,
          universityQuery: '',
          selectedUniversities: selectedUniversities,
          admissionType: document.getElementById('collegeApplyType').value,
          detailType: document.getElementById('collegeApplyDetail').value.trim(),
          major: document.getElementById('collegeApplyMajor').value.trim(),
          sortMode: collegeApplySortMode,
          topInterview: false,
          canEdit: collegeApplyCanEdit,
          singleField: ''
        };
      }

      function prepareCollegeApplySearch() {
        const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        pendingCollegeApplyPayload = payload;
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function searchCollegeApplySingle(field) {
        const full = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        const payload = {
          studentNo: '',
          name: '',
          region: 'ALL',
          universityQuery: '',
          selectedUniversities: [],
          admissionType: '전체',
          detailType: '',
          major: '',
          sortMode: collegeApplySortMode,
          topInterview: false,
          canEdit: collegeApplyCanEdit,
          singleField: field
        };
        if (field === 'studentNo') payload.studentNo = full.studentNo;
        if (field === 'name') payload.name = full.name;
        if (field === 'region') payload.region = full.region;
        if (field === 'university') payload.selectedUniversities = full.selectedUniversities || [];
        if (field === 'admissionType') payload.admissionType = full.admissionType;
        if (field === 'detailType') payload.detailType = full.detailType;
        if (field === 'major') payload.major = full.major;
        pendingCollegeApplyPayload = payload;
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function renderCollegeApplyUniversityChoices_(groups) {
        const list = document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityList');
        list.innerHTML = '';
        const selected = [];
        groups.forEach(function(group) {
          const title = document.createElement('div');
          title.style.cssText = 'padding:18px 8px;font-size:1.8rem;font-weight:1000;color:var(--text-main);text-align:center;';
          title.textContent = '[' + group.term + '] 검색 결과';
          list.appendChild(title);

          if (!group.options || group.options.length === 0) {
            const empty = document.createElement('div');
            empty.className = 'empty-box';
            empty.textContent = '일치 대학 없음';
            list.appendChild(empty);
            return;
          }

          group.options.forEach(function(opt) {
            const btn = document.createElement('button');
            btn.type = 'button';
            btn.className = 'college-apply-univ-option';
            btn.textContent = opt.display;
            btn.onclick = function() {
              if (!selected.includes(opt.raw)) selected.push(opt.raw);
              btn.style.background = 'var(--primary-soft)';
              btn.style.borderColor = 'var(--primary)';
              btn.style.color = 'var(--primary)';
            };
            list.appendChild(btn);
          });
        });

        const applyBtn = document.createElement('button');
        applyBtn.className = 'btn-main';
        applyBtn.style.margin = '18px 0 0';
        applyBtn.textContent = '선택 대학으로 조회';
        applyBtn.onclick = function() {
          collegeApplySelectedUniversities = selected.slice();
          closeCollegeApplyUniversityModal();
          const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
          payload.selectedUniversities = collegeApplySelectedUniversities.slice();
          runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
        };
        list.appendChild(applyBtn);

        document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityModal').classList.remove('hidden');
      }

      function closeCollegeApplyUniversityModal() {
        document.getElementById('collegeApplyUniversityModal').classList.add('hidden');
      }

      function runCollegeApplySearch_(payload) {
        setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', '조회 중입니다...');
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', '');
            renderCollegeApplyResult_(result || { rows: [], headers: [] });
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', err.message || String(err));
          })
          .mobileSearchCollegeApply(payload);
      }

      function refreshCollegeApplySearch() {
        const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function setCollegeApplySort(mode, btn) {
        collegeApplySortMode = mode;
        document.querySelectorAll('.college-apply-sort-btn, .college-apply-special-btn').forEach(function(item) {
          item.classList.remove('active');
        });
        if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
        refreshCollegeApplySearch();
      }

      function clearCollegeApplySpecialActive_() {
        document.querySelectorAll('.college-apply-sort-btn, .college-apply-special-btn').forEach(function(item) {
          item.classList.remove('active');
        });
      }

      function searchTopInterviewCollegeApply(btn) {
        clearCollegeApplySpecialActive_();
        if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
        const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        payload.topInterview = true;
        payload.sortMode = '';
        collegeApplySortMode = '';
        pendingCollegeApplyPayload = payload;
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function searchTopNaesinCollegeApply(btn) {
        clearCollegeApplySpecialActive_();
        if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
        const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        payload.topNaesin = true;
        payload.sortMode = '';
        collegeApplySortMode = '';
        pendingCollegeApplyPayload = payload;
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function searchMedicalCollegeApply(btn) {
        clearCollegeApplySpecialActive_();
        if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
        const payload = collectCollegeApplyPayload_();
        payload.medical = true;
        payload.sortMode = '';
        collegeApplySortMode = '';
        pendingCollegeApplyPayload = payload;
        runCollegeApplySearch_(payload);
      }

      function showCollegeApplyUniversityStats(btn) {
        clearCollegeApplySpecialActive_();
        if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
        setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', '대학별 지원 현황을 불러오는 중입니다...');
        document.getElementById('collegeApplyCount').textContent = '대학별 지원 현황';
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(result) {
            setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', '');
            renderCollegeApplyUniversityStats_(result || { universities: [] });
          })
          .withFailureHandler(function(err) {
            setStatus('collegeApplyStatus', err.message || String(err));
          })
          .mobileGetCollegeApplyUniversityStats();
      }

      function renderCollegeApplyUniversityStats_(result) {
        const list = result.universities || [];
        const target = document.getElementById('collegeApplyResultTable');
        if (!list.length) {
          target.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-box">대학별 지원 현황이 없습니다.</div>';
          return;
        }
        const total = list.reduce(function(sum, item) { return sum + Number(item.count || 0); }, 0);
        document.getElementById('collegeApplyCount').textContent = '대학별 지원 현황 ' + total + '건';
        let html = '<div class="college-apply-univ-summary">';
        list.forEach(function(item, idx) {
          const detailId = 'collegeApplyUnivDetail_' + idx;
          html += '<div class="college-apply-univ-card">'
            + '<button type="button" class="college-apply-univ-head" data-detail-id="' + detailId + '" onclick="toggleCollegeApplyUniversityDetail(this.getAttribute(\'data-detail-id\'))">'
            + '<span>' + escapeHtml_(item.label || '') + '</span><span>' + escapeHtml_(item.count || 0) + '건</span></button>'
            + '<div class="college-apply-univ-detail" id="' + detailId + '">';
          if (!item.rows || !item.rows.length) {
            html += '<div class="empty-box">해당 지원 내역이 없습니다.</div>';
          } else {
            html += '<div class="table-responsive-wrap"><table class="college-apply-univ-inner-table"><thead><tr>'
              + '<th>학번</th><th>이름</th><th>내신</th><th>전형명</th><th>모집단위</th><th>1단계</th><th>면접</th><th>최종</th><th>최저</th><th>1차</th><th>2차</th><th>예비</th>'
              + '</tr></thead><tbody>';
            item.rows.forEach(function(row) {
              html += '<tr>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.studentNo || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.name || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.naesin || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.detailType || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.major || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.step1Date || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.interviewDate || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.finalDate || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + (row.minimumMark ? 'O' : '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.result1 || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.result2 || '') + '</td>'
                + '<td>' + escapeHtml_(row.reserve || '') + '</td>'
                + '</tr>';
            });
            html += '</tbody></table></div>';
          }
          html += '</div></div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
        target.innerHTML = html;
      }

      function toggleCollegeApplyUniversityDetail(id) {
        const el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el) el.classList.toggle('open');
      }

      function renderCollegeApplyResult_(result) {
        const rows = result.rows || [];
        const displayInfo = getCollegeApplyDisplayInfo_(rows);
        document.getElementById('collegeApplyCount').innerHTML = '검색 결과 ' + (result.count || rows.length) + '건' + (displayInfo.labelHtml ? ' <span class="college-apply-count-detail">' + displayInfo.labelHtml + '</span>' : '');
        const target = document.getElementById('collegeApplyResultTable');
        if (!rows.length) {
          target.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-box">검색 결과가 없습니다.</div>';
          return;
        }

        const columns = buildCollegeApplyColumns_(displayInfo.omit);
        let html = '<table class="college-apply-table">' + buildCollegeApplyColGroup_(columns) + '<thead><tr>' +
          columns.map(function(col){ return '<th class="college-apply-head-' + escapeAttr_(col.key) + '">' + escapeHtml_(col.header) + '</th>'; }).join('') +
          '</tr></thead><tbody>';

        rows.forEach(function(row) {
          html += '<tr>';
          columns.forEach(function(col) {
            html += '<td class="' + getCollegeApplyTdClass_(row, col.key) + '">' + renderCollegeApplyColumnCell_(row, col.key) + '</td>';
          });
          html += '</tr>';
        });
        html += '</tbody></table>';
        target.innerHTML = html;
        window.__collegeApplyRows = rows;
      }

      function getCollegeApplyDisplayInfo_(rows) {
        const payload = pendingCollegeApplyPayload || {};
        const field = payload.singleField || '';
        const omit = {};
        let label = '';
        if (field === 'studentNo') {
          const q = String(payload.studentNo || '').trim();
          const classMatch = q.match(/^(\d{1,2})\s*반$/);
          if (classMatch) {
            label = escapeHtml_(q);
            omit.studentNo = true;
          } else if (rows.length) {
            const first = rows[0];
            label = escapeHtml_((first.studentNo || '') + ' ' + (first.name || '') + (first.naesin ? ' 내신 ' + first.naesin : ''));
            omit.studentNo = true; omit.name = true; omit.naesin = true;
          } else {
            label = escapeHtml_(q);
          }
        } else if (field === 'name') {
          if (rows.length) {
            const first = rows[0];
            label = '<button type="button" class="college-apply-clickable" onclick="openCollegeApplyCounseling(\'' + escapeJsAttr(first.studentNo || '') + '\')">' + escapeHtml_((first.studentNo || '') + ' ' + (first.name || '') + (first.naesin ? ' 내신 ' + first.naesin : '')) + '</button>';
            omit.studentNo = true; omit.name = true; omit.naesin = true;
          } else {
            label = escapeHtml_(payload.name || '');
          }
        } else if (field === 'region') {
          label = escapeHtml_(payload.region && payload.region !== 'ALL' ? payload.region : '전체');
          if (payload.region && payload.region !== 'ALL') omit.region = true;
        } else if (field === 'university') {
          const selected = payload.selectedUniversities || [];
          label = escapeHtml_(selected.length ? selected.join(', ') : '전체');
          if (selected.length) omit.university = true;
        } else if (field === 'admissionType') {
          label = escapeHtml_(payload.admissionType && payload.admissionType !== '전체' ? payload.admissionType : '전체');
          if (payload.admissionType && payload.admissionType !== '전체') omit.admissionType = true;
        } else if (field === 'detailType') {
          label = escapeHtml_(payload.detailType || '');
          if (payload.detailType) omit.detailType = true;
        } else if (field === 'major') {
          label = escapeHtml_(payload.major || '');
          if (payload.major) omit.major = true;
        } else if (payload.topInterview) {
          label = escapeHtml_('상위권 면접');
        } else if (payload.topNaesin) {
          label = escapeHtml_('내신 3.5 이하');
        } else if (payload.medical) {
          label = escapeHtml_('의치약한수');
        }
        return { labelHtml: label, omit: omit };
      }

      function buildCollegeApplyColumns_(omit) {
        const all = [
          { key:'studentNo', header:'학번' },
          { key:'name', header:'이름' },
          { key:'naesin', header:'내신' },
          { key:'region', header:'지역' },
          { key:'university', header:'대학명' },
